bsten dka' ba zhig 'dug pas chos 'brel ma zhus gsungs pa yang snang bas thugs bze reg yod par snang /'u yug pas sa skyar 'jam dbyangs sa skya pan chen la rnam 'grel gsan/ sa
skyar bshad pa mdzad/ slob ma zhang mdo sde dpal sogs te/ rnam 'grel dar ba 'di 'jam mgon sa skya pa dpon slob kyi drin yin/bo dong rin chen rtses gram ram du bshad pa
btsugs/ slob ma bu ston grags seng dang / dbu ma pa shes rab 'bum sogs so/'jam gsar gyis rkyang dar du bshad pa btsugs/ slob ma kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer dang rong pa sga
lo sogs so/skyel nag grags seng la mchims chen mos zhal ta mdzad nas snar thang du bshad pa btsugs/ slob ma skyi ston grags 'bum dang chu mig pa seng ge dpal la sogs pa'o/bcom
ldan rig pa'i ral gri yang / yul phu thang pa yin la/ phyis snar thang du byon/ snar thang gi them pa la zhabs bzhag pa/ dbu la nyi ma shar ba/ snar thang gi tshogs
dung bus pa gsum 'dzom pas rten 'brel gyi gnad zab mo 'grig/ mdze'i rnam rtog cung zad yod kyang / tshad ma rnam nges stong tshar gcig shar bas yul bud/ bka' bstan bcos
kyi sgyur byang dang bam tshad sogs la nges nges mdzad de so sor 'debs/ deng sang bka' 'gyur bstan 'gyur zhes grags pa yang / thog mar khong gis phyogs su phyogs su sdebs/
bstan pa rgyan gyi me tog sogs bstan bcos po ti bcu drug tsam brtsams/

slob ma'i mchog/ dbus pa blo gsal byang chub ye shes dang / btsun pa 'jam sgeg gam 'jam nyeg sogs mang du byon/phyis btsun pa 'jam dbyangs kyis rgya nag nas mthun rkyen sbyar/
dbus pa blo gsal/ lo tsA ba bsod nams 'od zer/ rgya ro byang chub 'bum gsum gyis bka' 'gyur bstan 'gyur gyi glegs bam bzhengs nas/ 'jam lha khang gi gtsug lag khang du
bzhugs su gsol ba las mang du mched/ phyis bu ston gyis go rim bsgrigs shing dag ma dag gi rab dbyes gtan la phab bo/rngog lo'i bu chen gro lung pa blo gros 'byung gnas
kyis lo tsA ba'i gsung la gces spras cher mdzad/ de nyid la cha pa chen pos gtugs/ gro lung pa slob brgyud las 'phel ba dang / 'bre ar gyi lugs tha dad pa yin zer te/ rgyu
mtshan 'bre ar gyi phar phyin gyi bshad pa ni/ bstan pa snga dar gyi bshad rgyun khams su 'phos pa las byung ba yin la/ gro lung sogs ni/ rngog los phyis kha che nas bslabs
pa'i bshad rgyun la gtsor mdzad zer bar snang ngo/cha pa chen po pan shaka pas/ cha pa chen po lo chen gshegs pa'i sa mo glang la 'khrungs nas lo re gcig pa sa mo glang
la gshegs zhes bshad 'dug lo chen gyi dngos slob gangs pa she'u blo gros byang chub dang / khyung rin chen grags gnyis kyi slob ma stod lung rgya dmar byang chub grags
la tshad ma gtso bor sbyangs/ rig pa'i sgo bye ste/ cha bsdus yid kyi mun sel la sogs pa'i rang shar gyi rtsom pa mang du mdzad/ ne'u thog dm: sne'u thoggi gdan sar phebs
te 'chad pa'i rgyun bsrings/slob ma'i mchog kyang / seng chen brgyad/ jo sras bzhi/ seng 'dra

brgyad ces sogs yod pa las/ gtsang nag pa brtson 'grus seng ge/ dan 'bag pa smra ba'i seng ge/ bru?gru sha bsod nams seng ge/ rma bya rtsod pa'i seng ge/ rtsegs pa dbang phyug
seng ge/ myang phran pa chos kyi seng ge/ ldan ma dkon mchog seng ge/ gnyal pa yon tan seng ge lte seng ge chen po brgyad/ kha cig gtsang pa 'jam seng 'dren zer/'khon
jo sras rtse mo/ rngog jo sras ra mo/ khu jo sras ne tso?rtso/ gnyos jo sras dpal te jo sras bzhi'o/'gar dbang grub/ rkong pa 'jag chung / lho pa sgog zan/ spar phu ba bzhi
la shes can bzhi zer/ de ltar cha pa'i seng chen brgyad dang / gnyal zhig bu dgu sogs kyis gtso bor mdo phyogs kyi bstan pa la phan pa che bar mdzad 'dug go/de dag gis
ni bstan pa phyi dar sum stong brgya dang gsum lon pa la lo chen rin bzang byon pa nas/ sum stong brgya pa'i skabs cung zad bshad zin nas/ gnyis pa sum stong nyis brgya
pa'i skabs su byon pa'i mkhas grub dam pa ni/ dpal sa skya pa chen po yab sras rnams dang / dwags po bka' brgyud yab sras rnams dang / bka' gdams sku mched gsum gyi thugs
sras rnams te/ de yang sum stong nyis brgya dang nyer bzhi 'das pa'i nyer lnga pa chu pho sprel spyi lo 1092lo dpal sa skya pa chen po bltams lo 'di/ phyi dar sa mo bya
nas brgya dang zhe bzhi pa yin la/ jo bo byon pa'i shing rta nas so dgu pa yin zhing / rngog lo byon pa'i me bya nas so drug pa yin pas/ 'di'i bcu drug pa me mo phag la
rngog lo bstan pa'i nyi ma sku

gshegs/ rngog los bcu gcig lon pa me mo lug la lo chen rin bzang mkha' spyod la bzhud/ sa chen rang gi bcu gcig pa la yab sku gshegs/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags kyi bka'
drin chen pos bskyangs te/ gzim khang rnying mar 'jam dbyangs bsgrubs pas/ phyi'i bar chad sel te sgrol ma'i zhal gzigs/ nang gi bar chad sel te mi g.yo ba'i zhal gzigs
te zla ba drug nas/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi zhal gzigs te/ zhen pa bzhi bral la sogs pa'i phar phyin gyi gdams pa zab mo'i bka' drin stsal/ bcu gnyis pa la rong ngur smrig
tu brang ti dar ma snying po la mngon pa gsan pa brang ti de ni khu ston gyi slob ma rwa khri bzang 'bar gyi slob ma ste/ rngog lo chen panDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa la
mjal ba'i 'khor dge slong sum brgya dang bcas te phebs pa na/ lo tsA ba'i 'khor dge slong re re la khong rang gi slob bu dge slong bcu gsum bcu gsum bsnyen bkur byed du btsud/
de nas lo tsA ba'i dngos slob khyung rin chen grags dang / mes lhang tsher ma la dbu tshad/ kha'u pa dar ma rgyal mtshan sku mched la gsang 'dus dang mgon po zhal gyi
chos skor/ sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar la kyai rdor/ gung thang mal lo la bde mchog dang mgon po'i man ngag gsan/ pu rangs lo chung la bde mchog sogs gsan te/ rang lo nyi
shu rtsa dgu pa lcags pho byi lo gung thang nas 'cham mgon sa skyar phyag phebs/'cham mgon 'di ni/ mtho btsun grub rjes/ ma hA bo dhi'i sku bzhengs pa'i dus bzhengs pa
yin/ de'i tshe bla ma zhang ston dgung lo re brgyad bzhes pa'i tshe/ bya lo de nas lo ngo bzhi'i bar zhang ston la gsung ngag

zab mo'i bka' drin nod de/ rang lo so gnyis pa chu mo yos bu'i lo sgrub pa'i lung sbyin/ ngo mtshar ba'i rdzu 'phrul gyi ltad mo bstan/ rang lo zhe bdun pa sa pho rta'i lo/
rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug grub chen bi ru pa gtso 'khor lnga/ chos sgo skyel du byon te/ spyir rgyud sde bdun bcu rtsa gnyis kyi man ngag/ khyad par lcags ri mi 'da' ba'i
zab chos bzhi la sogs te/ mdor na gsung ngag nye brgyud kyi gnad zab mo'i bdud rtsi ngom par gsol/ rang lo lnga bcu pa lcags mo bya'i lo zhang gi gdams pa'i lo bco brgyad
bka' rgya yang grol te/ mdo khams kyi khams pa a seng gis zhus pa'i ngor gsung ngag thog mar bka' stsal/ gzhung bshad a seng mar grags pa yi ger bkod/ rgyud man ngag
zab mo'i bdud rtsi spel/ sku'i bkod pa mi 'dra ba drug bstan/ slar re bdun pa sa pho stag la dbyug pa zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi la sku 'bum rnam rgyal du grags par chos dbyings
su gshegs/ bde ba can/ po ta la/ u rgyan/ byang gser mdog can bzhi na sku'i bkod pa bzhis skal ldan gyi don mdzad cing da lta yang bzhugs skad/phag mo gru pa'i rnam
thar na bde ba can/ byang a yu ta ra/ gser mdog can gsum na sku'i bkod pa gsum bstan te bzhugs/ 'di rang ngo mtshar che gsung skad do/slob ma'i mchog ni/ sing ga gling gi
rnal 'byor pa/ byang chub sems dpa' stag/ sgom pa skyi 'bar te mchog thob gsum/rje btsun chen po/ zhus (zhu) byas dngos grub/ dga' ston rdo rje grags/ sgom pa 'od zer grags/
nags sgom pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/

'tshar (tshar) kha'i rnal 'byor pa/ mang chung ma ste bzod thob bdun/gzhan rtogs pa dang ldan pa brgyad cu byon no/ 'o na rje btsun rtse mo mi 'dren pa ji ltar zhe na/ de ni
bla ma chen po dang ngo bo gcig pas so sor ma phye zhes mkhas pa dag tsungs so/gzhan yang gzhung bshad gces par 'dzin pa'i thugs sras bcu gcig/ tshig rkang rnam par 'grel
ba'i thugs sras bdun/ phyogs kyi mkhas grub chen po bzhi zhes bya ste/ zhu byas kyis bsdebs pa'i bstod pa las/ zab don yongs su rdzogs pa'i slob ma ni/ pho brgyad mo gsum
dag la yi ger gdams/ zhes pa ltar/ khams pa a seng / lho pa zhu byas/ klog skya jo sras chos grags/ thugs sras snyan (gnyan) phul chung ba gtsug tor rgyal po'am mtshan
dngos bsod nams rdo rje/ spyan ras gzigs kyi rnam 'phrul byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ zangs ri phug pa/ khams sga theng gnyag bzhi/ rwa ba dbang phyug rgyal mtshan te
pho brgyad/sras kun dga' 'bar gyi yum jo lcam phur mo/ g.ya' lung gi jo mo ba'u ('a 'u) ma/ mang mkhar gyi jo mo mang chung ma ste mo gsum/rnam 'grel bcu gcig ces grags
pa ni/ gang zag 'di bcu gcig la gdams pa yin gyi/ gzhan du yid g.yo bar ma byed cig/gnyis pa ni gzhung bshad mdzad pa'i dngos slob/ na ro bandhe/ stod sgom byang chub shes
rab/ me nyag pradznya dzwa la/ zhu brag dmar ba/ hang ze dmar ba/ 'u yug gi g.yar sbu ba ma/ phag mo gru pa'o/phyogs kyi mkhas grub bzhi ni/ las stod pa dkon mchog mkhar/

khams pa rgwa?sga lo/ ne tshe sbal ston/ gshen rdo rje bzang po'o/mdor na/ spyir mdo rgyud kyi snying po dang / sgos bla chen 'brog mi'i rgyud man ngag gi bcud kyi snying po
'dzin pa ni/ dpal sa skya pa chen po 'di kho na ste/ ji skad du/ ma dros ye shes zhabs las rgyun bzhi'i bla ma ni// rgyal po rigs dang snying po snang ba'i mtha' can ste//
rig dang snying po zhabs las 'bar ba 'bar ba'i mtha'// rgyun bzhi 'dzin pa'i bla chen de la bdag phyag 'tshal//zhes pa ltar 'brog mi lo tsA ba ma dros pa'i mtsho chen
po las/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ se ston kun rig/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'phyin lo tsA ba 'od kyi snang ba ste gangga la sogs pa'i chu bo chen po bzhi dang
'dra ba'i rgyud man ngag gi rgyun babs/ bla chen sa skya pa chen po'i thugs kyi snod du nye bar gzung ba yin te/ de yang rgyun thog mtha' gnyis ni/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal
pos/ 'brog mi dang 'phyin gnyis char la dngos su gsan zhing / de la bla chen sa skya pas dngos su gsan pas grub/rgyun bar pa gnyis ni/ se las zhang ston chos 'bar dang /
mnga' ris pa las sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar gyis gsan la/ de gnyis la sa chen gyis dngos su gsan pas grub pa yin no/de ltar na yang spyir gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi bka' srol
bco brgyad ces grags te/ bla chen 'brog mi dang gyi jo las brgyud pa'i lam 'bras gnyis lab kyi jo lugs dang gcig/ dang po las 'phel ba la/ bla chen 'brog mi'i sku'i sras
indra dang / rdo rje las brgyud pa'i lam 'bras/ thugs kyi

sras 'brom de'i lam 'bras gnyis te gsum/se mkhar chung pa nas 'phel ba rab 'bring gsum yod pa'o/ 'bring du thob pa zha ma nas 'phel ba la/ pho brgyud mo brgyud bsres brgyud
gsum/ pho brgyud la yang rje khum bu ba chos rgyal nas se sgom grags rgyal/ rje mal gro sogs las 'phel ba'i slob brgyud dang / sras zha ma tsandi nas spangs rje nyi ma grags
las 'phel ba'i bsres brgyud de gnyis mo rgyud la yang / zha ma'i slob ma nyang sgom las/ smon dkar ba/ stod g.yung / dbon po sher tshul gsum nas 'phel ba'i lugs gsum
ste pho mo'i lugs lnga dang brgyad/bsres brgyud la/ zha ma pho mo bsres pa dum bu ko brag pa'i lugs/ zha ma pho mo gnyis sa lugs dang gsum bsres pa cha gan gyi lugs/ 'brog
mi lugs dang gyi jo lugs bsres pa/ jo nang kun spangs kyi lugs/ lam 'bras sbyor drug rdzogs chen gsum bsres pa la/ la stod dbang rgyal gyi lugs te bsres brgyud bzhi dang
bcu gnyis/rab tu thob pa zhang gi brgyud 'dzin sa lugs la snga bu dang phyi bu gnyis/ snga bu la phag gru lugs dang / gces sgom lugs gnyis/ phyi bu la nye brgyud dang
ring brgyud gnyis te sa lugs bzhi dang bcu drug/'brog jo sras gnyis dang zhang ston mched gnyis te bzhi'i gsung ngag gi gces mdzod bsdus pa mang lam zhig po'i lugs dang bcu
bdun/ se thon las mtha' mar thob pa byang chub ye shes kyis zhing phug pa la gdams pa'i lugs dang bco brgyad do/ de dag re re la ji ltar 'phel tshul mang bas ma bris so/

sum stong nyis brgya dang don bzhi 'das pa'i don lnga pa chu phyo khyi spyi lo 1142la rje btsun rtse mo byon/ lo gsum pa la 'jam dbyangs/ kyai rdor/ sgrol ma gsum gyi zhal
gzigs/ bcu drug pa yan la rgyud man ngag gi sgro 'dogs chod/ bcu bdun pa la cha pa'i drung du byon/ snga phyir lo bcu gcig tu mdo phyogs kyi sgro 'dogs bcad cha pa sku gshegs
pa'i tshe/ chos khri'i steng du sku 'bum bzhengs pa la/ rtse mor gser tog phul/ cha pa'i sku tshad dang mnyam pa'i ras bris phyag bris su gnang ba la/ rdzas mdog ma
'dres so sor 'byed pa'i mig rtsa dmar po can zhes sogs kyi bstod pa yang yod zer ro/ nyer bdun par me mo phag la chos la 'jug pa'i sgo brtsams/ nyer brgyad par gsung ngag
rin po che gnang ba'i sgo nas/ gdul bya skal ldan la 'jam dbyangs phyag na padma/ bi rU pa gnyis kyi dag pa'i snang ba bstan/ zhe gcig pa chu pho stag gi smal po zla'i tshes
bcu gcig la dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/ rje pas mdzad pa'i gsol 'debs gdung dbyangs ma'i mchan las/ tshes bcu'i dgong rje btsun sku mched sogs kyis tshes bcu'i mchod pa
mdzad/ nang pa rje pas byon pas/ na bza' sbu gu thibs pe sku lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod la bzhud/ gdung dbyangs kyi gsol ba drag tu btab pas/ na bza'i sbu gu nas/ bung
ba'i skad lta bu'i lung bstan khyad par can byung zhes bshad do/sum stong nyis brgya dang don dgu 'das pa'i brgyad cu pa me mo yos spyi lo 1147 la rje btsun grags pa byon/
brgyad lon pa'i tshe byang sems zla rgyal las tshangs spyod dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa nod/ bcu gsum pa la dpal

ldan sa skya'i gdan sar phebs/ nga drug pa chu pho khyi lo snye mo ru mtshams kyi gtsang khang dgon par mtshan gyi 'od gsal chen po'i ngang las/ bla ma sa chen gyi sku ye shes
kyi snang ba bstan te/ lam 'bras shin tu nye brgyud ces grags pa brda don gsal ba'i bka' drin mchog tu nos so/ rang lo bdun cu pa me pho byi ba'i dbo zla'i tshes bcu
gnyis la dag pa'i hing du gshegs kyi bar du bstan pa'i bya ba kho na mdzad pa'i sras kyi dam pa ni chos rje sa pan nyid yin la/ grags pa'i mtha' can bzhir grags pa ni/kar
shAkya grags/ nub pa rig 'dzin grags/ nA ro bandhe gshin rje grags/ gsal la ba dbang phyug grags dang bzhi'o/grags pa mi brgyad ces grags pa ni/ snga ma bzhi'i steng du/
gras ston blo gros grags/ dga' ston rdo rje grags/ lhe ston dkon mchog grags/ sa ston 'jigs med grags dang bzhi la 'jog par sems so/gur rgyan zhus pa'i mi bzhi ni/ mu chu
byang chub grags/ gtsang ston brtson 'grus grags/ lha thog yon tan gzung / rigs ldan shes rab rin chen dang bzhi'o/rig 'dzin gyi sdom brtson chen po bzhi ni/ jo sras lcags
kyi rdo rje/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chen po/ rtsis 'dul gzhon nu seng ge/ khams kyi 'ji yon tan dge slong /des na da lta'i shing byi 'di sa chen gyi chu spre nas bzhi
brgya don gsum/ rtse mo'i chu khyi nas bzhi brgya dang nyer gsum/ grags pa'i me yos nas bzhi brgya dang bco brgyad lon pa'i lo de yin no zhes bshad par bya'o/

sum stong nyis brgya dang bcu gcig 'das pa'i bcu gnyis pa sa mo lug spyi lo 1079 la bka' brgyud dwags po bltams/ rang lo nyer drug pa la mar yul blo ldan la bsnyen par rdzogs/
thog mar rnal 'byor pa chen po'i slob bu mang ra brtson 'grus 'bar sogs las bka' gdams gsan/ rang lo so gnyis lon pa'i tshe/ rje mi la lo don gcig bzhes pa'i skabs su
mjal te bka' brgyud kyi zab chos gsan/ bka' phyag chu bo gnyis 'dres kyi gdams pa nyams su blangs/ khyad par du dwags po bka' brgyud ces snyan pas phyogs kun tu khyab pa
lags so/ 'di nyid don lnga pa bya lo sgrog gi tshes bco lnga'i snga dro gshegs so/de la slob bu'i tshogs ni/ dwags po sgom tshul/ phag mo gru pa/ grub thob dbu se/ dha ('ba')
rom ras pa ste rgyud 'dzin gyi bu chen bzhi/dwags po sgom chung / rmog chog (lcog) pa/ gsol (gsal) stong sgom shor (she)/ bla ma 'ol ka ba ste/ thugs sras bzhi/dwags
po 'dul 'dzin la sogs pa nye sras bzhi sogs mang du byon yang rgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo phag gru pa nyid lags so/dwags po 'di sa chen las lo bcu gsum gyis bgres so/dwags
po'i slob ma phag mo gru pa/ dbu se'am dus gsum mkhyen pa/ gsal stong sgom she gsum la khams pa mi gsum zhes grags te/ sum stong nyis brgya dang zhe gnyis 'das pa'i zhe gsum
pa lcags pho stag spyi lo 1110 la phag gru pa dang dus gsum mkhyen pa gnyis bltams/ 'di nyid sa chen las lo bco brgyad kyis gzhon/

de yang phag gru pas lo bco brgyad pa la dbus su byon// rgya dmar la dbu tshad gsan te nyer lnga pa la// zul phur bya 'dul gyis mkhan po/ stod lung rgya dmar gyis slob dpon/
ar gyis gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs shing mdo la sbyangs/ de nas gtsang du byon/ las stod dkon mchog mkhar gyi sras gsum gyi ya gcig yin/ sras dgra pa nyin phug
pa chos grags stag sde seng ge lung du chu mo bya la 'khrungs/ sa chen las lo gnyis kyis gzhon/ de nas phag gru pas dpal ldan sa skyar phebs/ sa chen la snga phyir lo
bcu gsum du bsten/ gzhung bshad bshad mdzod mar grags pa de zin thor sdebs/ khong gi slob ma pradznyA kirtis de la 'grel bshad kyang mdzad da lta yang lung rgyun bzhugs/
byang sems zla rgyal la sems bskyed dang / dmar chos rgyal la bde mchog sogs gsan/ phyis dwags po rin po che'i zhabs pad bsten/ dgung lo zhe dgu pa la phag grur phebs/ 'jag
spyil rin po cher lo bdun bzhugs/ grwa pa brgyad brgya la gdugs thogs lnga brgya byung zer/ re gcig pa lcags pho stag zla ba bdun pa'i nyer lnga la gshegs so/de la slob
ma'i mchog/ mos gus mthar thug stag lung pa bkra shis 'bar/ rtogs pa'i mthar thug sna bu pa gling ras/ shes rab mthar thug pa par bu ba/ nus pa mthar thug pa mtshan bu
ba ste bka' babs bu chen bzhi/ par bu ba 'di cha pa'i slob ma shes rab can bzhi'i/ par bu bar grags pa de yin/skal ldan ye shes seng ge/ rtogs ldan mi nyag sgom rin/ grub
thob

nyang re se bo/ kun ldan gtsang pa ras chung bzhi la gdams pa'i bu bzhi zer/'bri khung skyu ra rin chen dpal/ chos rje lta bum pa/ chos rje rgyal tsha/ ban dha phug pa bzhi
la ro gcig rtogs pa phyed dang bzhi zer te/ bandha phug pa jo mo yod pas phyed zer ro/ de sogs mang du yod kyang gtso bo bsdus na/ gling ras 'bri stag gnyis/ khro phu ba
kun ldan/ gtsang pa ras chung dang bzhir 'dus so/dus gsum mkhyen pa'am dbu se ni/ bcu drug lon pa'i tshe/ rngog lo'i slob ma bre bo mchog gi bla ma dang / chag seng ge grags
las rab tu byung / mtshan dpal chos kyi grags pa zer/ lo nyi shu pa la dbus stod lung se thang du byon/ rgya dmar dang cha pa las dbu tshad/ sha ra ba las bka' gdams/
pa tshab las rigs tshogs/ sa skya pa'i thugs sras gshen rdor bzang las lam 'bras/ sga lo dang a seng la sbyor drug sogs gsan/ mal 'dul 'dzin la bsnyen par rdzogs/ lo gsum
pa la dwags po'i sras su gyur/ lo brgyad cu rtsa bzhi pa la gshegs so/de'i slob ma ni/ brgyud 'dzin gyi bka' babs 'gro mgon ras chen/ 'gro don gyi bka' babs grwa pa bka'
gdams pa/ rtogs pa'i bka' babs dbra sgom pa chos brtson/ rdzu 'phrul bka' babs te chung sangs rgyas dang bzhi'o/sum stong nyis brgya dang nga lnga 'das pa'i nga drug pa
chu mo yos spyi lo 1123 la skye med zhang brtson 'grus grags pa byon/ dwags po sgom tshul dang / sga lo sogs bsten/ tshal dang gung thang sogs btab/ don

gnyis pa chu mo glang la gung thang gi 'bum mo che bzhengs/ bang rim gsum pa'i tshe zhi bar gshegs so/ des na da lta'i shing byi 'di/ dwags po'i sa mo lug nas bzhi brgya dang
gya drug/ phag gru pa dang dus gsum mkhyen pa'i lcags stag nas nyis brgya dang nyer lnga/ zhang gi chu mo yos nas bzhi brgya dang zhe gnyis su slebs pa'i lor shes par
mdzod cig/sum stong nyis brgya dang drug cu 'das pa'i re gcig pa sa pho sprel spyi lo 1128 lo gling ras bltams/ rang lo so gcig pa nas rgyal ba lo dang / sum pa lo sogs lo
ras mched gsum snga phyir lo bco lnga bsten te/ nA ro pa'i gdams pa nyams su bzhes/ zhe gcig pa la phag gru pa'i lhan cig skyes sbyor gsan pas/ chu bo gangga tshun na lta
ba bzang bar grags/ dbyar zla gsum phag grur bzhugs/ bud med sngon mo zhig gis mdo rgyud kyi lung gnang bas mdo rgyud rang dbang du 'grel ba'i spobs pa thob/ bka' 'gyur
thugs la bzhugs/ mkha' 'gro ma lngas rigs lnga'i dbu rgyan rgyu gos chen la sku rnams thugs las bton pa phul ba da lta yang sna phu chos lung na yod zer/ rang lo re gcig
pa sprel lo dbyar ra'i nyer brgyad la gshegs/'di skye med zhang las lo lngas gzhon no/ gling ras kyi slob ma'i gtso bo ni gtsang pa rgya ras ye shes rdo rje'o/ dgung lo
lnga bcu nga gcig bzhugs pa'o/sum stong nyis brgya dang don bzhi 'das pa'i don lnga pa chu pho khyi spyi lo 1142 la stag lung chos rje bkra shis dpal g.yang shod bong rar
bltams/ lo bco brgyad pa la rab tu byung / nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa la dbus su byon/

phag gru pa la lo drug bsten/ so dgu pa lcags pho byi lo la stag lung du phebs/ tshogs pa stong phrag 'dus/ rang lo re dgu pa rta lo mgo zla'i tshes bcu dgu la gshegs so/'bri
gung pa chen po ni/ khams kyi ldan mar chu mo phag spyi lo 1143la byon pas/ stag lung pa las lo gcig gis gzhon/ so lnga pa la zhang sum thog pa kye po ye rdor las bsnyen
par rdzogs/ sku gzhon nu nas phag gru pa bsten/ gdan sa lo gsum mdzad de gzhan don cher ma byung / phyis so bdun pa la 'bri khung du phebs/ tshogs pa lnga khri lnga stong
lnga brgya nyer lnga 'dus/ 'di ni slob dpon klu sgrub kyi skye bar grags te/ sing ga gling gi dgra bcom pa zhig gis/ kha che pan chen gyi gcung po la me tog bzhi bskur
te/ gcig 'bri zhes bya ba'i dgon pa na slob dpon klu sgrub byang chub sems dpa' rin chen dpal du skye ba glangs yod pa de la phul/ gcig ratna ku bzhi'i gtsug lag khang
na byang chub sems dpa' skal ldan shing rta yod pas de la phul/ gcig rwi bha ba zhig yod pa de la phul/ yang me tog gcig sa pan dang mjal tshe kha phye'o zhes pa'i gtam yang
snang ngo/ gcig des lha chen po zhig bzhengs pa 'dug pas de'i thugs kar zhog ces bshad pa dang / yang kha che pan chen klas mo cher bzhugs pa'i tshe 'bri khung pa'i khams
btsun zhig gis/ pan chen la chos gos slang zhes sku chos la 'jus/ nye gnas kyi kho brdabs te sna khrag byung bas/ pan chen thugs dam gyi tshe sgrol ma byon pa la zhag
bdun du ma byon te/ khyod dpon slob kyis klu sgrub kyi slob ma la sdig bsags nyes pa de sbyang ba la rab byung gzhan la rang gi lo grangs kyi chos gos byin cig ces sogs

bshad pa las shes so/ dgongs gcig la sogs pa'i bstan bcos brtsams/ thugs sras spyan snga bas 'grel pa yang mdzad do/ mthar rang lo don lnga pa glang lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nyer
lnga la sku gshegs pa las/ slob ma gnyis kyis tshogs pa la zhal ston par gsol bas slar 'od gsal las bzhengs te nyi ma gnyis su chos gnang bas nyer bdun la gshegs so/ mchod
pa gang la 'dzin zhus pas/ nyer lnga la gzung gsung nas lnga mchod du grags so/'di'i thugs sras ni/ spyan snga ba grags pa 'byung gnas te/ 'di nyid rje btsun grags pa
chos dbyings su gshegs pa'i gsol 'debs kyi tshogs dpon la/ chos rje sa pan gyis spyan drangs zhes kyang zer ro/ des na 'bri stag gnyis kyi bar na lo gcig las med la/ stag
lung pa chen po rje btsun bsod rtse dang na mnyam/ chos rje sa pan shar la thegs pa'i tshe/ 'bri khung 'jig rten mgon po mjal gsung ba cung mi 'grig pa 'dra ste/ de'i
[dus] 'bri stag gnyis char gshegs tshar bas/ des na de'i tshe 'bri khung spyan snga ba dang mjal las 'os med do/ de gnyis gling ras la lo bzhis gzhon no/bka' gdams pa'i skor
la/ glang thang pa shing pho rta lo yin pas sa chen las lo so brgyad kyis bgres/ sha ra ba lcags pho khyi lo ba ste/ sa chen las nyer gnyis kyis bgres/ bya yul ba gzhon
nu 'od shing mo yos lo pa ste sa chen las bco brgyad kyis bgres/ bya 'chad ka ba ye shes rdo rje lcags mo sbrul lo pa ste sa chen las lo dgus gzhon/ stabs ka ba dar ma

yon tan me mo lug lo pa ste sa chen las lo lngas gzhon/ bsod rtse las bco lngas bgres/ rje sgam po pa ni sha ra ba las lo brgyad dang / bya yul ba las lo bzhis gzhon/ gling

pa lags so/sum stong nyis brgya dang so gsum 'das pa'i so bzhi pa lcags mo sbrul spyi lo 1101 la/ gling gi thugs sras gtsang pa rgyal sras (rgya ras) nyang stod du byon/
'di rje btsun grags pa las bcu bzhis gzhon/ 'brug ra lung gi dgon pa btab/ 'brug pa zhes yongs su grags shing / nA ro pa'i sprul par byed/'di la slob ma'i mchog/ dbon sras
dang chos sras gnyis/ dang po ni/ dbon sras dar ma seng ge sogs so/ gnyis pa la dang por che ba spa rkyang gnyis/ bar du che ba brgya 'bras gnyis/ tha mar che ba lo rgod
gnyis sogs yod pa las/ dang po ni/ spa ri ba dang rkyang mo kha pa gnyis/ gnyis pa ni brgya legs pa dang 'bras mo ba gnyis/ gsum pa ni lo ras pa dang rgod tshang pa gnyis
so/de yang lo nas mched pa la smad 'brug dang / rgod tshang pa nas mched pa la stod 'brug dang / dbon sras sogs kyis skyong ba la bar 'brug ces grags so/gzhan yang sku'i
sprul pa dam pa sa skor ba/ gsung gi sprul pa dam pa gter khung pa/ thugs kyi sprul pa dam pa ko brag pa/ 'phrin las sprul

nyag bzhi ru slebs pa ni shing pho byi lo 'di yin no/gsum pa/ sum stong sum brgya pa'i skabs su byon pa ni/ ko brag pa/ khro lo/ sa lo/ rgod tshang pa rnams te/ de yang sum
stong sum brgya gnyis 'das pa'i gsum pa lcags pho stag spyi lo 1170 la ko brag pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan ding rir byon/ lo brgyad cu bzhugs/ dwags po bka' brgyud dang

ba bzhi'o/deb sngon las ko brag pa sa pan dang dgung mnyam yin zer ro/ dus gsal gyi lugs ltar na sa pan las lo skor gcig gis bgres so/sum stong sum brgya dang bzhi 'das pa'i

dm: rin chen mgon po dang / de'i dbon po kun ldan gtsang pa ras chung gnyis yod pa'i/ kun ldan ras pa'i dbon po yin la/ kun ldan ras pa'i slob ma gcig ri mas dm: ma cig re
ma/ nya pa lus skyes zhes pa la bu gcig skyes pa skyes bu dam pa gcig %'byor ldan% shes nas gso skyong mdzad pas gces sgom rdzong par grags/ mkha' skyong brag pa zhes kyang
bya/

'di nyid sa chen gyi dngos slob du 'dod/'ga' zhig/ sa chen gyi dngos slob rgyal tsha ta la phug pa yin la/ de dang ma gcig ri ma'i dngos slob gces sgom rdzong pa yin zer/'ga'
zhig 'di 'khrungs yul khams pa yin la/ nyi gzhug brag tu lta ba nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i don skyong ba'i mkha' skyong brag pa dang / rtag nag ga ga'i rdzong la sgom pas
gces sgom rdzong par yang grags zer/bdag gi bla ma ni/ gces sgom 'di la rta nag gces sgom dang / kha rag gces sgom sogs yod pa'i/ man ngag rin spungs gsung ba po ni rta
nag gces sgom yin gsung ngo/gang ltar na'ang khro los/ rje mi tra/ pan chen buddha shrI/ shAkya shrI gsum rim pas spyan drangs/ byams chen bzhengs pa sogs bstan pa'i bya
ba mtha' yas pa mdzad do/ 'di dang rje sa pan rtsod pa mdzad pa'i rtsod yig kyang yod do/sum stong sum brgya dang bcu bzhi song ba'i bco lnga pa chu pho stag spyi lo 1182
la gangs can mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan sa skya panDi ta byon/ chu stag de nas sum brgya dang dgu bcu rtsa gsum lon pa'i lo ni da lta'i shing byi 'di yin la/ des na phyi dar

gsung dbyangs snyan par

sgrogs/ bco lnga man chad la/ rje btsun chen po'i drung du/ sa skya gong ma'i gsung gi bcud mdo sngags kyi zab gnad yongs su rdzogs/ bcu dgu pa la ku mud bzhad pa'i dus kyi
'od gsal chen po'i ngang las/ a phyi 'bum pa'i drung du mkhas mchog dbyig gnyen la chos mngon pa mdzod dang / kha che pan chen la de nyid kyi chos zab mo rdo rje'i glu las
legs par nod/ rgya gar shar phyogs su phyogs kyi glang po'i gdan seng ge'i khri la 'khod de/ glegs bam gzhal du med pa'i lde mig bzung / pad dkar bzhad pa'i dus kyi mdangs
rab tu rgyas pa'i tshe/ 'phrang du zhu ston rdo rje skyabs la byams chos sogs lung gi chos skor/ nyi shu pa la rkyang 'dur du/ rma bya byang brtson dang gtsang nag pa'i
slob ma mtshur ston gzhon seng la bod bgres po nas brgyud pa'i tshad ma'i chos skor/ gzhan yang cha pa'i seng chen brgyad kyi rtsegs pa dbang phyug seng ge la bod la
grags pa'i grub mtha' bzhi'i chos ji snyed pa/ spyi bo lhas pa byang chub 'od la/ bod la grags pa'i zhi byed rdzogs chen gcod bka' gdams la sogs pa'i gdams ngag ji snyed
pa khong du chud/ nyer gsum pa shing pho byi lor gtsang chu mig tu kha che pan chen dang mjal/ pan chen de nyid dang de'i slob bu rgya gar shar nub gung gsum na sgra la mkhas
par grags pa'i sam ga shrI ste dge 'dun dpal dang / su ga tA shrI ste legs par gshegs pa'i dpal dang / dA na shI la ste tshul khrims sbyin sogs snga phyir bsten te/
bod rgan po'i 'dres kyis ma bslad pa'i lha rgyan gyi bshad srol las byon pa'i tshad ma la sogs pa'i rig gnas che ba lnga/ snyan ngag/ sdeb sbyor/ mngon brjod/ zlos gar/ rtsis
te rig gnas chung ba lnga ste/ rig gnas bcus bsdus pa'i

zab chos thams cad/ chos sgo skyel du byon pa'i sgo nas legs par nod de sa panDi ta zhes snyan par grags/pan chen dbus nas 'khor rjes de nyid kyis nyi shu rtsa bdun bzhes pa'i
sa pho 'brug gi lo lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug gis bzhengs pa'i nyang smad rgyan gong gi gtsug lag khang du/ kha che pan chen gyis mkhan po/ spyi bo lhas pa byang chub
'od kyis las slob/ don mo ri pas gsang ston bgyis te bsnyen par rdzogs/sa pan 'di nyid sku bltams pa'i lor rje btsun rtse mo 'ja' lus su gshegs pas zhal gyi bdud rtsi dngos
su ma thob kyang / rang lo so lnga pa'i bar du grags pa'i 'chi med bdud rtsi ngoms par gsol/ khyad par lam bzab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi sgo nas phyi nang gi rten
'brel gyi gnad rang sar 'grig ste sa dang po'i yon tan mchog tu bsnyes/ nyid kyi so gsum pa la kha che pan chen slar kha cher bzhud/ so lnga pa la rje btsun chen po bde ba
can du gshegs/ rje sa pan so lnga pa'i tshe grags pa gshegs dus bstan rtsis mdzad pa na so lnga pa me khyi yan la sum stong sum brgya dang lnga bcu song bas slan chad kyang
de bzhin rtsi bar bya'o/ zhes 'di pa ltar gyi rtsis khrul med pa 'di yin no/ so brgyad pa tsam gyi tshe/ rgya bod kyi ngag rtog gi brag ri 'joms par byed pa'i tshad
ma'i bstan bcos rigs pa'i gter zhes grags pa de brtsams/ lnga bcu rtsa gcig tsam gyi tshe legs bshad kyi sbrang rtsi spel ba'i dga' ston/ bstan pa'i pad tshal rgyas par byed
pa'i sdom gsum rab dbye'i nyin byed kyang shar/ lnga bcu rtsa dgu pa'i tshe 'phags pa wa ti'i dri'i gtsang khang dang 'dabs 'byor ba'i dpal

gyi gnas su/ rgya gar lho phyogs kyi 'phrog byed dga' bo la sogs pa'i phas kyi rgol ba ngan pa drug lung rigs kyis tshar bcad de rgyal ba'i bstan pa la bcug/ gang gi snyan
pa'i rnga sgra gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir ma shongs te/ rgya dkar nag dang hor bal gyi ljongs thams cad kyang gang bar byas/ drug cu rtsa gsum pa'i tshe/ stobs kyi 'khor los
bsgyur ba rgya nag mtha'i rgyal po go dan gyis bsod nams kyi mgron du spyan drangs/ drug cu rtsa lnga pa me pho rta'i lor pho brang chen po ling chu rtser gdan phebs/ rgyal
pos nyams sad pa'i phyir sgyu ma'i dri gtsang khang khang phran gyis bskor ba'i gtsug lag khang gi sgyu 'phrul gyi rwa bar spyan drangs pa'i tshe/ ting nge 'dzin gyi mthus
brtan par bzhugs su gsol te/ byang phyogs sprul pa'i sde'i gtsug lag khang zhes phyogs kun tu snyan pas grags/ sgyu ma'i mkhan po la bslus chen po der byung / rgyal
po 'khor bcas dga' bdes yid rab tu gsos/ bdun cu pa'i bar du rgya nag po'i yul du bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa spel/ lcags phag smal zla'i bcu bzhi'i tho rangs sku'i bkod pa
re zhig bsdus/sku'i skye ba phyi ma mkha' la spyod pa'i rig pa 'dzin pa'i gar gyis rol/ de nas gnyis pa'i tshe/ shar phyogs mu mu nir rgyal po nyi ma stobs 'phel gyi sras
dam par gyur te sa lam phal cher bgrod/ de nas gsum pa'i tshe mngon dga'i zhing du bde bar gshegs pa dri ma med pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas/ longs sku'i cha byad
sku mdog gangs ri'i mdog can chos 'chad kyi phyag rgya can rin po che'i rgyan dang rab tu mdzes pa'i gos klubs pa dag pa'i 'khor 'bum gyis bskor ba'o/

de ltar na phyi dar nyid la bstan pa'i nyin byed lan gsum shar te/ lo chen rin bzang gis/ dar mas bstan pa bsnubs rjes kyi chos min thams cad tshar bcad/ de rjes mgos rngog
rnam gnyis kyis blo bar gyi chos log thams cad sun dbyung / de nas bzung ste chos rje sa skya pa chen po grags pa'i mtha' can gyi sku'i tshe'i stod smad lo brgya tsam zhig
bstan pa sprin med kyi mkha' ltar gnas pa las/ phyis rang bzo phag mo'i byin rlabs/ yi dam dkrong bskyed/ gtum mo bde skyod/ sems skyed rmi lam (ma)/ sems skyed rku thabs/
bsngo ba yod dge/ dkar po chig thub sogs/ chos min gyi rnam grangs brgya rtsa zhig gi mun rum tshar gcod pa la bstan bcos sdom gsum rab dbye'i nyin byed 'di shar ba
yin/ des na deng gi dus na rgyal ba'i bstan pa la lung rigs kyis cung zad dpyad du yod pa 'di pan chen 'di nyid kyi bka' drin yin no/ shes bya rig gnas lnga'i sgo phye ste/
rig pa'i gnas la blo kha chung zhig phyogs pa'i bod kyi gzhon nu blo gsal dag la panDi ta zhes pa'i mtshan tsam gyis kyang kha ba can 'di dkar por byas pa min nam/ de
yang phyi dar la lo chen rin chen bzang po'i sku ngo la/ rmal lo tsA bas tshad ma la bshad pa cung zad mdzad cing / khyung po grags ses kyang tshad ma bshad de tshad ma rnying
ma zhes pa'i bstan pa cung zad dar/ de rjes rngog lo chen pos tshad ma rgyan dang chos mchog gtso bor bton te tshad ma gsar ma zhes bya ba'i bstan pa spel/ de nyid
kyi dngos brgyud kyi slob bu dag gi rang bzor sgro btags pa'i tshad ma'i bstan pa ha cang dar ches pa'i tshe/ dag ma dag gi rab dbye legs par phye ste/ sde bdun gyi snying
po gsal bar ston pa'i tshad ma rigs pa'i

gter zhes bya ba'i sgo nas tshad ma'i bstan pa ji lta ba bzhin shar ba yin zhing / rig gnas gzhan la yang des mtshon te shes par mdzod cig/sa panDi ta'i slob ma'i mchog rtogs
pa'i brgyud 'dzin tshogs grub dbon gsum/ man ngag gi brgyud 'dzin lho dmar rnam gnyis/ bshad pa'i brgyud 'dzin shar nub gung gsum/ sdom phrug bgres pa dpal bzang po bcu
gsum/ gzhon pa rgyal mtshan gyi mtha' can bdun/ lo tsA ba chen po bzhi/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor pa chen po bzhi/ mkhas btsun gyi thugs sras bzhi/ sgrub pa'i brgyud 'dzin rgyal
ba yang dgon pa/ sbas pa'i grub chen zangs tsha bsod rgyal lo/de dag kyang rim pa ltar/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ gtsang sgyer phur lcags pho rta la byon/ chos rje
pa lo bcu gsum bsten/ go brgyad pa la gshegs/ sa pan las lo nyer brgyad kyis gzhon/grub chen yon tan dpal stag ste ngam rings su byon/ chos rje pa lo drug bsten/ se mo che
ras pa zhes grags/dbon po 'phags pa rin po che sa pan nga bzhi bzhes pa'i shing mo lug la byang ngam rings klung khungs su byon no/tshogs grub dbon gsum gyi brgyud pa 'dzin
pa la la nyan zhang gsum zhes grags te/ la ru ba bsod nams bzang po/ stag rtse la ru gser khang du byon/ bco brgyad pa la 'phags pas rab tu byung / shar pa rdo rje 'od
zer la rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ phyis spyi'i sen mo rang grub thob yon tan dpal la lo gsum gsung ngag gsan no/

nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa la stod byang mdog rje rong dbyig mkhar du chu pho rta la byon/ tshogs sgom pa lo bcu gsum bsten/ lo go drug bzhugs/tshogs sgom pa las lo bcu gnyis
kyis gzhon no/ lho pa kun mkhyen rin chen dpal lho pha drug pa yin/ sku shin tu bgres pa nas byang ngos su brda don gsal ba'i tho sgrig zhu ba la byon/ dmar chos rgyal/
pu rangs lo chung gi dngos slob dmar chos rgyal mtshan gyi dbon rgyud yin/ chos rje pa lo brgyad bsten/shar nub gung gsum gyi/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas dang / shar
pa rdo rje 'od zer te sku mched gnyis/ nub pa 'u yug pa rigs pa'i seng ge/ de'i dbon po nyi thogs pa sangs rgyas kun smon/de'i ka chen khang gnyan zhang gsum zur khang
pa dang bzhir grags pa'i khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ gnyan dar ma seng ge/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ zur khang pa dkar shakya grags/ gung pa la skyo ston dri med de/ de thams
cad sa pan gyi dngos slob yin no/ dkar shAka ni gtso bor grags pa yin no/sdom phrug bgres pa bcu gsum ni/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal bzang po/ rin chen skyob pa dpal bzang
po/ lho pa kun mkhyen rin chen dpal bzang po/ zhang rgyal ba dpal bzang po/ zhang mdo sde dpal bzang po/ phyi ru ba seng ge dpal bzang po/ grub snying po rdo rje dpal
bzang po/ ldong ston shes rab dpal bzang po/ jo gdan byang chub dpal bzang po/

kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal bzang po/ skyi ston dri med dpal bzang po (gnyis chad) rnams so/jo gdan byang chub dpal ni/ chos rje pa'i slob ma shin tu yin kyang / kha che pan chen
gyi mkhan bu yin pas chos rje pa'i sdom phrug tu cung zhig mi rigs pa 'dra mod/ 'on kyang rje kun mkhyen gyi Tika ltar bgrangs pa'o/gzhon pa rgyal mtshan gyi mtha' can
bdun ni/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ gsol ja ba 'dul ba rgyal mtshan/ 'u yug pa dpal gyi rgyal mtshan/
yar klungs pa shAkya rgyal mtshan/ yar klungs pa byang chub rgyal mtshan rnams so/de yang yar klungs pa byang chub rgyal mtshan ni/ chos rje pa'i rnam thar tshigs bcad
ma rgyas pa rtsom pa po yin la/ rnam thar bsdus pa rtsom pa po'i yar klungs pa grags pa rgyal mtshan yang bsnan nas rgyal mtshan gyi mtha' can brgyad ces bya'o/lo chen
bzhi ni/ phyag (chag) lo tsA ba chos rje dpal/ glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ rong pa sga lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ zhang lo tsA ba grub pa dpal dang bzhi'o/chag lo ni/
chag dgra bcom gyi dbon po ste/ me mo sbrul lo la byon/ sa pan las lo bco lngas gzhon no/zhang lo ni/ kha che pan chen gyi slob ma'ang yin la gtso bor ras chung snyan brgyud
kyi brgyud pa la bzhugs pa de'o/yar klungs pa rgyal tsha lung gi dbang phyug/ zhang bya ru ba Arya de wa/

long bu ba bsod nams rin chen/ slang ra ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan de sbas pa'i rnal 'byor pa chen po bzhi/mkhas btsun chen po bzhi ni/ bo don pa rin chen brtson 'grus rdo rje/
gtsang nags phug pa 'jam dbyangs shes rab 'od zer/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bzod pa ring mo/ te ra pa byams pa mgon po dang bzhi'o/bo dong rin po che ni lcags pho sprel lo
pa ste/ sa pan las lo bco brgyad kyis gzhon/gtsang nags phug tu mkhas pa yongs su grags pa gsum byon pa'i/ gtsang nags brtson 'grus seng ge ni/ cha pa'i seng chen gcig yin
la/ gtsang nags phug pa thugs rje seng ge ni/ jo nang kun spangs zhang gi slob ma ste bar do 'phrang sgrol mdzad pa po de yin/'jam dbyangs shes rab 'od zer ni/ thog mar
sa pan la dgag pa mdzad pas 'jam dbyangs mi dges pa'i rnam pa bstan/ bshags pa byas te chos rje khu dbon gyi thugs sras su gyur pa'o/sum stong sum brgya dang bcu drug 'das
pa'i shing pho 'brug spyi lo 1184 la zangs tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan sku 'bum rnam rgyal du byon/ dgung lo nga drug pa sa mo phag rgyal zla'i nyer gnyis la mdog ros
kyi sag rir gshegs/ 'phags pa dang 'gro mgon phyag na gnyis [slob dpon rin chen rgyal mtshan] slob dpon ye shes 'byung gnas gnyis la re zhig zangs tsha'i sras bzhi zer/
phyi ma gnyis sa pho khyi lo pa dgung mnyam yin no/sum stong sum brgya dang nyer gcig 'das pa'i nyer gnyis pa sa mo bya

spyi lo 1189 la rgod gtsang pa mgon po rdo rje bltams/ lo bcu dgu pa la rab tu byung / gtsang pa rgya ras kyi zhabs zung zla ba gsum bsten/ kong po nas dza lan dha ra'i bar
gyi gnas rnams su sgrub pa gzhan don kho na mdzad/ bdun cu bzhes pa rta lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes gsum la gshegs/slob ma'i mchog rang las lhag pa gcig/ rang dang mnyam pa
brgyad sogs byon pa las/ rang las lhag pa ni yang dgon pa yin la mnyam pa brgyad ni rten 'brel rang dang mnyam pa ne rings pa/ sgrub tshugs rang dang mnyam pa pu tri ri
khrod gling pa/ mos gus rang dang mnyam pa spyil dkar ba/ snying rje rang dang mnyam pa ma bdun pa/ zhen log rang dang mnyam pa gangs shAkya bshes gnyen/ dag snang rang
dang mnyam pa nam mkha' rdo rje/ dka' spyad rang dang mnyam pa g.ya' mdo rings kyi shAkya ras pa/ brtul zhugs rang dang mnyam pa grub chen u rgyan pa dang brgyad do/des na
rgod tshang pa byon pa'i sa mo bya nas sum brgya dang don drug yin la 'di sa pan las lo bdun gyis gzhon/sum stong sum brgya dang so lnga 'das pa'i so drug chu mo phag spyi
lo 1203 la rong pa sga lo byon/ khams pa sga lo'i skye bar bzung nas sga lo zer/ khams pa sga lo 'di sa chen dang phar slob tshur slob yin/ dpyal lo'i drung du rgya yig
sogs la sbyangs/ brgyad cu pa la gshegs so/'di'i slob ma ni/ 'phags pa rin po che/ khro phu rin po che/ lho pa grub seng / thang ston lo tsA grags rgyal/ sman?man lung
pa chen po'o/sum stong sum brgya so drug 'das pa'i so bdun pa shing pho byi lo spyi lo

1204 la kha che pan chen shAkya shrI bha dra 'khor pan chung dgu dang bcas te bod du phebs/ de'i tshe ko brag pas lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ khro los so gsum/ sa los lo nyi shu
rtsa gsum/ rgod tshang pas bcu drug lon/ des na jo bo rje bod du byon pa'i shing pho rta lo nas/ lo brgya dang lnga bcu 'das pa'i nga gcig pa shing pho byi lo pan chen shAkya
shrI bod du byon pa yin zhes bya'o/'khor pan chung dgu ni/ dbu phar la mkhas pa su ga ta shrI/ sngags 'dul la mkhas pa dza ya ratna/ sgra dang mngon pa la mkhas pa bi
bi bhu ti tsandra/ tshad ma la mkhas pa dA na shI la/ tsandra pa la mkhas pa sam gha shrI/ mngon pa gong 'og la mkhas pa su ma ti garabha/ dus 'khor la mkhas pa dzi na
su pa ta/ spyod 'jug la mkhas pa ma hA bo dhi rnams so/de yang kha che khri brtan gyi bye brag dza sho dha ra zhes par shing mo glang gi lo spyi lo 1145 pan chen 'di nyid
sku bltams/ lo bcu pa la bram ze landha ra la sgra rig gsan/ lo dgu nas nyer gnyis bar la tshangs spyod dge bsnyen mdzad/ nyer gsum pa la mkhan po su kha shrI bha dra bde
ba dpal bzang po las rab tu byung / nyer dgu'i bar du kha cher bzhugs/ sum cu pa la yul dbus ma ga dhar byon/ mkhan po shanata ka ra gupta ste zhi ba'i 'byung gnas sbas
pa dang / da sha bha la dang / gsang ston dha bar ka sogs bco brgyad las bsnyen par rdzogs/ drug cu bzhes pa'i tshe khro lo lo so gsum lon pa gcig gis byi lo mchu'i zla
ba la spyan 'dren la byon te rgya gar bai durya'i tshog 'dus su phebs/ shAkya'i bstan la shAkya'i sras bltams shAkya'i mtshan/ zhes sogs kyi zhu yig rten dang bcas phul/
ba ne sha ra bya ba pan chen dang

mjal/ pan chen gyi gsung gis/ lo tsA ba 'di chos mang du shes pa/ lha chen po bzhengs pa'i stobs yod pa'i yar rgan cig yod bsam pa la na tshod gzhon nur 'dug/ chos sgyur ba'i
lo tsA ba yang mi phod/ sgrub thabs 'ga' byin la 'o skol dpon slob phyir log gsungs/ panDi ta dzA ya shrIs dpon slob rnams lo tsA ba'i gzugs la brnyas 'dug pas 'bel ba'i
gtam smros shig ces skabs dbye/ lo tsA bas pan chung dgu la dri ba mi 'dra ba gnyis gnyis byas/ pan chen rab tu dges te spyan drangs pa'i rngo thogs/ pan chung rnams la'ang
do li byas te rim pas spyan drangs/ chu mig tu khro phu'i bsu ba'i bkod pa dge 'dun drug cu/ dar gdugs rol mo sogs drug cu dang bcas pas khro phur spyan drangs/ de'i
tshe sa panDi tas yab dpal chen 'od po phag lo sku gshegs nas/ gshegs rdzongs kyi sku skal rkyang 'dur du 'bul bar phebs pa'i bar lam chu mig tu chos rje dang mjal/ tshad
ma chos mchog gi bstod pa sogs mdzad pa yin er/ khro phur byi lo'i dbyar gnas mdzad/ tshul shing len pa brgyad brgya byung / brgyad stong pa sogs gsungs so/ lo tsA bas
dar zab kyi thun yon de ma chag par phul/ lho brag pa byang chub dpal la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / dbus la 'bri khung pas spyan 'dren pa'i cha rkyen mang po slebs/ slas mo cher
phebs/ rgya gar nas spyan drangs pa'i rten mchod rnams zhal phye/ mchod pa gzab par phul/ gtsang po ba bsod nams mdzes kyis mjal/ bdag bsnyen par rdzogs nas ltung ba
byung ba ma dran pas tshul khrims bsrungs pa'i dge ba bsngo bar zhus pas/ dbu zhwa zul gyi phud phyag thal mo sbyar nas bsngo ba rgyu bzang 'di lta bu rgya gar na yang dkon
gsungs

nas bsngo ba mdzad/ glang lo'i dbyar gnas slas mo cher mdzad dgag dbye thon nas chu mig ring mor byon/ rgyan gong gnas su rdo rje dpal la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / gzhu snye mo'i
nang la byon/ mtshur phu nas stod lung brgyud de jo bo rnam gnyis la mchod pa phul/ mtshur phu ba'i skyel mi rnams la/ khyed kyi dgon pa na sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud
nas bshad pa'i sku gsum snang ba khyed kyis ngo ma shes gsungs/ sku gsum ni bde mchog yab yum go ldog/ shAkya thub pa sprul sku la yum rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ rdo rje dril bu
mnyam sbyor gyi lha dang gsum mo/ de nas srin po rir stag lo dbyar gnas mdzad/ byams chos khrid dang rigs tshogs rnams gsungs/ me mo yos la sol nag thang po cher phebs/
bstan rtsis mdzad pa na/smin drug zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi//tshes brgyad nam gung mnyam pa la//zla ba ri bo la nub tshe//thub dbang yongs su mya ngan 'das//de rjes lo ni
stong phrag gcig//bdun brgya dang ni lnga bcu dang //zla ba gnyis dang zla ba phyed//de bzhin nyi ma snga rabs 'das//zhes sogs bshad/'o na rang lugs kyi skar rtsis dang
ches mi mthun on snyam na skyon med de/ pan chen gyi bstan rtsis kyi 'das lo'i thog ma ni/ mtho btsun grub rje dang bde byed bdag pos byang chub chen po'i sku bzhengs dus
kyi me mo sbrul nas bzung ba yin no zhes bshad zin la/ de lta bu'i me sbrul de ni/ 'das lo nas stong dang lnga brgya gya dgu 'das pa'i dgu bcu pa yin no zhes kyang bshad
zin zhing / pan chen gyi bstan rtsis 'di ni me mo yos lo nag pa zla ba'i tshes lnga la mdzad pa yin pa dang / me yos nag pa zla ba'i tshes lnga ni/

ma hA bo dhi byon pa'i me sbrul nas/ lo stong dang bdun brgya dang lnga bcu 'das pa'i lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa me mo yos lo rang gi steng nas zla ba phyed dang gsum dang zhag
lnga song ba de yin par shin tu gsal ba'i phyir ro/ des na me yos 'di ni 'das lo nas lo sum stong sum brgya dang bzhi bcu dang pan chen bod du byon pa'i lo bzhi pa yin no/de
nas byang rwa sgreng du byon pa'i yar lam 'bri khung pas spyan drangs kyang / gdan cig pa dang bka' gdams pas gegs byas/ mjal du ma ster zer ro/ phyis de sa pho 'brug
gi lo gtsang du phebs/ nyang smad rgyan gong du sa pan la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / gsang ston spyi bo lhas pa byang chub 'od pa ni shing pho byi lo ste/ de'i tshe re lnga pa
yin/ sbrul lo'i dbyar gnas rin chen sgang du mdzad/ rta lo'i dbyar gnas shangs lu gu sdong (gdong) du mdzad/ lha btsun gung thang pa la bsnyen rdzogs gnang / sprel lo'i
dbyar gnas khro phur mdzad de/ chu pho sprel lo gre zla ba'i tshes gsum nas bcu gsum gyi bar du khro phu byams chen gyi rab gnas mdzad/ rim gyis khro phu nas mnga' ris su
phebs te/ bya lo'i dbyar gnas pu rangs su gnang / shing pho khyi lo kha cher phebs te lo nyer dgu tsam zhig tu bstan 'gro'i don mdzad/ dgu bcu rtsa dgu pa sgrog zla ba'i
tshes lnga la zhi bar gshegs/de la pan chen shing pho byi lor bod du phebs nas/ lo bcu gcig bod du bzhugs zer ba 'di la phal cher mthun mod/ 'khrungs lo la mi mthun pa
'ga' zhig 'dug pa'i/ deb sngon las/ pan chen me mo lug la bltams/ don brgyad pa shing pho byi lor bod du phebs/ chu mo bya'i bar lo

bcu bzhugs/ shing khyi la kha cher thegs/ go gcig shing bya la gshegs zer mod/ khro los mdzad pa'i bstod pa las/ gcig gis ma tshang lo brgya'i dus// bya lo sgrog zla'i dkar
phyogs kyi// spen pa'i nyi mai tshes lnga la// 'gro ba'i nyi ma nub par bstan// zhes go dgu pa bya lor zhi bar gshegs par bshad pa dang cung zad 'byor kyang / thub dbang
yongs 'das lo ni brgya phrag bcu// drug bcas dgu bcu rtsa gnyis mthar son tshe// shAkya'i bstan srog ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i gtsor// byon gyur drang srong de yi rnam thar
bris// zhes pa dang mi 'byor te/ lung des/ pan chen lugs kyi 'das lo nas stong dang drug brgya go gnyis 'das pa'i tshe pan chen sku 'khrungs par bshad la/ thang po cher bstan
rtsis mdzad pa'i me mo yos yan chad la lo stong dang bdun brgya lnga bcu 'das par pan chen rang gi bshad pa ltar yang khas blangs dgos pa las/ khyed ltar na thang po
che'i me mo yos lo ni pan chen gyi brgyad du rtsa gcig pa yin pas/ pan chen 'khrungs gong yan chad kyi stong drug brgya go gnyis dang / pan chen dgung lo gya gcig po bsres
pas stong bdun brgya don gsum du yang sleb 'dug pa'i phyir ro/jo brtan (gdan) mkhan chen chos grub seng ges mdzad pa'i pan chen gyi rnam thar las/ khro los mdzad pa'i/
thub dbang yongs 'das lo ni brgya phrag bcu// drug bcas dgu bcu rtsa gnyis mthar son nas// zhes pa 'di yi ge ma dag pa yin pas/ thub dbang yongs 'das lo ni brgya phrag bcu//
dgu bcas bdun cu rtsa gsum mthar son nas// zhes 'don dgos la/ de ltar na 'das lo nas lo stong dgu brgya don gsum 'das pa'i lcags pho sprel lo

pan chen bltams/ re lnga pa shing pho byi lor bod du phebs/ don lnga pa shing pho khyi la kha cher phebs/ go dgu pa khyi la zhi bar gshegs zhes bshad pa yang / thang po cher
rtsis pa'i bstan rtsis dang 'gal te/ khyed ltar na thang po che'i me yos ni pan chen gyi drug cu rtsa brgyad yin la/ drug cu rtsa brgyad po de dang / pan chen 'khrungs
gong gi lo stong dgu brgya don gsum po bsres pas/ nyis stong zhe gcig tu yang 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/des na kho bo ni skabs 'dir dus gsal sor bzhag nas/ kha che pan chen rang
nyid kyi bstan rtsis ltar gyi/ 'das lo'i stong dang drug brgya go gnyis 'das pa'i go gsum pa shing mo glang la pan chen bltams/ drug cu pa shing byi la bod du phebs/ bdun
cu pa shing khyi la mnga' ris nas kha cher phebs te go dgu pa la dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/ mnga' ris nas kha cher phebs dus jo gdan gtsang po ba/ byang rdor rnam gnyis
kyi gnas kyi slob dpon du bzhag/ shing khyi de nas lo bcu gcig pa pan chen gyi dgung lo brgyad cu lon pa'i tshe/ byang rdor rnam gnyis kyis dge 'dun gyi sde so sor btsugs
pa ni/ dge 'dun sgang pa dang / tshogs mo che pa zhes zer la/ de gnyis las mched pa bye ma rdzing bu dang / chos lung pa zhes zer te jo gdan tshogs sde bzhi zhes grags
so/des na thang po cher rtsis pa'i me mo yos lo ni/ pan chen gyi drug cu rtsa gsum pa yin la/ re gsum po de dang / pan chen 'khrungs gong gi/ stong drug brgya go gnyis po
bsres pas/ stong dang bdun brgya dang lnga 'byung ba la khrul pa med pa'i phyir ro/

on kyang pan chen shing glang la bltams nas/ go dgu la 'das pa'i lo de ni/ chu mo yos kyi lo yin pas/ khro los/ bya lo sgrog zla'i dkar phyogs kyi zhes sogs bshad pa ni yi
ge ma dag pa'o zhes khas blangs dgos te/ gzhan du na kha che pan chen gyi bstan rtsis dang 'gal ba'i phyir ro/mdor na kha che pan chen gyis bod du lo bcu gcig bzhugs/ mdo
sngags kyi bstan pa la phan che/ sa panDi ta dang byang rdor gnyis la bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa gnang / shangs pa jo gdan dang / seng ge zil gnon la me tog 'phreng rgyud
sogs rgyas par gnang / 'dul ba stod smad gnyis kyi steng du/ 'dul ba'i brgyud pa zur pa zhig kyang spel/ slob bu mang du byung yang sa panDi ta kho na sras kyi dam par mdzad/de
yang 'dul ba smad 'dul ba'i sdom brgyud ni/ thub dbang / shA ri'i bu/ sras sgra gcan zin/ bram ze sgra gcan zin/ klu sgrub/ legs ldan byed/ dpal sbas/ ye shes snying
po/ zhi ba 'tsho/ dba' ratna/ gtsang rab gsal/ bla chen dgongs pa rab gsal/ klu mes tshul khrims shes rab sogs yin la/ stod 'dul ba'i sdom brgyud ni/ dharma pA la/ pradznya
pA la/ zhang zhung rgyal she/ dpal 'byor shes rab/ zhing mo che ba byang chub seng ge/ yang rtse ba rdo rje seng ge/ stag pa padma g.yung drung / rtsis 'dul thugs
rje byang chub/ bde ba can pa shAkya byang chub/ kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ byang chub seng ge/ byang chub bzang po/ blo gros rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan bla ma/ mdog lho pa mkhas
chen kun dga' dpal bzang po/ red mda' ba sogs so/

mkhan brgyud gsar pa'i sdom brgyud ni/ ston pa shA ri'i bu/ sgra gcan zin gnyis/ klu sgrub/ gu na ma ti ste yon tan blo gros/ ratna ma ti ste dkon mchog blo gros/ shrI dharma
pA la ste dpal ldan chos skyong / gu na sA ga ra ste yon tan rgya mtsho/ dharma pA la ste chos kyis skyong ba/ ka a (u ka) ra gupta ste zhi 'byung sbas pa/ pan chen shAkya
shrI/ sa pan rnams so/ stod 'dul ba'i dharma pA la yan gyi sdom brgyud gsal bar bris pa mi snang /yang stod 'dul ba'i dharma pA la dang mkhan brgyud gsar ma'i dharma
pA la gnyis don gcig na klu sgrub nas brgyud tshul 'dra mod/ cung zad thog mi mtshungs pa 'dra'o/des na da lta'i shing pho byi lo 'di kha chen pan chen bod du byon pa'i
shing byi nas blo sum stong sum brgya lnga bcu rtsa gcig lon pa'i lo yin no/sum stong sum brgya dang zhe bzhi 'das pa'i zhe lnga pa chu pho sprel spyi lo 1212 lo/ stag sde
ba seng ge rgyal mtshan mdog pha ri lung du byon/ bo dong rin rtse'i zhabs la btugs/ lo gya gsum bzhugs/snga tshar gyi bu chen shong rdo rje rgyal mtshan dang / shong blo
gros brtan pa ste sku mched gnyis/ gcen gyis skyes rab dpag bsam 'khri shing dang / snyan ngag me long / sgra tsandra pa sogs sngar ma 'gyur ba'i chos mang po bsgyur/sku
mched de gnyis kyi slob ma ni mang mkhar khra tshang pa mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ de'i slob ma dpang lo ste lo tsA ba de bzhi sgra dang snyan ngag sogs la bka' drin
che ba yin/rgya gar gyi kha che blo brtan ni blo brtan dang po yin la/ shong blo brtan

dang / dpang blo brtan la blo brtan gnyis pa dang gsum pa zhes grags/ blo brtan bzhi pa ni/ tshig?chig gter gyi 'grel pa mdzad pa po de yin no/dpang los lo bcu gsum pa nas/
mdog tsha snar stag sde ba seng rgyal zhi bar gshegs kyi bar lo bcu dgu pa'i bar bsten zer bas/ stag sde ba'i phyi tshar gyi slob ma yin la/ stag sde pa ni tshogs sgom pa
las lo gnyis kyis gzhon no/sum stong sum brgya dang zhe lnga 'das pa'i zhe drug pa chu mo bya spyi lo 1213 yang dgon pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la stod lho'i shrI lung
par bltams/bla ma'i mchog ni/ rgod tshang pa/ sa pan/ ko brag pa/ 'bri khung spyan snga rin chen dang bzhi/slob ma'i mchog ni/ lo ras chos skyong dpal dang / dar ma rgyal
mtshan gnyis/ spyan snga rin ldan dang / zur pa rin chen dpal gnyis te bzhi'o/zur phug pa'i thugs sras ni/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ste/ yang dgon pa'i sku
skye ru byed do/ yang dgon pa'i zhe drug sa rta lo nam mthongs kyi tshes bcu dgu la gshegs so/sum stong sum brgya dang nga bdun 'das pa'i nga brgyad pa shing mo bya spyi
lo 1225 la nam ring pa sras bde legs rgyal mtshan las stod bya rog tshang du bltams/ nyer gnyis pa rta lo rgod tshang pa'i drung du byon/ de nas bcu gsum pa sa mo lug
la ne ring btab/ de nas lo sum cu rtsa gnyis 'gro don

mdzad de/ nga bdun pa sbrul lo dbyug zla ba'i nyer dgu'i srod la gshegs so/thugs kyi sras ni dbon kun dga' rdo rje dang / mkhan po sher grags so/ nam ring pa ni nyan chen pa
las lo gsum gyis gzhon/sum stong sum brgya dang re gnyis 'das pa'i re gsum pa lcags pho stag spyi lo 1230la grub thob u rgyan rin chen dpal ba lho nas lhums su (lung du)
byon/ bcu drug pa la rgod tshang pa las dge bsnyen mdzad/ bo dong rin rtse/ bcom ldan ral gri/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal sogs la mdo phyogs gsan/ go lung pa'i gcung po yin/
bo dong rin chen rtse las bsnyen rdzogs rgod tshang pa la gdams pa gsan pas sgro 'dogs chod/ shrI rdo rje rnal 'byor mas pu ti gcig gnang ba mid pas bka' mdo rgyud la
thogs pa med/ yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i u rgyan sogs dgu ru byon/ dgung lo go gnyis pa lcags mo bya lo zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes nyi shu la gshegs so/slob ma'i mchog/ karma
rang byung rdo rje/ grub thob tsha byung ba/ rtogs ldan g.yag mgo ba/ rtogs ldan zla seng dang bzhi'o/rtogs ldan tsha byung bas sbu tra nas lha sar nyin re la phebs/ rgya
khab brgya dus re la gsol nas ba spu'i bu gar dus gcig la 'don/ rtogs ldan zla seng sku 'da' khar bu ston rin po ches gsol ba btab ste lo gsum bzhugs zer ro/des na da lta'i
shing byi 'di/ yang dgon pa'i chu bya nas sum brgya dang gnyis pa/ nam ring ba'i shing bya nas sum brgya dang bzhi bcu pa/ u rgyan pas lcags stag nas sum brgya dang so
lnga pa lags so/

sum stong sum brgya dang re 'dun 'das pa'i re brgyad pa shing mo lug spyi lo 1235 'phags pa rin po che byon/ drug pa'i tshe/ chos rje sa pan gyi phyag phyir skyid grong du
byon zer/ bcu pa la cung phyag na dang bcas chos kyi rje gong la phebs pa'i zhabs phyir thegs/ dbus su chos rje sa pan gyis mkhan po/ zul phu ba'i na bza' 'phred gsol gyis
slob dpon bgyis te rab tu byung / bcu gnyis pa la rgyal po'i pho brang chen por phyab phebs/ bcu bdun yan la lung rtogs gyi yon tan phul du phyin/ de'i tshe chos rje sa
pan gyis bstan pa'i khur chen po nyid phyag tu gtad/ dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/ bco brgyad pa la chos rje'i dgongs rdzogs sogs legs par bsgrubs/ bcu dgu lon pa chu mo glang
gi lo/ hor rgyal po se chen gan gyis pho brang ta tur spyan drangs/ lugs kyi mdzad pas rgyal po'i thugs rab tu phrogs te/ rgyal pos zhus pa'i ngor/ rgyal pos gtsos pa'i
skal ldan gyi gdul bya lnga phrag la dgyes pa rdo rje'i smin byed kyi dbang bskur/ ti shri'i mtshan gsol/ dbang yon du bod khri skor bcu gsum phul/khri skor bcu gsum ni/
lho byang gnyis/ chu zhal gnyis/ lha shangs gnyis te gtsang la drug/ g.ya' phag gnyis/ rgya tshal gnyis/ 'bri stag gnyis te dbus la drug/ yar 'brog khri skor dang bcu gsum
yin la/ 'di nas bzung bod khams thams cad dpal ldan sa skya pas lugs gnyis kyis bskyangs so/de nas lo nyer gnyis pa la rgya hor yul gyi mtshams su/ mkhan po snye thang
pa grags pa seng ge/ las slob jo gdan bsod nams rgyal mtshan/

gsang sde [ston] yar lung pa byang chub rgyal mtshan sogs las bsnyen par rdzogs/ slar so gcig pa shing mo glang la dpal ldan sa skyar phebs/de'i tshe bod dbus gtsang gi dge
ba'i bshes gnyen che rgu thams cad kyis mdo khams su bsu ba ser sbreng la phebs/ shong rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis bstod pa spel legs kyi snyan ngag phul/ 'bel ba'i gtam gyis
bka' mchid mchog tu stsal/ de dag kun gyi nang nas la stod pa gangs shAkya bshes gnyen dang / dbus kyi 'bre'u rin po che gnyis la mchog tu dgyes pa thob ces kyang zer/
dbus gtsang khams gsum chos dang zang zing gis 'byor pas bde ba la bkod/slar so gsum pa la gong mas spyan 'dren gyi gser yig pa slebs pas shar la phebs/ de'i tshe gsol
gzim mchod gsum/ 'jal yig mdzod gsum/ thab 'dren gdan gsum/ rta skya gnyis/ mdzo khyi gnyis te las tshan bcu gsum gyi bkod pa gnang /bcom ral gyis/ sangs rgyas bstan pa bka'
phyag sprin gyis bsgrib/ ces sogs kyi zur za'i zhu mchid phul/ bstan pa 'phel 'grib 'byung ba rgyal bas gsungs// zhes sogs kyi bka' mchid stsal/so bzhi pa sa pho 'brug
la dpon chen shAkya bzang pos khri skor bcu gsum bskul te lha khang chen mo'i gzhi bting / rgyal po'i pho brang du phebs/ dbang yon du rgya'i yur ma chod/ bod chol kha
gsum phul/chol kha gsum ni/ dbus gtsang chos kyi chol kha/ mdo stod gon gyo mi'i chol kha/mdo smad gling kha rta'i chol kha zer/ 'ga' zhig/ mang yul

mtsho/ gu ge g.ya'/ pu rangs gangs kyis bskor bas stod mnga' ris skor gsum chol kha gcig/ gtsang la g.yas ru dang g.yon ru gnyis/ dbus la sbu ru dang g.yo ru gnyis te bar dbus
gtsang ru bzhi chol kha gcig/ tsha ba sgang / po 'bor sgang / rmar khams sgang ste mdo khams sgang gsum chol kha gcig yin zer ro/slar zhe gcig pa dpal ldan sa skyar phyab
phebs/ zhe gsum pa me mo glang la/ rgyal po jin gyim gyis sbyin bdag mdzad de/ gtsang chu mig ring mor dge 'dun khri phrag bdun la gser ja gos dar sogs kyis mchod nas
chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te/ zhe drug pa 'brug lo zla ba bcu pa'i nyer gnyis la bde bar gshegs so/'di nyid la slob ma'i mchog man ngag gi bka' babs zhang dkon mchog dpal
dang / dge slong kun blo gnyis/ rgyud kyi bka' babs dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal dang / dga' ldan pa kun bsod gnyis/ mgon po'i bka' babs dam pa kun dga' grags/ mnyes pa'i
mchod g.yog ti shri grags 'od/ bla chen sangs rgyas sras/ ring phug pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ sro lung pa kun smon dang bzhi'o/nus pa'i bdag nyid gcung phyag na rdo rje dang
/ rgyal bu jin kim gnyis so/gzhan yang che ba'i bdag nyid shar pa dus 'khor ba ye shes rin chen/ shar pa kun dga' seng ge/ shar pa 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ khang gsar ti shri sangs rgyas dpal/ gnyan tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/

cha gan dbang phyug mtshan dang drug go/de dag las 'gro mgon phyag na sa mo phag spyi lo 1239 la mdog gad ler byon/ lo drug pa la gong la byon/ brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mthar
phyin/ nyer lnga pa la bod du phebs/ nyer dgu pa yos lo zla ba bdun pa'i tshes gnyis la dgu rum du gshegs so/ 'di 'phags pa las lo bzhis gzhon/sum stong sum brgya don
gnyis 'das pa'i don gsum pa lcags pho khyi (byi)spyi lo 1250lo zhang dkon mchog dpal ra sa mtshal gung du byon/ shar pa sher 'byung la rab tu byung / brag sram du bo dong
rin chen brtson 'grus rdo rje la phar tshad sogs sbyangs/ tshogs sgom pa dang ra nyis pa chen po sogs kyang bsten/ ra ma la dge slong kun blo dang / gnyis 'phags pa rin
po che bsu ba la byon/ rang lo so lnga pa shing byi'i lo 'phags pa dang mdo khams gtso mdor mjal/ lo re brgyad bzhugs/sum stong sum brgya dang don 'dun 'das pa'i don brgyad
pa shing mo sbrul spyi lo 1245la ti shri grags 'od stag sde ra lung du byon/ ti shri lo bcu gnyis mdzad/ 'phags pa las lo lngas gzhon/ lo nga brgyad bzhugs des na da lta'i
shing byi 'di 'phags pa rin po che byon nas sum brgya dang nyer gnyis 'das pa'i nyer bzhi pa lags so/mdor na 'gro ba'i mgon po 'phags pa rin po ches bcu dgu bzhes pa
chu mo glang la hor se chen rgyal po'i ti shri thob pa nas/ theg chen chos rje kun dga' bkra shis kyis rang lo re lnga pa chu mo sbrul la rgya nag tA ming rgyal chen gyi

ti shri thob pa'i bar lo grangs brgya dang drug cu re gcig gi bar du dpal sa skya pa'i gdung rgyud rim pas/ rgya hor gyi rgyal po'i ti shri thob pa rim can du byung ba kho
na yin la de yang dpal ldan sa skya panDi tas rgyal po go dan gyi spyi bor dbang gi cod pan bcings pa'i bka' drin yin mod/ ti shri'i mtshan ni ma gsol te de'i tshe rgyal
po go dan rgyal srid kyi khur bor nas/ rang gi dbon po se chen rgyal po rgyal sar bton zin pa nyid kyis so/de ltar na chos rje khu dbon gnyis kyi bka' drin las bod khams
thams cad dmag khral las gsum las bton te/ lo grangs brgya lhag tsam zhig gi bar du rgyal srid chos bzhin du bde bar bskyangs pa ni/ gang la gang 'dul gyi dbang gis skal
ldan gyi gdul bya la bde ba'i ngal gso chen po thob pa yin no/deb sngon las/ dpal ldan sa skya pas lo grangs bdun cu rtsa lnga'i bar du khri skor bcu gsum bdag mdzad nas
sa mo glang nas ta'i si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan gyis khri skor bcu gsum bdag mdzad pa yin no zhes bshad la/ de la nges pa'i gtan tshigs yod na sa mo glang de 'phags pa
rin po che ti shri mdzad pa'i chu mo glang nas go drug 'das pa'i go bdun pa theg chen chos rje bltams pa'i lo de yin par gdon mi za mod/ ji ltar bden kho bos da dung dpyad
par bya'o/sum stong sum brgya dang go bzhi 'das pa'i go lnga pa chu pho khyi spyi lo 1262 lo bla ma bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal bltams/ mang mkhar khab smad du yab
slob dpon ye 'byung nyer lnga'i sras yin/ bcu drug pa

la 'phags pa dang mjal/ mi res pus mo la babs yon tan slob gsungs/ bcu dgu pa la 'phags pa zhi bar gshegs/ nyer gcig pa la gong la byon/ snyan sgra'i (dgra'i) stabs kyis so
lnga pa'i bar sman tshe'i yul'byon dgos pa shar/ ti shri grags 'od khu dbon gyis legs pa'i mtshams sbyar/ so drug pa la 'phags pa ti shri'i dbon po yin nges su 'dug pas
gdung rgyud spel dgos kyi rgyal po'i lung bud/ so bdun pa sa pho khyi la sa skyar phebs/ chos dang 'jig rten gyi 'byor pas gdan sa bskyangs/ re gsum pa shing pho byi ba la
zhi bar gshegs so/'di nyid la sras kun dril bco lnga tsam zhig byon par snang yang / yongs grags sras dgu ni/ ti shri kun blo yab so brgyad pa sa mo phag la byon bcu gcig
pa la ti shri thob/ nyer bzhi pa khyi lo bod du bsnyen rdzogs la byon/ nyer drug pa la yab gshegs/ sku mched rnams la bla brang so sor bgos/ nyer dgu la gong du gshegs
zer/mkhas btsun pa sku mched la bzhi thog bla brang pa zhes zer te/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa yab zhe bzhi pa sbrul lor bltams/ so dgu la gshegs/gcung gu shri nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan yab gshegs pa'i byi lo'am/ yang na chu mo byi lo pa chos rje bla ma dang dgung mnyam yin zer/ nyer gsum pa la gshegs so/ti shri kun dga' legs 'byung sku
mched la lha khang bla brang pa zer te/ gcen ti shri kun dga' legs 'byung yab zhe bdun pa sa pho sprel lor byon/

de'i gcung ti shri kun dga' rgyal mtshan yab zhe dgu pa lcags phyo khyi lor byon/ sa'i len dbang kun dga' legs pa lcam sring la dus mchod bla brang pa zer/ 'di ti shri kun
dga' legs dang dgung mnyam yin no/ta dbon kun dga' nyi ma sku mched gsum la rin chen sgang bla brang [pa] zer te/ ta dbon kun nyi'i gcung 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan
ti shri kun rgyal dang dgung mnyam yin/ so bzhi pa zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu gcig la gshegs so/gcung chos rje bla ma yab nga gcig pa chu pho byi lor byon/ re bzhi pa/
nyer lnga la gshegs so/ des na da lta'i shing byi 'di bdag nyid chen po byon pa'i khyi lo nas sum brgya dang gsum du sleb pa lags so/mnyam med grags rgyal 'di bas lo gcig
gis gzhon lo gya lnga bzhugs zer/kha che pan chen bod du byon pa'i shing pho byi spyi lo 1204lor karma paka shi byon/ sa pan las lo nyer gnyis kyis gzhon/ dus gsum mkhyen
pa'i slob ma pom brag pa'i zhabs la gtugs/ hor rgyal pos kyang spyan drangs/ mes bsregs/ chu la bskyur/ mtshon gyis btab kyang gnod pa ma byung bas zhabs tog byas zer/
brgyad cu pa lug lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes gsum la gshegs so/'di ni sa ra ha'i sprul pa yin la/ 'di sku skye brgyud spel du byon pa ni/ karma rang byung rdo rje/ rol pa'i
rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa/ mthong

ba don ldan/ chos grags rgya mtsho/ mi bskyoed rdo rje ste/ karma paka shi nas mi bskyod rdo rje'i bar bdun byon zin pa la/ dus gsum mkhyen pa ni/ skal bzang gi sangs rgyas
stong gi drug pa seng ge'i rnam 'phrul yin par bshad la/ karma paka shi ni/ sa ra ha pa'i rnam 'phrul du bshad kyi/ dus gsum mkhyen pa'i sku skye yin zhes kyang ma bshad
pas/ karma zhwa nag pa zhes grags pa'i thog ma ni karma paka shi nas ngos 'dzin dgos par sems la 'on kyang karma pa zhes pa'i mtshan 'dogs pa ni dus gsum mkhyen pas/ smad
du kam po gnas nang / bar du karma lha steng / stod du mtshur phu'i dgon pa btab nas karma pa zhes mtshan 'dogs par gsal bas/ dus gsum mkhyen pa la karma pa zhes pa'i sgra
bshad du yod pa tsam zhig yin no snyam du kho bos sems so/de lta bu'i karma paka shi'i slob ma ni/ rje u rgyan pa/ karma zhwa dmar can/ zhwa ser can/ zhwa khra can la
sogs pa'o/sprul sku zhwa dmar ba tshul khrims dpal ni me pho byi lor bltams/ til lo pa'i slob ma khol po dga' zhes pa'i sku skye yin zer ro/sa bcad bzhi pa sum stong bzhi
brgya pa'i skabs su byon pa ni/ bdag nyid chen po dharma pA la/ dpang lo/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bu dol la sogs pa'i mkhas pa rnams te/ de yang sum stong bzhi brgya 'das
nas nyag ma gcig gi steng du sleb pa sa pho 'brug spyi lo 1268lor/ 'gro mgon phyag na'i sras dharma pA la bltams/ bcu gsum pa la sa skya'i gdan sa mdzad/ de'i lor 'phags
pa zhi bar gshegs/ nang rten lha chen dpal 'bar dang /

'phags pa'i sku 'dra 'bum thob bcu gsum zhes grags pa rnams bzhengs/ bcu bzhi pa la gong la byon/ ti shri mdzad/ nyi shu pa la mdo khams pa tri mandal zhes par tshes bco brgyad
la gshegs so/ des na shing byi 'di dharma pA la'i sa pho 'brug nas nyis brgya go bdun pa yin/ sa pho 'brug de ni/ 'phags pas lha khang chen mo bzhengs pa'i lo yin te
dpal ldan sa skya btab nas lo brgya dang go drug pa sa pho 'brug la lha khang chen mo'i 'gram bting zhes 'byung ba yin no/sum stong bzhi brgya dang nyag brgyad 'das pa'i
(nyag dgu) me pho byi spyi lo 1276 lo dpang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa las stod gyam du byon khong gis lo lnga lon pa'i tshe 'phags pa rin po che dag pa'i hing du gshegs/
yum snga mor gshegs nas lug gi 'o mas gsos pas lu gu zhes par grags/ kho bo ba'i 'o mas gsos na legs pa la lug gi 'o mas gsos pas blo gros kyi phyed 'grib ces gsungs/
lo bdun pa la mkhan chen gser khang pa dang me ston 'dul 'dzin las rab tu byung / bcu gcig pa la mdo rtsa rdzogs par bzung / bcu gsum pa la mdog tsha snar stag sde seng rgyal
lo bcu dgu pa'i bar du bsten/ bcu dgu pa la stag sde pa gshegs nas mang mkhar khra tshang du lo tsA ba mchog ldan la dus 'khor sogs gsan/ gzhan yang / stag sde ti phug
gi mkhan po shes rab dpal dang / sa skya'i 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa dang / 'jam skya dang / rong pa shes rab seng ge sogs kyi zhabs pad bsten/ rong pa sher seng 'di ni
rong pa sga lo'i sras te lcags mo phag lo pa yin/ ti shri grags 'od las lo drug gis gzhon/ dpang lo las nyer lngas bgres/ slob

ma yang dpang lo/ dpal ldan seng ge/ skyi ston grags rgyal sogs mang du byung / lo yang re lnga bzhugs zer ba de'o/ nyi shu pa la sngar gyi mkhan slob las bsnyen par rdzogs/
nyer gcig pa la bal por byon sgra snyan ngag la sbyangs/ spyir bal por lan bdun byon/ so gnyis pa la gung thang gnas po cher chos gzhi btsugs/ gung thang bde blo sogs slob
bu mang du byon/dpang lo 'di ni khong rang bzhugs dus kyi mkhas pa/ bu dol/ rgyal sras pa/ ma ti pan chen/ kun spangs chos grags dpal/ 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan
sku mched gnyis/ ne ring pa 'jam dbyangs mtshan can sogs mkhas grub thams cad kyis tshur zhabs la btud/ mkhas pa'i grags pa shin tu che/ bo dong e'i gdan sar/ rgyal sras
rin po ches zhu phul bas/ gu ru thogs med thos pa'i gtam la snyan/ nyid kyi zhal nas legs par ma gtogs nyes par bshad pa ga la srid/ kho bo mkhan po chen po stag sde pa
seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis kyang ma thob pa'i gdan sa yin pas de ring rang la 'gro/ 'gyur na mi 'dod/ da lta rang 'gro zhes gsungs pa nas drug cu rtsa gcig lon pa'i tshe/
bo dong e pan chen 'bum phrag gsum pa'i gdan seng ge'i khri la 'khod/rgyud 'dzin gyi sras rang nyid kyi dbon po lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo zhes grags pa de yin la dgung
lo drug cu rtsa bdun pa chu pho rta lo nag pa zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bcu gsum la bo dong er dag pa'i zhing du gshegs so/sum stong bzhi brgya dang nyag dgu 'das pa'i bcu
pa me me glang spyi lo 1277 la brag phug pa bsod nams dpal bltams/ dpang lo las

gcig gis gzhon/ lo don bdun bzhugs/slob bu mang du byung yang gtso bo chos rje bla ma/ brag phug pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ brag phug pa blo gros bstan pa/ ka bcu pa gzhon
nu sing ge dang bzhi'o/brag phug pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi slob ma ni/ sa skya bu ston dbang phyug rgyal po/ g.yag sde ba nam mkha' bsod nams/ mdo khams gtso mdo dpal
'bar gyi thim chu ba blo gros dkar po ste blo bzang dkar por grags pa dang gsum/blo bzang dkar po'i slob ma ni/ gon gyi ye shes dpal yin la/ gon gyi slob ma ni khams kyi
chab la kha ba blo bzang dkar mo dang / mkhan chen g.yag pa sogs yin zhing / blo bzang dkar mo la/ lam 'bras pa blo bzang du grags pa dang / pan chen bo dong pa sogs kyis
gsan no/ri khrod pa blo brtan ni/ me pho 'brug lo pa ste/ chos rje bla ma las lo bzhis gzhon no/sum stong bzhi brgya bcu bzhi pa lcags mo sbrul spyi lo 1281 lor lam 'bras
pa ye shes dpal mdo khams su byon/ lo bcu bzhi pa la nyan chen po'i bu chen blo gros dkar po la 'khrid dang gdams pa gsan/ zha lu bu ston la theg chen sems skyed gsan/
sa skyar gzhung rgyas pa mkhan chen dbang phyug dpal la rnam rig gsan/ sa skyar gzhung rgyas pa mkhan chen dbang phyug dpal la rnam rig gsan/ kun spangs chos grags dpal
la sbyor drug gsan/ na bza' ba lo bcu gnyis bsten ten gsung ngag sogs gsan/ bla ma gu ru dbang phyug brtson 'grus la ni gu sogs gsan/ 'khon bla chen kun

dga' rgyal mtshan pa'i sras gung pa bkra shis dbang bzang po la dmar po skor gsum sogs gsan/ lo lnga bcu nas gya lnga'i bar du gzhan don kho na mdzad/slob ma'i mchog blo bzang
dkar mo/ mkhan chen g.yag mo sogs te/ gya lnga pa sbrul lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nyer gnyis la 'jam sa lha sdings su gshegs so/sum stong bzhi brgya bco lnga (drug) 'das
pa'i bcu drug (bdun) pa shing pho sprel spyi lo 1284lor karma pa rang byung rdo rje mnga' ris su byon/ lo gsum par ming yongs su grags pa'i karma pa yin zhwa nag khyer
shog gsungs/ rang byung rdo rje zhes pa karma paka shi'i gsang mtshan yin zer/ mdo sde ma gzigs par skyes rabs tsam ci yin zhus pas/ karma paka shi'i dus khams kyi ra ba
sgang du tshar gcig bltas gsungs/ 'dis hor tho han thi mur gyi ti shri mdzad zer bas/ spyir tho han thi mur gyis lo nyer lnga rgyal srid mdzad pa'i stod la ti shri kun rgyal
gyis ti shri mdzad/ bar skabs su bla chen bsod blos mdzad/ mjug tu ti shri med pa lo brgyad byung zer ba'i tho han gyi sku tshe'i stod ti shri kun rgyal dang thog mtshungs
tsam du ti shri mdzad par mngon te/ rang byung rdo rje ti shri kun rgyal las lo nyer drug gis bgres pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ gang na'ang dgung lo nga drug pa bya khra
tshes bcu bzhi la rgya nag pho brang la gshegs so/sum stong bzhi brgya dang nyer gsum 'das pa'i nyer bzhi pa lcags mo yos spyi lo 1291la gnyag phu pa bsod nams dbang phyug
mus gling skyar byon/ bcu gcig pa la mkhan po shAkya mgon dang slob dpon 'od zer rtse mo

las rab tu byung / mdog stod du mkhan chen kun rgyal las 'dul ba/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal dang / slob dpon shes rab ral gri sogs las mdo phyogs gsan/ bcu dgu pa la mkhan
chen chu bzang pa dang / slob dpon 'od zer rtse mo las bsnyen par rdzogs/ bshol gyis kha bskang ba sogs nas nyi shur sleb zin pa las ma 'das/ nyan chen pa las lam 'bras
sogs gsan/ g.ya' gdung rings su bsam gtan la bzhugs pa'i tshe/ sbyin bdag rnams kyis gnyag phu btab/ sbyin bdag dang gzhi bdag mched gsum dang bcas pas gnyag phu phul/ bshad
sgrub kyi 'phrin las mchog tu rgyas/ mthar phag lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes nyi shu la gshegs so/ 'di karma rang byung rdo rje las lo lngas gzhon zhing / bu ston las gcig
gis bgres so/sum stong bzhi brgya dang nyer gnyis 'das pa'i nyer gsum pa lcags pho stag spyi lo 1290la/ zha lu bu ston rin chen grub shab smad sgom gnas su byon/ dpang
lo las lo bcu bzhis gzhon/ kun mkhyen dol bu las lo gnyis kyis bgres/ rgyal sras thogs med las lngas bgres so/ lo bdun pa la khro phu rin po che sems dpa' chen po bsod nams
seng ge'i drung du sems bskyed dang brgyad pa la smin byed kyi dbang zab mo nod/ khro phu sems dpa' chen po de ni/ kha rag sgom chung pa'i bar srid gzhan don du skye ba
tshol ba na/ khro los dag pa'i spyan ras kyis gzigs te/ rigs kyi sras su bskrun pa yin zer/ bco brgyad lon pa'i tshe mkhan po rin po che seng ge dpal dang slob dpon tshad
ma'i skyes bu las rab tu byung / mkhas mchog tshad ma'i skyes bu/ rigs pa'i thigs pa/ bsod nams mgon po zhes mtshan gsum dang ldan pa

de'i drung du phar tshad sogs la sbyangs/ nyer gcig pa la yab dang lhan cig tu dbus gtsang gnyis su grwa skor mdzad/ dbus nas mkhas pa shAkya gzhon nu dang / kha rag byang
gzhon/ gtsang nas mkhas pa dpal ldan seng ge dang / 'jam skya sogs lung rigs kyis btul bas pha ston bu ston du grags/ nyer gsum pa la mkhan chen bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon
nu dang / slob dpon bsod nams grags pa las bsnyen par rdzogs/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan pa spel/ thar pa lo tsA ba la sgra snyan ngag/ bla ma 'phags 'od las gsang
'dus/ rong pa sher seng gi dbon po rdo rje rgyal mtshan la dus 'khor sogs gsan/ sum cu pa la/ phar phyin lung snying mdzad/ so gcig pa la zhwa lu'i 'dzin skyong gnang
/ zhwa lu ri phug btab/ ri phug tu tshogs pa brgya drug cu dang / zhwa lur sum stong brgyad brgya re 'dus/ re bdun pa la sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam rgyal la zhwa lu'i gdan
sa gtad/ ri phug tu gdan phab/ bka' 'bum po ti so gsum bzhugs/ don lnga pa shing pho 'brug zla ba drug pa'i nyer gcig la gshegs so/'di la slob bu shin tu mang yang /
gtso bo sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam rgyal/ byang pa dkon mchog grags/ gong gsum bde chen chos kyi mgon po/ yo ga ba rin bzang / yo ga ba tshe dbang / khyung po lhas pa sogs
so/ chos rje bla ma/ rgyal sras pa/ bu ston sogs ni phar slob tshur slob yin no/des na da lta'i shing byi 'di/ dpang lo'i me pho byi ba nas nyer brgya dang gya brgyad
pa/ na bza' brag phug pas me glang mas nyis brgya dang gya bdun pa/ rang byung rdo rje'i shing spre nas nyis brgya gya gcig pa/ bu ston gyi lcags pho

stag nas nyis brgya dang don lngar slebs pa lags so/ sum stong bzhi brgya dang nyer bzhi 'das pa'i nyer lnga pa chu pho 'brug spyi lo 1292la kun mkhyen dol bu shes rab rgyal
mtshan/ mnga' ris dol bu'i ban tshan du byon/ bcu gsum pa la skye stongs su mkhan po tshul khrims snying po las rab tu byung / der skyi ston 'jam dbyangs grags rgyal byon
pa la rdo rje phreng ba bslabs/ bco brgyad pa la skyi ston grags blo phar phebs pa la tshad bsdus sbyangs/ de nas skyi ston pa sa skyar phebs te slar dpal ldan sa skyar
skyi ston shAka 'bum dang skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan te khu dbon de gnyis kyi drung du mdo phyogs la sbyangs/ nyer gsum pa la bka' bzhi'i steng du spyod 'jug bsnan
te po ti lnga la grwa skor mdzad de/ nyer lnga pa la chos lung mkhan po bsod grags las bsnyen par rdzogs/ so gcig pa la jo nang du yon tan rgya mtsho'i zhabs pad bsten/
so lnga pa de'i gdan seng ge'i khri la zhabs pad brten/ so dgu pa la mchod rten chen po bzhengs/ lo phyed dang bzhi la grub/ nyams rtogs kyi mdzad rdol/ lo bcu gsum du jo
nang gi seng ge'i khri la 'khod de chos gsungs pas spyir bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa dang / khyad par gzhan stong pa zhes phyogs kun tu snyan pa'i ba dan g.yos/ nyid kyi zhe
bdun pa sa pho stag lor/ lo tsA ba blo gros dpal gdan sar bskos/ rta lor lo tsA ba gshegs te nyid kyi re gsum pa shing pho rta lor phyogs rgyal ba gdan sar bskos/ bdun
cu pa la nub chos lung du chos rje bla ma dang mjal bka' bsdu bzhi pa sogs gnang / slar bdun cu pa lcags mo glang zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes drug la zhi bar gshegs/

des na rje 'di karma rang byung rdo rje dang mjal te rang stong pa'i grub mtha' bzung bas/ karma pas phyis gzhan stong par 'gyur bar lung bstan zer/ spyir gzhan stong pa'i
lugs thog mar karma rang byung rdo rjes bzung bar sems/ jo nang du ni kun mkhyen chen po man chad gzhan stong par song ba yin no/'on kyang jo nang thog mar 'debs pa po ni/
jo nang kun spangs zhang thugs rje brtson 'grus shes rab grags pa de yin te/ chu mo yos kyi lo byang mdog stod ngab byar spangs khang du byon/ 'phags pa rin po che las
lo brgyad kyis gzhon/ bar pa 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa rin chen rgyal mtshan la lam 'bras gsan/ chos sku 'od zer la sbyor drug sogs gsan/ rkyang 'dur du 'chad nyan yang mdzad/
phyis 'chad nyan bskyungs te sgom la zhugs te kun spangs par grags slar jo nang gi dgon pa btang / bshad sgrub spel mar gnang bas kun spangs bu bzhir grags pa byon
te/ byang sems rgyal po ye shes/ las stod pa dbang rgyal/ mun me brag kha ba grags pa seng ge/ ston pa kun rgyal rnams so/ las stod dbang rgyal dang / jo nang kun spangs
ni lam 'bras bsres brgyud kyi skabs su mtshan smos pa de yang yin no/brag kha ba grags pa seng ge ni/ las stod byang gi rgyal sde thang dkar byon/ khro phu sems dpa' chen
po dang / bu ston seng ge 'od las bsnyen par rdzogs/ sa skyar phya rub seng ge dpal la rnam 'grel dang / jo nang kun spangs pa dang / byang sems rgyal ye la sbyor drug sogs
gsan/ lo gya dgu thug bzhugs/

slob ma yang chos rje bla ma dang / ka bcu pa gzhon seng sogs byon zer/byang sems rgyal ye'i slob ma ni/ mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho ste mdog gi spen par byon/ chung ngu
nas sa skyar 'jam dbyangs pa la sogs pa bsten/ phyis jo nang du sbyor drug gsan nas gdan sa bskyangs/de'i slob ma ni kun mkhyen chen po zhes bshad zin la/ kun mkhyen dol
bu bas lo bdun cu bzhugs/slob ma'i mchog kun spangs chos grags dpal/ lo tsA ba blo gros dpal/ phyogs las rnam rgyal/ sa bzang ma ti pan chen te sras kyi gtso bo bzhi'o/gzhan
yang 'jam dbyangs chos dpal mgon po/ g.yag sde pan chen/ 'jam sngon 'jam sgeg/ snar thang pa mchims blo bzang grags pa/ chos lung mkhan po bsod nams bzang po dang grags
pa rgyal mtshan gnyis/ bla brang pa bzang po dpal/ thang chen pa kun dga' 'bum sogs mang du yod do/kun spangs chos grags dpal ni/ g.yas ru byang gi dpon yon btsun chen
po grags pa dar gyi gcen dpon kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyi sras te/ dpang lo/ dpal ldan seng ge/ bu dol la sogs pa'i mkhas grub mang du bsten/ bzang ldan chos rje 'ga' rong
chud kha chos sde sogs chos grwa btab/ bstan pa'i rgyun la phan pa cher mdzad do/sa bzang ma ti pa ni mdog spang bor du byon/ bzang ldan gyi mkhan po thog ma yang mdzad/
mkhas shing 'phrin las rgya che bar byung ngo/

phyogs las rnam rgyal ni mnga' ris dol por me pho rta la byon/ kun mkhyen dol po las lo bcu bzhis gzhon/ gzhon pa'i dus su dbus chos 'khor gling du gsan sbyongs mdzad/ dbus
gtsang du grwa skor mdzad pa'i zhor la jo nang du kun mkhyen chen po'i zhabs zung bsten/ byang bdag chen tA dben nam mkha' brtan pas/ kun mkhyen dang dpon slob gnyis mnga'
ris su spyan drangs/ chos sde chen po btab/ phar tshad kyi bshad nyan yang dag pa mdzad/ gdan sa mkhan chen bstan rgyal ba la gtad nas rang lo zhe dgu pa la jo mo nang
gi gdan sa mdzad/ lo lnga nas de yang gtad nas dbus la bzhud/ slar se mkhar chung du phebs/ dus 'khor sogs kyi 'chad nyan gnang nas/ sa ga li 'grem pa sum brgya tsam gyi
nang nas/ gsol ja rgyug pa'i chos dpon brgyad cu tsam byung zer ro/jo nang phyogs las pa 'dis dpal ngam rings chos sde'i chos sde bla brang dang 'du khang rnying pa dang
shar nub kyi gra khang la sogs pa btab pas chos sde btab ces grags pa ni/ 'das lo nas sum stong bzhi brgya dang bdun cu rtsa 'dren gyi skabs su yin par sems la/ 'di nyid
chos sde'i mkhan rabs lnga pa yin zhing / 'di nyid kyis mkhan po bsod nams rgyal mtshan la gtad rjes/ slar yang mkhan po mdzad cing de nas mkhan po bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan
la gtad ces mkhan rabs las 'byung / khong gis mkhan po lan gnyis mdzad pa de/ khong pas jo nang gdan sa mdzad rjes yin nam ji ltar yin ma 'tshal/gangs khrod pa grags pa
dpal ni/ chu mo 'brug gi lo sgyer phu rgya

par byon/ kun mkhyen dol bu dang dgung mnyam yin zhing / mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa zhig yin zhing / lam 'bras sa lugs dang zhwa lugs gnyis char bzhugs/de yang sa lugs ni/
la tu (ru )ba dang nyan chen pa gnyis la gtso bor gsan gzhan yang tshogs sgom pa'i dngos slob gnyan (gnyag)snying po rgyal mtshan/ de'i slob ma mang mkhar ba rta lung
bkra shis bzang po/ dza tsha lung pa rgyal mtshan dpal/ bar ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ dge rgan thugs rje bsod nams dang bzhi'i rta lung la'ang thor chags gsan zer/khong
gis zhwa lugs ni/ 'dzin pa rgyal mtshan dpal la gsan pa yin la/ 'dzin pa de la lam 'bras kyi 'khrid lugs mi 'dra ba bco brgyad bzhugs par grags pa'i/ rgan mo lhas pa mkhan
chen byang chub dpal la gsan/ des ko brag pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan la gsan pa yin la/ de lta bu'i gangs khrod pa nas brgyud pa'i gsung ngag ni/ des sa bzang ma ti la gnang
/ des theg chen chos rje la gnang / des 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan la gnang / des bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan nas brgyud de kho bo cag gi
brgyud pa 'di la bzhugs pa yin no/gangs pa 'di nyid kyis dpal ngam rings kyi mkhan po yang lo dgu'i ring mdzad de mkhan rabs gsum pa yin/ mkhan po thog ma ni dpon chen yon
btsun chen pos/ ti shri grags 'od dang / de'i dbon po ti shri sangs rgyas dpal dang / de'i dbon po kun spangs grags pa rgyal mtshan rnams la bka'i nang ba zhus shing /
khu dbon de dag gis mthun pa'i rkyen sbyar nas

stag sde la rgyab tu sku 'khrungs pa'i mkhan po shAkya seng ge spyan drangs nas chos sde chen po thog mar btsugs zhes 'byung bas sum stong bzhi brgya dang nyi shu tsam zhig
'das pa'i tshe dpal ngam rings kyi chos sde thog mar gzhi tshugs pa yin snyam du sems so/ des na kun mkhyen dol bu dang kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa byon pa'i chu pho 'brug
nas lo grangs nyis brgya dang don gnyis 'das pa'i don gsum pa shing pho byi lo 'di yin no zhes khong du chud par bya'o/sum stong bzhi brgya dang nyer bdun 'das pa'i nyer
