brgyad pa shing mo lug spyi lo 1295la rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal lho phul chung du byon/ bcu bzhi pa la bsam gling pa dpal 'bar dang / rin chen dpal bzang gi drung
du rab tu byung / mtshan bzang po'i dpal zhes gsol/ bco lnga pa la bo dong er slob dpon kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa'i drung du mngon pa sogs la sbyangs/ 'jam dbyangs nyi
ma rgyal mtshan pas/ mngon pa nas zang zing med pa'i tshor ba sdug bsngal bshad kyang / zang zing med pa dang / tshor ba sdug bsngal srid pa 'gal bas lan thobs gsungs pa
la/ nyan rang dgra bcom pa la nyon mongs med kyang / snga ma'i las dbang gi tshor ba sdug bsngal 'byung tshul bshad pa'i sgo nas lan mdzad pas/ thogs med bzang po dpal zhes
snyan par grags/ dpang lo bu dol chos rje bla ma la sogs pa'i mkhas grub dam pa bsten nas bcu gu pa la bshad pa'i dga' ston spel/ nyer gcig pa nas 'chad po'i ring lugs
bskyangs/ nyer dgu pa la byang sems rin mgon dang / nam mkha' sangs rgyas sogs las bsnyen par rdzogs/ so gnyis nas zhe gcig gi bar du bla brang rta ra'i gdan sa mdzad/ de
nas e'i chos kyi khrir gsol ba

btab kyang ma gnang ste/ kho bo las ches lhag pa zhig sgrub gsung dpang lo chen po nyid spyan drangs/ byang chub kyi thugs kyis bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa ches lhag par bsgrubs
te re bdun sa glang lor dbus la byon/ ta'i si tu byang rgyal dang mjal tshur zhabs gtugs zer bas/ theg chen chos rje'i bcu gsum lon pa'i si tu ba gshegs pa'i lo de tsam
yin par sems/ gang na'ang don lnga pa lcags phag (sa bya) tshes nyi shu la zhi bar gshegs so/slob ma'i mchog ni/ bu dol chos rje bla ma lo chen byang rtse sogs mtha' yas
shing / gtso bor rgyud 'dzin ni dpal ldan seng ge sogs so/rgyal sras pa bu rin po che las lo bzhi dang / dol bu ba las gsum gyis gzhon zhing / lo chen byang rtse las brgyad
dang / chos rje bla ma las bcu bdun gyis bgres so/sum stong bzhi brgya dang so lnga 'das pa'i so drug pa chu mo yos spyi lo 1303la lo chen byang rtse la stod lho zur
tshor dpang gi lcam mo zhig gi sras su bltams/ bdun pa la dpang lo'i drung du dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa nod/ bcu drug pa la shong lo'i dbon po mkhan chen chos skyong dpal las
dge tshul du bsgrubs/ dpang los mnga' ris gnas po che dang / sa skya sogs su bzhugs pa'i spyan sngar 'khrid de bslab sbyangs mdzad/ dpang los brtag pa mdzad pa'i phyir/
bur rdog mang po bgrongs byas pa bcal nas re re nas blangs shing rtsis pas ma tshang ba med par rtsis 'grig/ 'phrul phugs kyi mdzad pa la dges pa thob ste dkar po nam langs
shes mtshan du gsol/ nyer gnyis pa shing mo glang lor dpal ldan sa skya'i mkhan po 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal

mtshan dang / las kyi slob dpon dpang lo dang gsang ston chos rje bla ma/ grib tshod mkhan chen bsod nams bzang pos bgyis te/ bsnyen par rdzogs/ sprel lor sa skyar bshad gsar
dang / gzhan yang zhwa lu sogs su gra skor mdzad/yongs kyi bshes gnyen chen po chos rje bla ma sku mched/ dpang lo/ rgyal sras pa/ bu dol gnyis/ gangs khrod pa grags pa
dpal/ ma ti pan chen/ mchims blo bzang grags pa sogs la mdo rgyud kyi gsan sbyangs mthar phyin/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan pa rin po che gsal bar mdzad de/ don brgyad
pa rta zla'i tshes nyer gcig la gshegs so/slob ma'i mchog nyid kyi dbon po lo chen grags pa dang / sgra pa nam mkha' bzang po sogs so/sum stong bzhi brgya dang so bdun
(brgyad) 'das pa'i so brgyad (dgu) pa me pho rta spyi lo 1306 la rig pa 'dzin pa gzungs kyi dpal ba mdog gad gler (sler) byon/ gung lo brgyad cu rtsa bzhi bzhugs/ byang
rtse las lo gsum gyis gzhon/sum stong bzhi brgya dang zhe gnyis 'das pa'i zhe gsum pa lcags pho kyi spyi lo 1310lor 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan byon/ 'di nyid bzang
po dpal gyi sras rnams bla brang go bzhir gyes pa'i bla brang rin chen sgang pa zhes grags pa de yin la/ 'di'i gcen rin chen sgang pa ta dben kun nyi dang / dus mchod
bla brang pa dbang kun legs dang / lha khang bla brang pa ti shri kun dga' legs 'byung gsum dgung mnyam yin la/ 'di'i gcung bla ma dam pa dang / bzhi thog bla brang pa gu
shri nam mkha' rgyal mtshan gnyis dgung mnyam

yin zhing / bdag nyid chen po'i sras dgu'i tha chung yin no/de yang 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan ni/ rang lo nyer gnyis pa'i tshe/ gcung bla ma dam pa dang gnyis bo dong
bya rgod gshong rnying pa'i gtsug lag khang du/ tshogs pa'i mkhan po bsod nams grags pa dang / slob dpon dpal ldan seng ge las bsnyen par rdzogs/ gdul bya dag pa la 'jam
dbyangs seng ge'i zhabs pad brten par yang mthong / so bzhi pa sprel lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu gcig la gshegs so/'di nyid lo chen byang rtse las lo bdun gyis gzhon
zhing / rab tu ma byung gong gi sras bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ de nyid ni
rgyud pa gsum ldan gyi gsung ngag rin po che'i bdud rtsi ngoms par gsol ba/ kho bo cag gi rgyud pa'i gtso bor byed pa yin no/Bla ma dam pasum stong bzhi brgya dang zhe bzhi
'das pa'i zhe lnga pa chu pho byi spyi lo 1312 lo chos rje bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan bltams/ gzungs pa las lo drug gis gzhon/ lo gsum pa'i tshe bla ma bzang po dpal
la 'jam dbyangs kyi lung nod nas bsnyen pa mdzad pas thogs med kyi spobs pa brnyes/ bcu gcig pa la bla chen kun blo bod du bsnyen rdzogs byon pa la dge bsnyen zhus/ bcu
bdun pa la mkhan chen bsod grags las rab tu byung / nyi shu pa la bya gshongs rnying par bsnyen par rdzogs/yongs 'dzin gyi dam pa dpang lo/ bu ston/ lo chen byang rtse/
rgyal sras thogs med/ dam pa brag phug pa/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/

mkhan chen bsod nams bzang po/ dpal ldan seng ge sogs las mdo rgyud kyi zab don blangs/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa'i ring lugs legs par bzung / dbus gtsang
gnyis su 'dus pa chen po rnam gnyis kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ rje btsun gong ma'i bka' bsdu ba mdzad de/ bstan pa rin po che gsal bar mdzad do/de yang re gcig pa byi
lor bo dong e'i chos grar/ bo dong er gtsang phyogs kyi dge 'dun stong phrag bzhi bcu dang re gnyis pa glang lor bsam yas su dbus phyogs kyi dge 'dun stong nyi shu la/ gser
dngul zho dar la sogs pa'i zho 'gyed dang / 'bel ba'i gtam gyis dga' ba bskyed/ snye thang du dus kyi 'khor lo 'chad pa na dpe 'grems don gnyer ldan pa lnga brgya lhag
cig 'dus/ bstan 'gro'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad de/ stod lung pa shes rab rdo rjes 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar bar mthong ba sogs dag pa'i snang ba bstan/ 'di nyid kyi bka'
'bum la yang po ti nyi shu rtsa lnga bzhugs/ dgung lo re bzhi pa shing mo yos kyi lo zla ba drug pa'i nyi shu lnga'i nyin dag pa'i zhing du gshegs so/slob ma'i mchog ni/
sngags kyi rgyal tshab chen po gnyis/ gsung ngag 'dzin pa'i thugs sras brgyad/ bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu chen po bzhi/ yongs grags kyi mkhas pa chen po bcu gcig go/dang po
ni/ snar thang pa sher snang ba dang / yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gnyis so/gnyis pa ni/ sngags 'chang gzungs pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ bla

chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ jo nang mkhan chen byang seng / lo chen byang rtse/ lo chen skyabs mchog dpal/ spyan snga grags pa byang chub bo/de dag
las sngags 'chang gzungs pa las bzang po rgyal mtshan dang / mkhas pa dge bzang gnyis kyi sgo nas gsung ngag rdzong lugs zhes grags pa'i brgyud pa'i gtso bo yin la/ gnyis
pa chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims nas/ grub chen buddha shrI la brgyud de gsung ngag ngor lugs zhes grags pa'i brgyud pa'i gtso bo mdzad pa yin no/de nas brgyud pa gsum
pa bzhi pa lnga pa gsum ni/ kho bo cag gi brgyud pa'i gtso bo bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan la yang bzhugs pa yin te/ chos rje bla ma/ bla chen kun rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs
nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros pa zhes dang / chos rje bla ma/ nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ rtse chen pa kun blo/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po/ bdag chen blo
gros pa zhes dang / chos rje bla ma/ mkhan chen byang seng / theg chen chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros pa zhes brgyud pa yin la/ de nyid
las rdo ring kun spangs pa/ yongs 'dzin blo gsal rgya mtsho/ kho bo cag gi 'dren pa dam pa de nyid la bka' babs pas so/drug pa lo chen byang rtse las/ lo chen grags pa/
des pan chen phyogs las rnam rgyal zhes bo dong pa dag gi rgyud pa'i gtso bo mdzad pa yin no/brgyud pa bdun pa ni lo chen skyabs mchog nas/ shangs chos 'khor

sgang pa sgra pa shes rin sogs las rgyud pa yin la/ brgyad pa ni spyan snga pa nas rje tsong kha pa sogs pa'o/bstan 'dzin skyes bu bzhi ni/ bu dol rgyal sras pa mkhan chen
g.yag pa dang bzhi'o/yongs grags kyi mkhas pa bcu gcig ni/ ma ti pan chen/ red mda' pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ne rings pa 'jam dpal rdo rje/ theg chen chos rje kun dga' bkra
shis/ gnyag phu ba bsod nams bzang po/ rtog ge pa dkar po dpal ldan bzang po/ grub chen buddha shrI/ karma rol pa'i rdo rje/ spos khang pa rin chen rgyan/ lha btsun bsam
yas pa/ shar tsong kha pa blo bzang grags pa rnams so/sum stong bzhi brgya don gnyis 'das pa'i don gsum pa lcags pho 'brug spyi lo 1340la karma rol pa'i rdo rje kong yul
du byon/ chos rje bla ma las nyer brgyad kyis gzhon/ lo gsum pa'i tshe/ nga karma paka shi'i skye ba yin 'jam gling 'dir nga'i gdul bya mang du yod gsungs/ mkhan chen don
grub dpal dang gdan gcig pa bsod nams 'bum las rim gyis rab byung bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ mtshan chos kyi grags par gsol/ rol pa'i rdo rje ni/ rang byung rdo rje'i gsang mtshan
yin zer/ nyer gcig pa la hor gyis gdan drangs te/ the mur gyi bla ma mdzad zer/ bla chen bsod blos ti shri mdzad pa'i skabs tsam yin par sems/ dgung lo zhe bzhi pa chu
phag gi zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga'i tho rengs gshegs so/gNyag Phu Pa bSod Nams bZangs Posum stong bzhi brgya dang don gsum 'das pa'i don bzhi pa lcags mo

sbrul spyi lo 1341la gnyag phu pa bsod nams bzang po gtsang gsum mdor byon/ 'di chos rje bla ma las lo nyer dgu dang / karma rol pa'i rdo rje las lo gcig gis gzhon/ theg chen
pa las brgyad kyis bgres so/ lo lnga pa la gnyag chen bsod nams dbang phyug la dge bsnyen zhus/ bcu gcig pa la mkhan po don grub dpal ldan las dge tshul nod/ khyi lor
mkhan po yon tan rgya mtsho dang / las slob dpal ldan brtson 'grus las bsnyen rdzogs/ dpal ldan sa skyar nya dbon kun dga' dpal la tshad ma gsan/ de nyid kyis slob bu bzhi
brgya'i nang nas mchog tu mdzad/ de'i dus na dpal ldan sa skya na mkhas pa nya brtson gnyis grags che zhing / mdo phyogs kyis 'chad nyan rkang tshugs su gnang ba las/ nya
dbon ni dol bu'i slob ma'i mchog dang / brtson 'grus dpal ni bu ston gyi slob ma'i mchog yin/ de'i tshe gnyag phu ba 'dis mkhan chen brtson 'grus dpal yang rigs pas bcom
ste ston pa bzang ba'i grags pa thob ces kyang zer ro/ rje 'di nyid g.yag phrug sangs rgyas dpal dang / karma dkon mchog gzhon nu dang mkhas pa sangs rgyas 'phel dang
gzhan gnyis dang bcas pa'i dpal ldan sa skya'i mkhas pa drug gis dbus gtsang la gra skor la phebs pa na/ nya brtson gnyis kyis thog drangs rgya mtsho dpon rnams kyis/ sa
skya mdun gyi zhing bya khra ma'i khar skyel thung mdzad/ mkhas pa khyod drug phyogs su 'bel ba'i dga' ston la chags la/ grangs lhag rgyu mi 'dug kyang / yon tan khyed drug
las lhag pa phyin chad mi 'byung zhing / so so nas yon tan gzhal du med kyang gnyag dbon bslab pas che bar 'dug pas gral gyi dbus su zhog ces kyang bsngags so/ gsang

phu dang / rtse thang sogs su bka' chen bzhi mdo rgyan mdzod drug la bshad pa'i sgra snyan lhag par bsgrags/mkhas mchog bsten tshul yang / kun mkhyen gangs pa la bde mchog/
dpal ldan bla ma dam pa las dus 'khor/ mkhan chen byang seng la sbyor drug/ ma ti pan chen la spros med/ rgyal sras pa las sems skyed/ theg chen chos rje la lam sbas ['bras]
bshad/ jo nang phyogs las pa la dus 'khor gsan/de yang se mkhar chung du/ dpe 'grems sum brgya/ chos dpon brgyad cu la phyogs las pas dus 'khor gzab bshad mdzad/ ngas
shes tshod de tsam yin/ khyed rnams so so'i go yul yig chung re khyer shog gsungs/ so so nas phul bas/ gnyag phu ba'i shog ril la 'dis kho bo'i grub mtha' go 'dug gsungs
phyag rgyas spras te gnang zer ro/g.yas ru byang nas kyis 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rin chen gyi bka' stsal te/ dpal bzang ldan gyi chos grwar slob bu btsun chung drug gnang
nas 'chad nyan la bskos/ lo bcu drug 'chad nyan bsrings pas blo gsal sum brgya tsam 'dus te bzang ldan dge 'phel gyi grwa tshang tshugs/ slar gcung pa chos gzhon dang
grwa pa thug phrad kyis nyen bslangs/ 'jam dbyangs pas zhal 'phrad ma gnang bas/ mtshams sbyar te/ chos kyis 'byor yang nor dang mi ldan zhing // bden tshig yod kyang zhu
ba'i skabs med la// nyes pa med kyang nag can gnyag phu ba'i// zhu ba'i tshig 'di cung zad gsan par rigs// zhes sogs kyi zhu mchid phul te phyogs la phebs pas/ jo gdan mkhan
po'i

brtag pa bud pa dang rten 'brel sne 'joms te mkhan por mnga' gsol/ de yang sa pho khyi lo bco brgyad pa nas/ sa mo bya lo nyer dgu pa'i bar lo bcu gnyis su phyi nang gi bslab
sbyang mthar phyin mdzad/ sum cu pa lcags pho khyi nas zhe gcig pa/ byi lo'i bar lo bco lnga 'chad nyan yang dag pa mdzad/ zhe gcig pa shing pho byi lo sne gdong grags
pa rgyal mtshan pas spyan drangs te/ jo gdan dge 'dun sgang pa'i mkhan po/ kha che pan chen gyi gdan seng ge'i khri la lnga bcu rtsa drug pa sa mo yos kyi bar lo bcu drug
zhabs brtan par 'khod do/mdor na bla ma yongs 'dzin bdun gyis lhag pa'i bcu phrag brgyad bsten/ 'chad pa'i rgyun bsrings/ rtsom pa phal cher sku shin tu bgres pa nas mdzad
de/ don gsum pa la 'dul ba'i bka' 'grel bdud rtsi nying khu/ don brgyad pa la 'jam dbyangs kha ches bskul te/ chos dbyings bstod pa'i rnam bshad snying po don gsal/ brgyad
cu pa la rnam 'grel gyi Tika/ gya gcig pa la lo tsA ba skyabs mchog gis gzhan stong dgag pa'i lan lung rigs gter mdzod mdzad do/ gya gsum pa la 'dul ba 'di la bag chags
sad/ rgan po'i lag rjes 'jog gsungs/ lung sde bzhi so thar gyi mdo dang bcas pa la mchan bu btab/ gya lnga pa la rgyud bla'i Tika mdzad/ rtsod pa yang sangs pa dang
bde gshegs snying po skor la rtsod pa mdzad pa sogs bstan pa dpang btsugs kyi rtsod pa mdzad/ dgung lo dgu bcu rtsa gsum pa chu mo glang gi lor gshegs so/slob ma'i mchog
ni/ chos bzang nyi ma/ bka' bcu pa padma

bzang po/ karma de bzhin gshegs pa/ karma mthong ba don ldan/ smra ba'i seng ge rong ston chen po sogs so/des na da lta'i shing byi 'di/ rgyal sras thogs med byon pa'i shing
mo lug nas nyis brgya dang bdun cu pa lo chen byang rtse'i chu mo yos nas nyis brgya dang re gnyis pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa'i chu pho byi ba nas nyis brgya dang gsum
pa/ gnyag dbon byon pa'i lcags sbrul nas nyis brgya dang nyi shu rtsa bzhir sleb pa yin no/g.Yag ston Sangs rgyas dpalmkhas pa'i dbang po g.yag phrug sangs rgyas dpal zhes
grags pa yang / gnyag dbon dang rigs lam smra ba thog mtshungs shing / 'di las sku cung zad gzhon la mkhan chen g.yag pa lcags pho stag lo pa ltar na gnyag dbon las lo
dgus gzhon par mchis so/ rje btsun red mda' pa las cung bgres pa shig yin la pan shAka pa'i gtam gyi rol mtsho las/ bu ston lcags pho stag lo 'khrungs pa'i re gcig pa lcags
pho stag lor g.yag pa 'khrungs/ de'i nyer brgyad pa me lo lug la rong ston 'khrungs zhes bshad 'dugde yang rtse thang ga gi chen po byang chub rin chen sras yin pa la/
rnam pa de nyid kyi nye gnas g.yag yu zhes pa'i sras su ngos blangs pas na/ g.yag phrug ces grags la/ 'khrungs yul dngos ni sa skya 'phrang zhes bya ba de yin zhing / dpal
ldan sa skya dang rtse thang sogs su gsan sbyong mdzad/ sa skya'i mkhas dbang brtson 'grus dpal la gtso bor brten nas mdo la sbyangs shing / gon gyo ye shes la gsung ngag
sogs gsan/ bu dol gyi slob ma nya brtson gnyis/ nya brtson gnyis kyi slob ma g.yag gzhon rnam gnyis zhes bstan

pa'i gsal byed dam par gyur/ dbus gtsang gi mkhas grub gong ma'i bsti gnas so sor/ mkhas pa'i slob grogs ha cang mang ba min pa zhig la 'chad rgyun bsrings/ rgyun 'dzin mkhas
pa rong ston smra ba'i seng ge dang / red mda' pa chen po/ gzhon nu rgyal mchog sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byon la/ 'di nyid mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i nyer bdun
pa shing pho rta lor dga' ldan du gshegs zhes 'byung bas/ red mda' pa chen po zhi bar gshegs pa'i chu pho 'brug gi yang phyi ma'i rta lo de yin par sems so/des na mkhan
chen g.yag pas don lnga bzhugs te/ lcags pho stag la bltams nas shing rta la gshegs pas so/sum stong bzhi brgya dang brgyad cu 'das pa'i gya gcig pa sa pho byi spyi lo 1348
lo mnyam med red mda' pa chen po bod kyi blon po mgar stong btsan gyi rgyud du/ dpal ldan sa skya dang khad nye ba'i red mda' khab sor byon/ gnyag dbon las lo bdun gyis
gzhon no/ theg chen chos rje las lo gcig gis bgres/ lo bco brgyad pa la sa bzang ma ti'i drung du/ tshigs snga ma gnyis nod de mtshan gzhon nu blo gros zhes gsol/ thog
mar dpal ldan sa skyar/ mkhas pa nya dbon dang / mkhan chen sangs rgyas 'phel ba'i drung du tshad ma/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i drung du phar phyin/ lo chen byang rtse las
mngon pa gong 'og/ rgyal sras pa'i drung du blo sbyong / mdog lo pa mkhan chen kun dga' dpal las bsnyen par rdzogs shing / 'dul ba gsan/ mkhan pos stod 'dul gyi sdom rgyud
'di ma chad cig gnang dgos zhes bka' stsal phebs zer mod/ stod 'dul ba'i bshad rgyun ma gtogs sdom rgyun rang du

cung mi 'gro bar sems te/ mdog lo pas chos rje bla ma las bsnyen par rdzogs shing / chos rje bla ma'i sdom rgyun ni kha che mkhan po shAkya shrI las brgyud pa'i phyir ro/ gzhan
yang bla ma dpal ldan pa'i drung du lam 'bras/ lo tsA ba nam bzang / lo tsA ba grags rgyal/ lo tsA ba skyabs mchog dpal sogs las gsang 'dus sogs kyi rgyud man ngag dang
/ mkhan chen byang seng la dbu ma gsan zhing dkon mchog la gsol ba btab ste rang gi rnam dpyod kyis dpyad pas dbu ma thal 'gyur ba'i gnad la nges pa rnyed de/ nged dang
po slob gnyer byed dus dbu ma'i dpe cha gcig 'dug ces nor mi che bar byed pa las/ deng sang rtsis su byed pa ni kho bos bstan pa la bya ba byas pa yin zhes dang / karma
pa dkon gzhon gyi gsun gis/ deng sang mkhas rmongs kun la dbu ma dbu ma zer ba 'di red mda' pa'i drin yin/ de gong thang zag na dbu ma shi ro gcig las gzhan med ces kyang
gsung zer te/ rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa dang / dbu ma thal 'gyur ba'i bstan pa la 'di kho na bka' drin che ba yin/de yang mkhas pa 'di sngon bu rin po la mos pa shig yin
na'ang / slob dpon dang grogs kyi stobs kyis kun mkhyen chen po'i grub mtha' la 'dris che ba zhig byung / de nyid kyi grub mtha'i rgyab brten bka' bstan bcos la gzigs rtog
tshar gsum mdzad pas dang po la gzhan stong gi grub mtha' de ni bka' bstan bcos dag gi dgongs pa yin nges pa shar/ gnyis pa la som nyi za ba gcig byung / gsum pa la min
par nges shes 'drongs pa gcig byung gsung zer ba na'ang / gnas skabs so sor phye dgos so zhes kho bo cag

de'i tshe chos kyi gnad ma rtogs par grub mtha'i kha 'dzin rang stong gzhan stong zhes pa'i ming tsam la zhen pa dag gis/ chos spong gi las rgya cher bsags par snang ba ni/
blun rmongs kho na'i spyod yul lo/ mkhas pa 'di ni bshad sgrub zung ldan du mdzad de/ bul rong gi dben gnas su lo bcu gnyis bzhugs pa'i lo lnga rtsod sgom gtso bor ston
pa'i thugs dam nyams bzhes kho na mdzad/ lo bdun skal ldan gyi gdul bya brgyad cu skor la nyams khrid legs bshad kyi dga' ston spel/rtsom pa mdzad pa yang / 'dzam gling mdzes
pa'i rgyan mchog dka' chen bzhi// rtsa 'jug gzhi gsum theg chen rgyud bla ma// chos mngon mdzod dang dpal ldan 'dus pa ste// rnam bshad mdzad pa'i gzhung lugs bcu phrag
cig// phar tshad shes pa'i slob ma brgya phrag brgal// ces pa ltar yin la/ 'chad pa dbyangs kyi gsung las skyes pa'i slob ma'i grangs kyang / gzhung lugs rab 'byams smra
ba'i bshes gnyen bdun// bka' bzhi legs par smra ba bcu phrag gcig// phar tshad shes pa'i slob ma brgya phrag brgal// zhes pa ltar te/bshes gnyen bdun ni/ sbyangs pa'i
mchog gyur kun mkhyen sher 'od dang // sras kyi mchog gyur blo bzang grags pa dang // lta ba'i mchog gyur gon gyo nyi ma grags// nyams len mchog gyur kun dga' dpal bzang
po// rtsom ldan mchog gyur dpal 'byor shes rab dang / 'chad mkhas mchog gyur bsod nams shes rab dang // rtsod bzang mchog gyur dar ma rin chen te// zhes pa ltar yin zhing
bka' bcu ba gzhan yang / byang pa bka' bcu pa dge legs dpal la sogs pa'o// de lta bu'i skyes bu 'di ni/ drug cu

rtsa lnga pa chu pho 'brug gi zla ba bcu pa'i nyer dgu'i nyi shar la dag pa'i zhing du gshegs so/des na sum stong bzhi brgya pa'i mjug 'dir bka' bzhi pa dang bka' bcu pa la
sogs pa'i mtshan dang ldan pa'i mkhas grub mang dag byung ste/ hor bka' bzhi pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bka' bzhi pa nam mkha' 'od zer la sogs pa dang / bka' bcu pa ni/ rgyal
tshab dar ma man chad nas byung bar gsal te/ de yan du bka' chen bzhir grags pa dang / de bzhi'i steng du ci rigs bsnan pa'i drug tsam la gra skor mdzad pa sha stag byung
ba yin la/ rgyal tshab rjes po ti bcu la bshad pa'i srol btod man chad nas dka' bcu pa zhes mtshan grags shing / bo dong phyogs las pas bco lnga la bshad pa gnang yang
dbon po bka' bcu pa zhes pa tsam las ma byung la/ phyis byams chen smra ba'i dbang po sangs rgyas 'phel man chad nas rab 'byams pa zhes kyang yongs su grags so/ 'on kyang
bka' pa gzhon nu seng ge sogs/ de yan du yang bka' pa'i mtshan chung zhig grags par gsal lo//sum stong bzhi brgya dang gya gcig 'das pa'i gya gnyis pa sa mo glang spyi
lo 1349 la theg chen chos rje kun dga' bkra shis dpal sa skyar byon/ chos rje bla ma las so bdun gyis gzhon/ de yang bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal gyi sras rnams bla
brang go bzhir gyes pa'i lha khang bla brang pa'i gdung brgyud dri ma med pa ste/ lha khang bla brang pa ti shri kun rgyal/ yab bzang po dpal zhe dgu pa lcags pho khyi lor
byon pa yin la/ de'i sras rtan dben chos rgyan yab nyer gsum pa chu pho sprel lo la byon pa yin zhing / de nyid bco brgyad pa'i

sras theg chen chos rje 'di yin no/de yang dang po sa bzang ma ti las rab tu byung / phyis chos rje bla ma las bsnyen par rdzogs/ gzhan yang / gangs khrod pa grags pa dpal/
jo nang phyogs las sogs mkhas grub mang du bsten/ gsung ngag gsan pa'i bla ma yang / thog mar ma ti pan chen la sa bzang dgon par gsan pa yin mod/ de nyid la lam dus kyi
chu rgyun chag med mi bzhugs pas/ phyis sa skya zur khang du bu ston dbang phyug dar la gsan/brgyud pa de yang chos rje brag phug pa nas brag phug dkon rgyal/ des sa skya
bu ston la brgyud pa yin gyi chos rje bla ma brgyud pa la mi bzhugs pas/ phyis chos rje bla ma las dngos su nod pa mkhan chen byang seng la gsan pa yin no// zhes rje btsun
dam pa kun dga' grol mchog gsungs la/ rje btsun blo gsal rgya mtsho'i gsung las/ mkhan chen byang seng la zab chos mang du gsan yang / gsung ngag gsan pa'i bla ma ni
snga ma gnyis kho na'o zhes gsungs so/gang na'ang dbang khrid gdams pa'i sgo mo brgya phrag gis skal ldan gyi 'gro ba'i yid gsos par mdzad de mthar tA ming rgyal pos spyan
drangs te/ re bzhi pa chu pho 'brug la sa skya nas shar phyogs la phebs/ re lnga pa chu mo sprul la pho brang gser khang du rgyal po dang mjal/ rgyal po 'khor bcas la dbang
gdams pa'i sgo phye/ 'phags pa ti shri dang 'dra bar bod chol kha gsum yang 'bul gsungs/ slar pho brang tA'i tur byon/ gser dngul gyi thub pa nye ba'i sras brgyad kyis
bskor ba gandho la dang bcas pa yang phul/ 'di nyid byang ngam

rings su yang lo bskor gcig tsam bzhugs/ gzhan yang / byi ru'i gshed dmar %gshed snying% gi 'jigs byed (sa skya'i gdung rabs nang sher shing gi 'jigs byed ces gsal/ sgrig pa
pos) gse'u thags kyi thang sku gnyis/ za 'og thogs gnyis la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul/ slar re drug pa rta lo la gong nas bteg/ re bdun pa lug lor dpal ldan sa
skyar phebs te/ don bdun pa shing mo sbrul gro zhun zla ba'i tshes bcu'i nyi shar la dag pa'i zhing du gshegs so/slob ma'i mchog ni kun dga' rgyal mtshan 'jam dbyangs grags
pa'i dpal lo/ sum stong bzhi brgya dang gya dgu 'das pa'i dgu bcu pa me mo bya spyi lo 1357 la shar tsong kha pa blo bzang grags pa mdo khams su byon/ chos rje bla ma
las zhe lngas gzhon/ red mda' pa chen po dang / theg chen pa las rim bzhin lo dgu dang brgyad kyis gzhon no/ 'di nyid lo bdun pa la mdo khams pa don grub rin chen las rab
tu byung / don grub rin chen de ni/ bcom ldan rig ral gyi bu chen ldong ston rigs pa'i seng ge'i slob ma yin zer/ dgung lo bcu drug pa la dbus gtsang la byon/ grwa sa bde
ba can du snye thang pa bkra shis sogs las [phar] phyin sbyangs/ bcu dgu pa la gsang phu sogs su grwa skor gnang / gtsang phyogs kyi zha lu/ snar thang / sa skya sogs
su byon/ sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam rgyal dang / ma ti pan chen sogs la zab chos gsan grwa skor yang mdzad/ la stod byang gi bzang ldan ngam ring 'ga' rong sogs su grwa
skor mdzad/ jo nang du phyogs las pa la sbyor drug gsan/ bo dong du grwa

skor mdzad nas snar thang du phyag phebs/ de nas nya dbon la phar phyin dang / rje btsun red mda' pa las mngon pa dang dbu ma sogs gsan te/ de nyid kyi thugs sras dam par gyur/
skyor mo lung gi mkhan po bka' bzhi pa blo gsal la 'dul ba gsan/ gong gsum bde chen pa sogs las sngags kyi rgyud man ngag gsan/ jo gdan tshogs chen po'i mkhan po dka'
bzhi pa tshul rin las bsnyen par rdzogs/ bla ma dbu ma pas mtshams sbyar te rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs la chos gsan/ bla ma dbu ma pa ni/ mdo khams su byis pa'i dus nyid
nas 'jam dbyangs kyi sku'i snang ba shar/ rje 'di dang phar slob tshur slob yin/ mdor na rje 'dis sku tshe'i stod la thos bsam gyis rgyud sbyangs/ bar skabs su bya bral
kho na mdzad/ zab don la dpyad sgom gyi sgo nas don nyams su bzhes/ 'phral gyi kun spyod 'dul ba'i lag len gsos btab/ khyad par du dbu ma thal 'gyur ba'i bstan pa cher
spel/sku tshe'i smad la gzhan don phyogs med du rgyas/ dgung lo nga gsum pa sa mo glang la chos 'khor lha sar smon lam chen mo mdzad/ jo bo la rin po che'i dbu rgyan yang
gsol/ bka' chems las/ de nas khyad par bsnyen bkur cher mdzad pa// dge slong byang sems shar phyogs sku 'khrungs pa// gsang sngags 'chang zhing rnal 'byor chen po ni// snying
po'i mtha' can skyes chen dam pa ni// zhal yang bsgyur zhing bsnyen bkur dam pa mdzad// ces pa'i lung gi don yin par yang 'chad/ lo de nyid la ri bo dge ldan yang btab/
de phyin ri bo dge ldan pa zhes yongs su grags pa yin no/ de nas dgung lo re gsum pa sa mo phag gi nyer lnga la dag pa'i zhing du gshegs so/

slob ma'i mchog ni/ rgyal tshab rje/ mkhas grub rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub/ 'dul 'dzin grags rgyal/ 'dul 'dzin blo gros sbas pa ste 'dul 'dzin rnam gnyis la sogs
pa bsam gyis mi khyab bo/des na da lta'i shing byi 'di/ theg chen pa byon pa'i sa mo glang nas nyis brgya dang bcu drug pa/ shar tsong kha pa byon pa'i me bya nas nyis
brgya dang brgyad du slebs pa yin no/sa bcad lnga pa sum stong lnga brgya pa'i skabs su byon pa ni/ rong ston smra ba'i seng ge/ bo dong phyogs las rnam rgyal/ sa skya pa'i
btsan 'dzin kun dga' rnam gnyis/ karma de bzhin gshegs pa la sogs pa ste/ sum stong bzhi brgya dang go dgu 'das pa'i lnga brgya'i steng du sleb tsam gyi me mo lug spyi
lo 1367la rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan shar rgya mo rong du byon/ shar tsong kha pa las lo bcus gzhon/ lo bco brgyad yan chad du bon la 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gnang / bco
brgyad pa la gsang phu ne'u thog gi chos grwar gling stod pa rin chen rnam rgyal dang / kong ston blo gros dbang phyug gi drung du rngog lo nas brgyud pa'i phar tshad
bsdus gsum dang / dbu ma rang brgyud pa'i bshad srol/ skyor mo lung gi mkhan chen dka' bzhi pa dang / 'phan yul gro pa'i mkhas pa dmar ston la 'dul ba smad lugs bya 'dul
dang thog ma dka' chen gyi bshad srol/ mngon pa mdzod mchims lugs kyi bshad srol/ thang zag pa sprul sku gzhon nu rgyal mtshan la dbu ma thal 'gyur ba tshab kyi bshad srol/
lo pa shAkya rin chen gyi drung du mngon pa gong ma sogs la sbyangs/ lo nyer gnyis pa la/ gro pa'i mkhan po kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang dmar ston pa'i drung du

rab tu byung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs/ rnam nges kyi ti ka brtsams shing 'chad pa'i 'khur bzung / mdor na lo nyer gnyis nas gya gsum gyi bar la mkhas pa'i bya ba gsum gyis dus
'da' ba kho na byung zhing nyer bdun pa sa mo bya'i lo la/ mkhan chen g.yag pa dang mjal te sa lugs kyi mdo'i bshad srol dang / theg chen chos rje la gsung ngag sogs sngags
kyi zab don blangs nas sa rngog rnam gnyis kyi bshad srol rgyun bsrings te/ cha pa chos seng dang / bcom ldan rig ral dang / kun mkhyen 'di gsum las 'chad pa'i rgyun
dang / dngos slob bstan 'dzin gyi thon che ba ma byung zhes grags/gtsang phyogs la yang lan gsum byon pa'i dang po lo nyer bdun pa'i tshe/ mkhan chen pa'i zhabs 'bring
mdzad de mdo'i zab don gsan pa dang legs bshad kyi skyes 'bul ba kho na mdzad/ gnyis pa rang lo zhe brgyad pa la mkhan chen pa gshegs te/ lnga bcu tsam gyi tshe ding ri dang
mus sogs su sngags kyi zab don bzhes pa dang / mdo phyogs kyi 'phrin las spel ba kho na mdzad/ lan gsum pa drug cu rtsa gcig pa'i tshe/ sde dpon so so'i bsod nams kyi
mgron dang / mdo sngags kyi chos 'khor bskor ba kho na mdzad/ bdun cu pa me pho 'brug la nA landre'i chos grwa btab nas lo bcu bzhir gzhan don mdzad cing / dbus gtsang du
gra skor mdzad pa'i po ti bcu kho na yin yang / gzhan la 'doms pa'i gzhung lugs drug cu rtsa bzhi dang / rnam bshad mdzad pa'i gzhung lugs bzhi bcu yod gsungs/ gzhan yar
lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ lo chen skyabs mchog/ lo chen grags pa/ kun mkhyen sher 'od/ lo chen skyabs mchog/ lo chen grags pa/ kun mkhyen sher 'od/ snyan ngag pa 'jam
dbyangs kha che/ mus nam mkha'i rnal 'byor sogs

la zab don mang du blangs/ dam pa sangs rgyas kyi sku lus la kA ma la shi la'i thugs grong 'jug mdzad pa de'i sku'i skye bar gdon mi za bas/ dam pa'i zhi byed/ kA ma la shi
la'i sgom rim sogs ched du gsal bar mdzad cing / khyad par phar phyin gyi bstan pa dang / dbu ma rang rgyud pa'i bstan pa la kun mkhyen 'di bka' drin che ba yin no/legs
bshad 'doms pa'i 'bras bu mkhas grub slob ma'i grangs ni/ snga tshar gyi bu chen bstan pa 'debs pa'i ka chen bzhi/ bar tshar gyi bu chen gangs can mdzes pa'i rgyan brgyad
dang mchog gnyis/ sku gsung thugs kyi mdzad spyod mtshungs pa'i bu chen gsum/ phyi tshar gyi bu chen bstan pa'i gsal byed bcu drug/ yang tshar gyi bu chen grags pa can bzhi
la sogs pa'o/dang po ni/ sems dpa' gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ sems dpa' chen po padma bzang po/ gzad pa blo gros rgya mtsho/ spyan snga tshul khrims dar ma'o/bar tshar brgyad
ni/ smar khams pa grags pa bzang po/ dge ba rgyal mtshan/ gung ru rgyal mtshan bzang po/ rong chung shes rab dpal te khams pa bzhi/ chos lung bka' bcu pa/ sga sdong
pa (dga' gdong) pa chos rgyal dpal bzang / mkhas dbang ratna shrI bha dra/ snar thang pa shes rab seng ge/ bzang ldan bka' bcu pa ste gtsang pa bzhi'o/ (gcig lhag)mchog gnyis
ni/ dbus pa dmar ston rgya mtsho rin chen dang / gtsang pa sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gnyis so/mdzad spyod mtshungs pa gsum ni/ mdo khams dpal ldan thod
se/ sgoms sde khra hral/ sa skya nas gzhon nu seng ge dang gsum mo/

phyi tshar drug la pan chen bzhi ni/ snar thang lo tsA ba samabha bha dra/ yar rgyab dbon po pan chen bsod nams rnam rgyal/ slob 'dar ba lo chen gzhon nu dpal/ dwags po dbon
po pan chen bkra shis rnam rgyal lo/gsung sgros 'dzin pa'i mkhas pa bcu gnyis ni/ khams su lha 'bri ston pa shes rab rdo rje dang / rin chen blo gros gnyis/ dbus su bzod
chen phyogs las rnam rgyal dang / mkhas grub don yod dpal ba gnyis/ dbus su bzod chen phyogs las rnam rgyal dang / mkhas grub don yod dpal ba gnyis/ nyang stod pa shes
rab legs dpal/ ngam ring pa sangs rgyas grub/ mnga' ris su 'jam dbyangs sher rgyal lo/ nges med du bzhugs pa gzhu ston bsod nams rin chen/ gsang phu nas panDi ta nam mkha'
bstan pa/ gtsang rong byams chen nas dkar shAkya grags/ khams nas gon gyo sbyin bzang dang / ga zi blo gros seng ge rnams so/yang tshar bzhi ni/ gsang phu nas gra ston
pa yon tan rgya mtsho dang / rtse thang nas chen po dpal 'byor rgya mtsho gnyis/ khams su go bo rab 'byams pa shes rab dpal dang / gtsang du byams chen rab 'byams pa sangs
rgyas 'phel te bzhi'o/sum stong lnga brgya dang brgyad 'das pa'i dgu pa me pho 'brug spyi lo 1376la/ la stod lho shrI sar sa ta dm: par pa tadpal gyi ri'i byang ngos kyi
'brog sde chen por/ bo dong phyogs las rnam rgyal byon/ lo bdun pa la/ gyi dgon par rang gi zhang po lo chen grags pa'i drung du rab tu byung / mtshan sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan gsol/ slar bo dong er lo chen de nyid las dge tshul du bsgrubs te/ mtshan chos kyi rgyal mtshan du btags/ lo bcu drug pa la dpal ldan sa skyar rnam

'grel gyi grwa skor mdzad/ bo dong er dbyangs can ma bsgrubs pas/ rgyud mangs kyi sgra las zab rgyas kyi chos tshul nod de/ phyi nang gi mdzad 'phrin ma lus pa sad pas dbyangs
can dga' ba'i dpal zhes grags/ dgung lo nyer gsum pa la/ rtse thang dang gsang phur pu ti bco lnga'i grwa skor gnang bas mkhas pa'i grags pas khyab/ de'i tshe gsang phur
mkhan chen g.yag phrug sangs rgyas dpal dang / rigs gter gyi dgongs pa/ rang rig yul yod med la rtsod pa'i tshe/ mkhan chen pas rang rig yul med du zhal gyis bzhes pa
la/ rje 'dis/ rang rig chos can/ rang gi gzhal bya mi bslu ba'i rig par thal/ tshad ma yin pa'i phyir/ 'dod na khyod kyi yul yod par thal lo zhes dang / mkhan chen pas gzugs
sgra ka bum sogs rtag par khas blangs pa la/ ka ba chos can/ khyod kyi gzugs med par thal/ khyod rtag pa yin pa'i phyir zhes pa'i rigs pa'i sgo nas snyan par grags so/
'on kyang pha rol gyi grub mtha'i go don dang bstun na khyab pa med mtshams de kho na yin pas/ phas rgol pham par gyur pa yang ma yin no/ de nas slar/ e chos kyi 'byung
gnas su lo chen grags pas mkhan po dang / rje btsun red mda' pa chen pos las slob bgyis te bsnyen par rdzogs/des na pan chen 'di'i rnam thar ni bsam gyis mi khyab brjod
kyis mi langs na'ang / gtso bo bsdus na rtsod pas phas rgol dregs pa gzhom nus tshul/ rtsom pas bka' bstan bcos kyi dgongs pa bkral tshul/ 'chad pas bstan 'dzin gyi bu slob
spel tshul gsum las/dang po ni/ las stod lhor/ ta'i si tu lha btsan byang rgyab pas mthun

pa'i rkyen sbyar te/ g.yag phrug sangs rgyas dpal dang rtsod pa'i tshe/ bka' bstan bcos kyi gzhung phal che ba/ rgol phyi rgol gnyis char gyi mgrin pa nas thogs med du sgrogs
shing / phas kyi rgol ba g.yag phrug sangs rgyas dpal dang chen po'i spobs pa sgrub pa la/ rgol ba de nyid kyi yi dam lha rje btsun mi g.yo ba mngon sum du byon pa pan
chen nyid kyis kyang zhal gzigs/ de'i tshe lha gcig ma ngo log/ sod cig ma mgo ma thon/ gdong gang bo rtsod pa pham zhes grags so zhes zer mod/ don du na rje btsun mi g.yo
ba mngon sum du byon pa na/ rgol ba gnyis char gyi ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i rnam thar yin zhing / rtsod pa'i ngag la yang / rang rang gi gdul bya'i snang ngor pham
rgyal gyi snang ngo tsam las/ phas rgol gyi rgol ba nyid gshis la pham par rigs pa ga la yin te/ dper na de'i tshe mkhan chen g.yag pas sems can sangs rgya nges yin/ rgyas
pa mi srid ces khas blangs pa la/ pan chen pas sa bon las myu gu skye/ skyes pa mi srid par thal/ dam bca' de yin pa'i phyir zhes pa la sogs pa la lan ma byung zhes sgrogs
mod/ yang dag par na de gnyis mtshungs pa'i go skabs ga la yod de/ sems can sangs rgyas pa med par khas blangs kyi sems can las sangs rgyas byung ba med par khas ma
blangs pa'i phyir ro/ sa bon myu gur song ba med par khas len gyi sa bon las myu gu skye ba med par khas blangs mi dgos pa'i phyir ro/de nas byang ngam rings su bdag chen
'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rin chen pas mthun pa'i rkyen sbyar te dpal ngam rings kyi bshes gnyen dag la 'bel ba'i gtam gyi sgo phye/ don dam don byed nus pa gang // zhes pa'i
gzhung la grub mtha' rnam bzhi'i bden

gnyis kyi rnam gzhag phra zhing zhib pa'i blo gros kyi sgo phye ste/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsod nams skyabs dang / mkhas grub dge legs dpal sogs rigs pas pham par byas so/ zhes
grags so//des na byang mdog gi pho brang du ta'i si tu rnam rgyal grags pas mthun pa'i rkyen sbyar te kun mkhyen rong ston chen po slob bu'i tshogs dang bcas pa la 'bel
ba'i gtam chen po gleng / gsang sngags kyi dkyil 'khor chen po khri phrag gcig gi zhal phye bar zhal gyis 'ches shing / 'jam dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor drug cu'i rnam grangs
legs par bgrangs shing / 'phags yul du byon pa'i thal rang gi skyes chen 'dren res bgyis pa na/ rong ston chen pos legs ldan 'byed/ dpal sbas/ ye shes snying po/ zhi
'tsho/ ka ma la shI lakA la ma shi la te lnga las bgrang ma bzod pa la/ pan chen nyid kyis nyi shu rtsa lnga tsam zhig thal byung du bgrangs pa sogs kyi sgo nas pha rol zin
gyis mnan to zhes grags so//gnyis pa rtsom pa ni/ yi dam gyi lha dpal rdo rje sems dpa' dang / rdo rje phag mo la sogs pas mngon sum du gnang ba stsal zhing / dpal de
nyid 'dus pa la rtsoms shig ces gnang ba nod pa dang / mtshan gyi 'od gsal chen po las/ dpal sa skya pa chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan dang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa dang
/ shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan la sogs pas kyang de ltar gnang ba stsal ba la brten/ de nyid bsdus pa'i rgya mtsho/ 'jug pa'i sgo bzhi/ le'u nyi khri chig stong /
man ngag bdun khri nyis stong / chos kyi tshogs brgyad khri bzhi stong yod pas rgyas pa la glegs bam brgya dang bcu/ 'bring po la nyi shu/ bsdus pa la glegs bam gnyis/ shin
tu bsdudas pa'i snying po la glegs

bam gcig yod pa'i rtsom chen po mdzad de/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa gsal bar mdzad do//gsum pa 'chad pas blo gsal gyi bu slob spel ba'i tshul ni/ bzo rig nas bzung yongs su rdzogs
pa'i bar// de dang de yi bka' babs nyi shu gsum// 'jam pa'i rdo rje mi yi zlos gar mkhan// rnam dag 'khon gyi gdung rgyud rnam pa gsum// rig sngags 'chang ba'i khyu mchog
chen po gcig// nyi ma zla ba ltar grags mkhas grub gnyis// 'jig rten gsum gyi mig gcig lo chen gsum// phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i bshes gnyen drug// mdo sngags yongs
rdzogs mkhas pa bcu gsum dang // pan chen shAkya shrI'i gdan sa gnyis// 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i gtsug rgyan bcu drug dang // mtshan nyid rab 'byams smra ba'i bshes gnyen gsum//
sngags gzhung rab 'byams smra ba'i bshes gnyen gsum// grub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i rnal 'byor bzhi// drag po'i brtul zhugs rdzogs pa'i sngags 'chang gnyis// dka'
bcu legs par smra ba stong phrag gcig// dka' bzhi kun tu smra ba stong phrag zung // phar tshad shes pa'i slob ma khri phrag brgal// tshe 'di blos btang grub chen lnga
bcur ldan// lhag par rgyal ba thams cad bskyed pa'i yum// rdo rje phag mo gsang ba'i mdzod 'dzin ma// sa la dge slong ma yis rab grags pa// sprul pa'i gar gyis gsang ba
'dzin par mdzad//ces pa ltar/ bka' babs nyi shu rtsa gsum ni/ bzo rig gi bka' babs mnga' ris pa bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan/ gso rig gi bka' babs byang pa rnam rgyal grags bzang
/ snyan ngag gi bka' babs ngam rings

pa dka' bcu pa dpal ldan bzang po/ tha snyad gtsug lag gi bka' babs dpal e'i bka' bcu pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / tshad ma rig pa'i bka' babs stag lung dka' bzhi pa manydzu shrI/
'dul ba'i bka' babs gung thang pa dpal ldan seng ge/mngon pa'i bka' babs gsang phu ba bzod pa blo gros rgya mtsho/ phar phyin bka' babs gung thang pa rgyal mtshan dkon
mchog/ byams chos kyi bka' babs sa skya bka' bcu pa mchog gi blo gros/ dbu ma'i bka' babs bka' bzhi pa shar mgon/ spyod 'jug gi bka' babs sa skya byang sems gzhon nu rgyal
mchog/ 'chad pa'i bka' babs smar khams pa grags pa bzang po/ rtsod pa'i bka' babs shel dkar ba thugs rje dpal bzang / rtsom pa'i bka' babs rtse thang pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ btsun pa'i bka' babs gung thang pa ma ti bi dza ya dm: blo gros rnam rgyal/ srid pa las grol ba'i bka' babs rgyal khams kyi spong ba pa yon tan seng ge/ mos gus
kyi bka' babs sku zhang 'jam dbyangs chos rje/ rgyud rdo rje phreng ba'i bka' babs rtse thang pa mkhan chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ gar gyi bka' babs bo dong pa dar ma
seng ge/ sde snod gsum gyi bka' babs shel dkar ba dpal ldan sangs rgyas/ rgyud sde bzhi'i bka' babs stag lung thang pa bka' drug pa ngag dbang grags pa/ rtogs pa'i bka' babs
rang dbon glang 'khor ba ngag dbang rgyal mtshan/ bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi bka' babs shel dkar ba 'jam dpal grags pa dang nyer gsum mo//'khon gyi gdung rgyud gsum ni/
bdag po grags pa blo gros/ grags pa rdo rje/ theg chen pa'i dbon po bde legs bkra shis pa gsum mo//

sngags 'chang ba'i khyu mchog gcig pu ni/ rdo rje 'dzin pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan no//nyi ma dang zla ba ltar grags pa gnyis ni/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang po dang / spang
lo'i [dpang] sku skyer grags pa blo gros brtan pa gnyis so//'jig rten gyi mig gsum ni/ e'i lo tsA ba bsod nams bzang po/ lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ lo tsA ba thugs
rje dpal te gsum mo//phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi mkhas pa drug ni/ bo dong stag sde pa dol pa rgyal mtshan grags/ spyi bo lhas kyi mkhan po bshes gnyen nyi ma/ rtse thang
pa chos kyi grags pa/ gsang phu ba bka' bcu pa padma bzang po/ snar thang pa dge 'dun grub pa/ shangs chos 'khor sgang pa'i mkhan chen bka' bcu pa shes rab rin chen te drug//mdo
sngags yongs rdzogs bcu ni/ bo dong rta ra'i chen po rin chen chos bzang ba/ dol pa rgyal bzang / bo dong grang mo chei rgyal grags/ grang mo che'i chen po sher
grags/ stag sde pa sher dpal/ sgro smon can gyi bla ma kun dpal/ bo dong rta ra'i chen po 'jam dkar/ bo dong grang mo che'i chen po seng ge rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon chos kyi
nyi ma/ gsang phu rong chung shes rab dpal/ dka' bcu pa ratna shrI/ rje'i dbon po shel dkar mkhan chen rje btsun pa/ ngam rings rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas seng ge ste bcu'o//
(gsum lhag)kha che bsod snyom pa'i gdan sa pa gnyis ni/ tshogs chen po'i mkhan po

don grub dpal 'byor dang / dge 'dun sgang pa'i mkhan po seng ge dpal gnyis so//gtsug rgyan bcu drug ni dam pa rgya gar gyi gdan sa pa glang 'khor chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
pan chen 'bum phrag gsum pa'i gdan sa pa mkhan chen nam mkha' rin chen/ yang de'i mkhan po nyid kyi dbon po bshes gnyen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ ngam rings mkhan chen
bsod nams skyabs/ yang de'i mkhan po dkon khang pa nyi ma/ mngon dga'i chos dpon 'jam dbyangs kun legs/ de'i mkhan po rgyal mtshan blo gros/ nyang stod bde chen gyi mkhan
po dkon mchog bzang po/ byams chen gyi mkhan po sku skye/ 'dzim pa'i mkhan po bkra shis rin chen/ mkhan chen lha'i rgyal po/ 'dus pa 'bring gi rtsom yig pa nam mkha' rgyal
mtshan/ 'phags pa nam snying / 'dar mkhan chen bde gshegs rgyal mtshan/ dge 'dun sgang pai mkhan po byang chub mchog ldan te bcu drug go//mdo rab 'byams pa bzhi ni/ gsang
phu go rab 'byams pa/ shel dkar ba yon tan rgya mtsho/ byams chen rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas 'phel/ mnga' ris pa nam mkha' bsod nams dang bzhi'o//sngags rams pa gnyis
ni/ shab lhun rtse ba kun mkhyen 'phags 'od dang / rmog lcog pa'i gdan sa ba sangs rgyas dpal gnyis so//sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa bzhi ni/ jo gdan ras chen gzhon
nu dpal/ chos rje brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ la phyi ba nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/

grub pa'i rgyal mo bsod nams 'bum dang bzhi'o//sngags 'chang drag po gnyis ni/ ngam rings kyi A nanata dang / gung thang gi bla chen chos dpal bzang po/dka' bcu stong phrag
ni bsod nams blo gros sogs so//dka' bcu stong phrag zung ni/ mu srad dka' bzhi pa sogs so//phar tshad khri phrag brgal ba ni/ de dus kyi bshes gnyen phal che ba'o//sgrub
chen lnga bcu ni/ rnal 'byor pa rdo rje phag mo sogs so//des dpang lo chen po'i/ bo dong e'i gdan seng ge'i khri la 'khod pa yin la/ de'i snag gi dbon po pan chen 'di nyid
do/ dbon rgyud de dag gis rim par bzung zhing bo dong pa zhes snyan par grags so//des na lo 'di ni pan chen 'di byon pa'i sbrul nas brgya dang brgyad cu rtsa brgyad yin
la/ pan chen 'di/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin kun dga' rnam gnyis las/ lo bdun gyis bgres shing rong ston chen po las lo bco brgyad kyis gzhon no/ mnga' ris bla
chen chos dpal bzang po lcags mo phag lo ba ste/ pan chen 'di nyid las lo lngas bgres/ A nan ta pa chu pho byi lo pa ste pan chen 'di bas lo bzhis bgres pa tsam yin no/ pan
chen 'dis don bdun bzhugs/sum stong lnga brgya dang bcu 'das pa'i bcu gcig pa shing mo glang (sa pho rta) spyi lo 1378la/ sum stong lnga brgya dang bcu bzhi 'das pa'i
bco lnga pa

chu pho khyi spyi lo 1382 la dpal ldan sa skya'i bstan 'dzin kun dga' rnam gnyis byon// (skabs 'di'i 'khrungs lo'i tshig 'gros la gzhigs na kun dga' bzang po sngon dang kun
dga' rgyal mtshan rjes la byon par ngos 'dzin dgos 'dra yang / ngor chen kun dga' bzang po 'di nyid byi ba lor sku 'das pa dang / gsham du mus chen gyi lo rgyus skabs mus
chen las dgung lo drug gis bgres pa sku 'das pa'i lo de yang me byi lo yin pa gsal por bkod pa des na chu khyi spyi lo 1382 lor bltams/ dgung lo don lnga pa me byi spyi
o 1456 lor sku 'das pa kha tshon bcad chog pas thog mar kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang / de rjes ngor chen kun dga' bzang po bltams par ngos 'dzin dgos 'dra ba da dung dpyad
par 'tshal/ spe sgrig pas)unauditedde yang rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po ni/ sa skya tshogs kyi nye gnas dpon tshang grums yon tan gyi sras su bltams/ lo dgu pa la/ shar
pa ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis mkhan po/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros kyis slob dpon mdzad de tshigs snga ma gnyis nod/ de nas bzung ste/ lo nyi shu rtsa lnga bzhes
kyi bar du gtso cher shar chen po'i zhabs pad bsten te rgyud man ngag zab chos blangs/ shar chen pas mkhan po/ mkhan chen blo gros dpal bas las slob/ sa bzang 'phags
pas gsangs ton bgyis te bsnyen par rdzogs par mdzad/ rdor dkar gdan gcig kho na mdzad cing nyes rdung gi dris mas dben/ gzhan yang sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros la
rdo rje 'phreng ba sogs rgyud sde'i bshad srol mang du gsan/ mkhan chen g.yag pa la rnam rig sogs rigs pa'i gsang tshig gnad du dril ba gsan/

sa skya sgo rum gyi rje btsun gong ma'i gsung rab la lo gsum gyi bar du gzigs rtog nan tan du mdzad pas/ chos spyi dang khyad par dpal dan sa skya pa'i zab don gyi gnad la
phyin ci ma log pa'i go ba phul byung bsnyes/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims pa la kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi bka' gsan pas/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i 'jug sgo thog
ma yin zhes mi 'phrog pai dad pa thong / dgung lo nyer lnga pa'i tshe shar chen pa zhi bar gshegs te/ gsung ngag rin po che'i bdud rtsi sngar ma gsol bas/ thugs kyi 'dun
pa cher g.yos te/ shangs chos khor sgang du lo chen skyabs mchog drung du lhags pa na/ mdo rgyud zab rgyas kyi chos mang dag dang snang gsum gyi khrid rim tsam las thugs
kyi re ba ma rdzogs pa na/ dus de'i tshe mtshan gyi 'od gsal chen po'i ngang las/ bla ma kun dga' bzang po lam 'bras zhu na 'di na yar byon zer ba gcig byung bas de na
phar byon pas/ ri 'bor gcig na/ dang ra sgo byang bstan rtsig pa khrol le ba gcig gi nang / khang pa sgo shar bstan gcig gi skas la 'dzegs byon pas/ skas mgo nas dge bshes
sha rtsi smug po byas pa gcig gis spos sna byas byon pas/ tshoms kha lhor bstan gcig na bla ma sku bgres se ba ber thul mnab pa gcig dang mjal te zag med kyi dga' ba
chen po myong ba gcig byung / phyis dpal ldan sa skyar byon/ gsung ngag gi rtsad bcad pas chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims dpal la gsung ngag yongs rdzogs kyi slob ma'i gtso
bo gsum gyi shar chen pa ni zhi bar gshegs/ mi nyag rin rdor ni mdo khams la bzhud/ grub chen buddha nyid 'os su gzigs te/ dgung lo nyer bdun pa sa pho byi lo zhig dgon
du byon pas/ 'od gsal du ji ltar shar

ba de mngon sum du gyur pas/ mos gus kyis bsam pa tshims te lus nyams mnan gyis mi bzod pa cher skyes/ byi ba dang glang gi lo de nyid du gdan phab/ stag lo chos rje buddha/
sa skya dang sa bzang gnyis su chos 'khor bskor ba'i tshe'ang zhabs pad la btud de/ gsung ngag gi bdud rtsi sogs snying bcud la tshim par rol/ dgung lo zhe brgyad yan la
sa skya/ sa bzang sogs gnas nges med du/ gsung ngag sogs zab rgyas kyis dga' ston so sor spel/ de nas gnas kyi brtag pa mdzad pa na/ e wam chos ldan gyi ri khrod de 'od
gsal la gsal por shar gang na yod ma nges la/ khyod kyi dgon pa don grub kyis ston pa yod zer ba 'od gsal la shar/ phyis nyag brel don grub zer bas/ gnas de'i yon tan bsngags
pas/ dgung lo zhe brgyad pa sa mo bya la e wam chos ldan gyi dgon pa chen po btab/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i rgyud man ngag dang / rgyud sde bzhi'i bstan pa spyi khyab
dang / khyad par bya spyod kyi bstan pa la/ rje 'di kho na bka' drin che ba yin no//rje 'di nyid kyis dbang khrid gdams pa'i sgo bye ba phrag brgya phye/ gsung ngag rin
po che lam 'bras tshar gsum gyis lhag pa'i bcu phrag brgyad gnang / bsnyen par rdzogs pa khri ral pa can gyis mkhan po mdzad/ dge 'dun gyi sde gsar btsugs kyang / glo bor
dge 'dun stong phrag 'du ba'i chos sde/ chu 'dus su lnga brgya 'du ba/ steng khyebs su nyis brgya 'du ba/ gu ger brgya phrag sogs dang / e wam chos ldan du gsung ngag pa
stong phrag 'du ba sogs su bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa dar rgyas mdzad/mthar don lnga pa byi lo sa zla'i nyer lnga la gshegs/ zla ba tshes 'phral rje mus chen gyis gsung ngag
btsugs/ phyi nang gi rten bzhengs

pa sogs mdzad do//sngags kyi bstan pa spel ba'i slob ma'i grangs kyang / bu ston rin po che dang rje 'di gnyis las lhag pa med pas bgrang bar mi spobs kyang / gtso bo bsdu
na/ bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu chen po bcu ni/ sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog/ smar khams pa grags pa bzang po/ chos rje gzhon nu seng ge/ byams chen rab 'byams pa
sangs rgyas 'phel/ pan chen shAkya mchog ldan/ kun mkhyen go rab 'byams pa bsod nams seng ge/ pan chen 'bum phrag gsum pa/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' chos bzang / thugs sras kyi
gtso bo sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan (gcig chad)/gzhan yang gung ru shes rab bzang po/ nyag bre rgyun sgul ba pan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dpal gyi rgyal
mtshan/ kun mkhyen dga' gdong pa/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ bzod chen phyogs as rnam rgyal sogs so//bstan 'dzin dam pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan ni/ lo tsA ba zhang
ye shes sde sogs byon pa'i rigs rgyud/ dbon po nor 'phel gyi sras su/ dpal ldan sa skya'i mthong smon bla brang du chu pho byi [khyi] lo de nyid la byon/ lo lnga pa la bo
dong phyogs las rnam rgyal las dge bsnyen nod/ bcu pa la shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan la dge tshul nod/ kun dga' rgyal mtshan zhes btags/ nyi shu pa la theg chen chos rjes
mkhan po dang / shar yes slob dpon mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ tshad ma rigs gter rtsa 'grel la shin tu byang bas/

mtshan 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i dpal zhes theg chen pas gsol bar mdzad/ bo dong er bla ma kun dga' bzang po lo bdun tsam bsten/ tshad ma sogs la sbyong bshad mdzad/ lo bcu gsum
pa la gdan sa chen por grwa skor mdzad/ mkhan chen g.yag pa la phar phyin Tika chen po rtsom pa'i rtsom yig pa mdzad de/ Tika chen brtsams pa dang / yi ger 'bri ba/ thugs
la zin pa dang gsum dus mnyam du byung bas/ phar phyin legs par mkhyen/ de'i tshe mkhan chen pa bar skabs ngal gso ba'i ched du gnal cung zad mdzad de/ sad res kyi da
len yang kho bos dga' ldan du phyin/ byams pa dang mjal zhes yang yang gsung ba yin zer/ theg chen chos rje'i drung du gsung ngag sogs zab rgyas kyi gdams pa nod/ zhang
bla chen kun rgyal/ sa bzang pa gzhon nu blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan don grub sogs las rgyud man ngag mang du gsan/ phyis byang nas 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rin chen gyis spyan
drangs te/ dpal ldan sa skya'i zab chos mang po sgo phye/ dpal ngam rings kyi chos sde dang / ya ga chos sdings zhes grags pa/ nor bu gling pa'i grwa tshang gi 'dzin
skyong yang gnang / yos lor ngam rings su mgon khang bzhengs dus/ lha khang ka gnyis ma la logs bris skya ris ja sbyor gcig gi ngo la gnang / blo bzang dkar mor grags pa'i
grub chen blo gros bzang po la/ gsung ngag sa lugs dang / zha lugs sogs gsan pas thugs skyed thon par byung / grub chen des kyang / bde mchog sogs zab rgyas kyi gdams
pa zhus/ mtshan gyi 'od gsal chen po las/ rje btsun gong ma lnga'i zhal gzigs te/ rgyal ba'i mdun na rgyal sras sbyin pa dpal// zhes sogs/ sho lo ka lngas bstod

cing phyag 'tshal ba/ 'od gsal las bzhengs pa'i tshe yang gsal bar dran/ deng sang ya ga chos ldings na yang rgyun du 'don par mdzad do/ mdor na 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi
sgo nas [bstan pa] ches cher gsal bar mdzad de/ nga lam 'bras pa mkhas pa yin/ ni gu ba rgod po yin/ sbyor drug pa nyams myong can zhes gsung ba yin zer ro/ slob ma'i mchog
kyang sngags 'char A nan ta pa/ bdag chen dpal ldan chos skyong / sems dpa' gzhon nu rgyal mchog mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang po la sogs pa mang du byon te/ slar yang
lo re lnga pa me pho 'brug (stag) gi lo khrums zla ba'i nyer brgyad la gshegs so/ A nan ta pa chu pho byi lo la rje btsun kun rgyal ba lo bcus bgres brgyad cu rtsa gsum
bzhugs/ mkhas pa dge bzang sa mo glang A nan ta pa las lo nyer gsum gyis bgres te re gcig bzhugs/ mnyam med dpal ldan chos skyong lcags pho stag lo pa rje kun rgyal las
so brgyad kyis gzhon lo zhe gsum bzhugs 'dug go/'das lo nas sum stong lnga brgya dang nyi shu 'das pa'i nyer gcig pa sa pho 'brug spyi lo 13889/ mus stod gling skyar mus
chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan byon/ dgung lo dgu pa la/ dbang 'od pas mkhan po mdzad de rab tu byung / bco lnga par gle lung mkhan po kun smon dang / zur chos pa byang seng
gnyis la phar phyin spyod 'jug sogs sbyangs/ bco brgyad pa la bshad ston mdzad/ nyi shu pa la nam mkha'i rnal 'byor la gcod khrid gsan/ nyer gcig pa la ngam rings su/ blo
gros rgyal mtshan pa dang / sang lo pa'i drung du phar phyin

sogs sbyangs/ lo gsum nas der grwa skor mdzad/ nyer bzhi pa la lhor/ mkhas mchog thugs rje dpal ba'i drung du phar phyin gyi dka' gnad la dpyad/ sa skyar grwa skor mdzad/ nyer
lnga pa la shel dkar du mkhas pa g.yag pa dang mjal/ lho'i nags 'dabs khu lung du zla ba gnyis/ ngam rings su zla ba gnyis/ tsha snang zla ba gnyis te zla ba drug bsten
phar phyin gyi gnad zab mo nyams su myong / nyer bdun pa la g.yag pa mkha' spyod du bzhud/ nyer brgyad pa la mu gu lung du sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog gnyis
lo bdun bsten/ tshad ma 'u yug pa'i rigs mdzod chen po sogs la sbyangs/ so gnyis pa la ngam rings su chos rje rong chen pa la phar tshad kyi gnad zab mo gsan/ so bzhi pa
la byang du bka' lnga pa dpal 'byor shes rab la dbu ma red mda' pa'i lung gsan/ so lnga pa stag lor lha sar skor ba 'bum ther mdzad/ yar lam nub chos lung du gangs chen
kun dga' dpal las bsnyen par rdzogs/ so brgyad pa 'brug lo dpal ldan sa skyar/ rje ngor pa'i drung du bde dgyes kyi lam zab mo gsan thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ so dgu pa sbrul
lor theg chen chos rje gshegs/ der dpon slob kyis brtag gnyis bshad pa dang sbyor drug gi gnad zab mo la nyams len mdzad/ bzhi bcu rta lor dpal ldan sa skya der gsung
ngag rin po che'i zab don nyams su myong / slar yang zhe gnyis pa sa spre lo nas zla ba bdun du gsung ngag rin po che'i zab mthil phyin par gsan/ zhe gnyis pa sa mo bya nas
ngor dgon gsar 'debs pa'i mkhar las dang / zab don nyams len zung 'jug tu mdzad cing / rje 'dis de'i tshe brtag gnyis rnam bshad kyi dga' ston legs par skyed/ de

nas bzung ste rje 'di'i re brgyad dang / rje ngor chen don bzhi bzhes pa'i bar ngor dang mus su byon res kyis/ rgyud man ngag gi bstan pa'i me ro sor chud par mdzad/ zhe dgu
pa 'brug lor lha gong du kye rdo rje'i bsnyen pa zla ba bcu gsum du 'bum phrag bcu gcig gnang / nga dgu pa stag lor/ rje ngor pa nub chos lung du phebs/ rje 'di la/ ngor
du lam 'bras 'dus pa'i tshogs la bdag med ma'i dbang bka' dang 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi rten 'brel zab mo sgrigs shig gsung ba ltar rten 'brel bsgrigs/ rje 'di'i re dgu
pa/ rje ngor chen don lnga pa me pho byi lo sa ga zla ba'i nyer bzhi la ngor gyi gdan seng ge'i khri la 'khod/ lo de la rje rdo rje 'chang dag pa'i dbyings su gshegs/ de
nas byi glang stag gsum 'dzin skyong gi khur bzhes gnang / don gnyis pa stag lo rin spungs nor bzang la bde mchog sogs kyi dbang gnang / yar lam mus su ya ma'i dgon pa btab/
don gsum pa 'brug lor mus bstan 'dzin phug tu bde mchog gi bsnyen pa gnang / ston ta'i si tu rnam rgyal grags pa yab sras la bde kyes kyi dbang gnang / don bzhi pa sbrul
lor ngamngar rings su 'dus tshogs la gsung ngag dang blo sbyong sogs kyi dga' ston gnang / don lnga pa rta lor rgyam pa ngor gyi gdan khrir bzhag don bdun pa sprel lor
bsam gtanbstan 'dzin phug tu bdud rtsi ril bu bsgrubs/ 'od gsal chen po'i ngang du rnal 'byor dbang phyug zhal gzigs/ brgyad cu rtsa gnyis pa smin drug zla ba'i tshes
brgyad la mus bstan 'dzin phug tu dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/ bstan 'dzin kyi bu slob bkrang bar mi bgrod kyang / gsung ngag

bshad kyi bka' babs ni bdag chen rdo rje 'chang ma ti hAtstsha shrI bha dra kho na'o/ sum stong lnga brgya dang nyi shu rtsa gsum 'das pa'i rtsa bzhi pa lcags mo lug spyi lo
1391thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub dpal ldan sa skya'i gung ru ba zhes pa'i 'brog gnas su byon/ 'brog ma tshugs par kha yul chags te rdzi bo sogs kyang mdzad/ lo bco
lnga pa la dpal ldan snar thang gi gdan sa bcu bzhi pa grub pa shes rab las rab tu byung ste/ thos bsam gyi gzhi btsugs/ nyi shu pa la snar thang gi gtsug lag khang du grub
pa shes rab de nyid las bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyer lnga pa shing mo lug lor dbus la byon te/ khra 'brug tu sems dpa' chen po kun bzang la dbu tshad/ thang po cher rong ston
shAkya rgyal mtshan la phar phyin gsan/ bkra shis rdo khar rje btsun tsong kha pa chen po dang mjal te/ grangs nges rnam 'byed sogs gsan/ gsang pur shes seng la phar
tshad sogs gsan/ gro sar dmar ston dpal ldan rin chen dang rgya mtsho rin chen gnyis la 'dul ba gsan te/ me pho rta'i bar lo bcu gnyis dbus su bzhugs/ me pho rta la gtsang
la byon/ bang chen sogs su 'chad nyan mdzad/ bzhi bcu pa lcags pho khyi la 'jug pa'i rnam bshad mdzad/ zhe gcig phag lo la stod lho shel dkar sogs su chos dbyar bteg mkhas
grub dpal sangs rgyas dang bgro gleng mdzad/ padma chos sdings su bo dong phyogs las rnam rgyal la sgrol ma'i dbang sogs gsan/ zhe gsum pa chu mo glang la rtsa she'i
rnam bshad mdzad/ nyid kyi lnga bcu rtsa bdun pa me mo yos la bkra shis lhun po'i chos grwa chen po btab ste/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan pa rin po che gsal bar mdzad/
brgyad cu rtsa bzhi pa shing mo rta lo tshes brgyad la zhi

ba'i dbyings su gshegs so/sum stong lnga brgya dang lnga bcu rtsa drug 'das pa'i nga bdun pa shing pho 'brug spyi lo 1424lor mtshungs med rdo rje rgyal mtshan chag skyar skya'i
phu'i 'brog gseb tu byon/ theg chen chos rje don drug bzhes pa'i lo de yin/ 'di nyid byams chen rab 'byams pa las lo bcu gsum gyis gzhon/ paN shAka pa las bzhi dang
/ kun mkhyen go rams las lo lngas bgres/ zla ba gnyis nas mnga' ris gung thang du spyan drangs/ lo brgyad pa la glang 'khor ba manydzu shrI las rab byung mdzad/ dgu pa la/
sha ra ba'i dngos slob kun smon mdzes pa'i dpal gyis btab pa'i dgon pa mus srad kyi gdan seng ge'i khri la zhabs bsten/ lo gsum gyi bar du chos rje yon tan mgon po las
rta mgrin yang gsang sogs gsan/ bcu gcig pa shing pho stag lor/ gung thang gi chos grags/ bla chen chos dpal bzang po lo re bzhi bzhes pa'i tshe zhabs pad bsten/ lo drug
gi bar du rgyud gsum gyi gsan stong sogs dpal ldan sa skya'i gsung rab dri med pa thugs la smin/ lo bco brgyad pa lcags mo bya lor/ dpal ngam rings kyi chos grwar rdo rje
'chang A nan ta ma ti lo bdun cu pa zhig dang / mnyam med dpal ldan chos skyong gi lo so gnyis pa zhig gi zhabs la gtugs te/ A nan ta pa las/ lo nag dril gsum/ 'jigs byed
rwa lugs/ phag mo skor gsum/ chos skyong gi man ngag sogs dang / bdag chen dpal chos drung du rgyud gsum las byung ba'i dbang bka' bcu bdun sogs dang / bde kyes kyi bka'
du ma gsan/ bcu dgu pa la sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog pas mkhan po dang / nam mkha' lhun bzang pas slob dpon mdzad

de/ bsnyen par rdzogs zer/ nyer gcig pa la gung thang gi dpal ri 'dabs kyi dgon par sems dpa' chen po rgyal mtshan dkon mchog lo nga bdun pa zhig gi drung du/ gsung ngag lam
skor dang bcas pa dang / gsang 'dus mi bskyod lugs kyi dbang bka' 'gos lugs dang / bshad bka' bo dong lugs dang / nag khrid dmar khrid sogs nod/ bzhi bcu pa la gung thang
gi chos grwar shAkya bha dra lo gya brgyad pa zhig la/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i dbang bshad man ngag mang du nod/ zhe lnga pa la mus srad kyi bstan 'dzin gling du rin chen
chos sde legs pa lo don gnyis lon pa zhig la/ gur si sbyong rgyud sogs kyi dbang bshad man ngag mang du gsan/ bo dong phyogs las rnam rgyal dang / bde chen rnam rgyal
grags bzang la dus 'khor dbang sogs gsan/ zhe dgu pa la dpal ldan sa skyar gdan phebs/ thog mar sa skya sman grong du/ zhi khro sogs rnying ma'i chos 'khor mang du bskor/
de nas nyi thog dang zhe dgon sogs su bzhugs/ de nas grang mo che pa'i brgya dpon chos rje kun bsam pas/ bla ma mnyam med pa dang / chos rje gzungs pa nas brgyud pa'i chos
rgyud dri ma med pa bzhugs par dgongs nas bla brang che mor spyan drangs gdan phab ste/ dgung lo lnga bcu pa nas zhi bar gshegs kyi bar gnas de nyid du zab don nyams bzhes
dang 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan pa rin po che gsal bar mdzad/ de yang rtsom ni rgyud man ngag lag len/ spyi 'gro gsal byed de gsal byed rnam bzhi/ bla ma 'phags
pa/ bla ma dam pa/ phyag len/ bka' sgrub ste sgrub pa rnam bzhi/ bir srungs 'khrul sel sogs 'khrul sel rnam

bzhi dang / chu rgyun rnam bzhi sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad/ thugs sras bstan 'dzin byon tshul yang / snga tshar la gnag tshar ba/ ba 'brog rdor gling gi gdan sa ba 'jam
dbyangs bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje nyid kyi gcung rtogs ldan blo gros bzang po/ de nyid kyi sku zhang dka' bcu pa dkon mchog bzang po/
chen po rin chen rgyal mtshan/ de nyid kyi dbon po si ra ba nam mkha' rin chen dang drug bar tshar la/ byang pa bdag chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ me nyag chos grags/ 'dzam
bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ grang mo che'i mkhan po kun bsam/ bo dong bka' bcu pa chos rin/ jo nang pa chos skyong / shangs pa kun dga' dpal ldan dang bdun/phyi tshar la/
bdag chen rgya gar ba shes rab rgyal mtshan/ bdag po bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rje rin po che byams pa dkon mchog dpal/ 'dzim pa kun dga' snying po/ nyid kyi dbon po kun rin/
grang mo che'i gdan sa ba nam mkha' dpal/ sdom btson shes rab rin chen/ rab 'byams pa lha dbang / rgyud man ngag gnyi ka tshar ba'i sa dkar ba/ mus chen rnam rgyal bzang
po dang bcu'o/ rje 'di nyid rigs kyang phun sum tshogs pa gtsang gi rigs yin zhing / sngar dar gyi tshe/ rgya nag nas jo bo shAkya mu ne spyan 'dren pa'i gyad pa mi bzhi'i
ya gcig gi brgyud pa yin la/ 'di rigs las byon pa yang sad mi bdun gyi gtsang de wa intra rakSha zhes bya ba dang / phyi dar gyi rtsa ba g.yo dmar gtsang gsum gyi gtsang
rab gsal zhes bya ba dang / de rjes gtsang ban

rdor mo zhes bya ba rnying ma'i grub thob chen po dang / de nas rnam grol ba kun rin zhes bya ba sgyu 'phrul sde brgyad sogs la mnga' bsnyes pa'i mkhas grub chen po sogs mang
du byon no/ thug dam gyi rim pa yang / tho rengs lam zab bir srungs thun mong min pa/ de nas mchod gtor rgyas pa dang 'brel ba'i lam yab la brten pa'i lam dus rgyas pa/
de nas dkar chab bzhi dang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg de nas gsol ba/ de nas mchod gtor 'brang dang 'brel ba'i lam dus 'bring po/ de nas yul dang / gur regs sdus/
sam Ta'i mtshon bya can man ngag lung la brten pa'i lam dus rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ de nas gung tshigs/ de nas zab tshang mchad pa dang rtsom pa sogs mdzad/ de nas mchod
gtor rgyas pa lam dus rgyas pa/ sgrub pa lung sbyin gyi nyams bzhes sogs mdzad do/ mdor na rang gzhan gyi don mthar phyin te don lnga pa nyer bzhi la dag pa'i dbyings
su dpal ldan sa skya'i grang mo che de nyid du gshegs so/sum stong lnga brgya dang zhe gsum 'das pa'i zhe bzhi pa lcags mo yos spyi lo 1411lor/ bstan pa'i gsal byed byams
chen rab 'byams pa rong gi snar rdo spe zhes par byon/ lo bdun pa la chos 'khor sgang du seng ge rgyal mtshan las rab tu byung / bcu gsum pa %sum la %gsang phu ne'u thog
tu phyag phebs/ shangs ston rin chen grub pa la gsan pa mdzad cing / bcu bzhi pa la mngon dga'i chos grwar dka' ba'i grwa skor gnang bas skyog po dka' bzhi par grags/ bco
brgyad par rtse thang mnyam sogs

su dka' bcu'i grwa skor gnang zhing / gsung phu'i chos lung spyi khang bzhugs sa mdzad pas chos lung dka' bcu pa zhes grags/ bcu dgu pa la mkhyen rab dbang phyug gi grwa sar
phyag phebs/ lo bcu bzhugs te/ nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa la po ti bzhi bcu rtsa lngas thog drangs pa'i gzhung lugs rab 'byams la/ dpal ldan sa skyar bshad pa'i dga' ston spel
bas byams chen rab 'byams pa zhes grags/gzhan yang rong ston smra ba'i seng ge/ sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog rong chung sher dpal sogs la mdo phyogs kyi gsan
pa rgya cher mdzad/ e waM chos ldan du rdo rje 'chang gis mkhan po/ rje 'khor lo ldom pas las gsang / mkhas pa gzhon seng gis dus go bar mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan
slob gnyis las gsung ngag rin po ches gtsos pa'i bde dgyes gsang gsum gyi rgyud man ngag gi bcud chen po blangs/ de nas 'di ltar dgongs te/ dben pa'i bdud rtsis nyin mtshan
'da' ba rje mi la lta bu'am/ 'dus pa'i tshogs la rna ba'i bdud rtsis nyin mtshan 'da' ba rje blo ldan shes rab lta bu gang yang rung ba'i rnam thar la zhugs par bya
yi/ gzhan ni bdag gi cha ma yin no/ 'on kyang de gnyis gang zhig bstan pa la phan par lung bstan du gsol zhes bla ma dkon mchog dpang du gsol ba'i brtag pa mdzad pa na/
'od gsal gyi ngang der/ rgyal gyi shrI yin zer ba'i rir/ lung gi chos po ti brag ri gtams pa pha mtha' mngon sum zhig gi brda don bsam pas 'chad pa'i sgra dbyangs bstan 'gro'i
dpal du dgongs te/ thog mar nA lendra'i chos grwar 'dus pa'i tshogs ha cang mi mang

ba zhig la 'chad pa'i bdud rtsi spel/ slar sum cu rtsa brgyad pa 'brug gi lo la kha reg bod 'brug tu bstan pa'i gzhi btsugs/ 'chad nyan 'brug gi sgra ltar mtho bas/ rong ston
chen po'i zhal gyi bdud rtsi las/ 'brug gsum 'dzoms pas gangs can 'dir snyan grags kyis khyab par 'gyur zhes lung bstan/ slar nyid kyi so dgu pa sa mo sbrul gyi zla ba
dang po la 'dus pa'i tshogs brgya phrag gnyis dang bcas sa yi bdag po rin spungs nor bu bzang pos mthun pa'i rkyen sbyar te 'bras yul skyed tshal du 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum
gyis rgyal ba'i bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar byas pa yin no/ mdor na/ lo bco brgyad pa nas don lnga'i bar bstan pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod kho nas dus 'da' bar byed/ lo
lnga bcu rtsa brgyad du 'chad pa'i rgyun bsrings pa yin no/ /zhes grags te/ mthar don lnga pa shing mo sbrul snron zla ba'i tshes gcig la gshegs so/ slob ma'i mchog bstan
'dzin chen po bgrang bar mi bzod cing / skyed tshal nyid las mched pa'i grwa sa chen po yang thub bstan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling de las mched pa yangs pa can dang gnyis/
mnyan yod bya gshongs dang / chos 'khor lhun po/ gzha' ri dgon gsar ba rtsa ba nyid dang grwa sa chen po drug po 'di nyid kyis kyang 'dzam gling 'di mdzes par byas pa
ma yin nam/ bstan 'dzin gyi thugs sras mkhas grub bstan gsal/ rtse thang sangs rgyas lhun/ go rab 'byams pa/ 'bum phrag gsum pa/ byams pa chos don grub/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs
kun dga' chos bzang sogs so/ des na shing pho byi lo 'di byams chen rab 'byams pa byon pa'i lcags mo yos nas brgya

dang lnga bcu rtsa bzhi pa yin no/ sum stong lnga brgya dang drug cu 'das pa'i re gcig pa sa pho sprel spyi lo 1428 lor paN chen shAkya mchog ldan gsang phu'i bar tshigs zhes
par byon/ lo brgyad pa'i tshe rong ston chen po skyor mo lung du byon pa'i zhabs phyir bar ma rab tu byung ba'i mtshan shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blor gsol/ bcu
pa la nA lendrar dge tshul du bsgrubs shing / de nas nyer gcig gi bar rong ston chen po'i zhal gyi bdud rtsi nyams su myong zhing / rgyan drug mchog gi gzhung la sbyangs/
nyer lnga'i tshe ngor du ngor chen/ brag dkar sems dpa' chen po/ mus chen gsum gyis mkhan po dang las gsang mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan slob de gsum/ lcang lung
pa gzhon nu blo gros/ paN chen nags rin sogs las/ gsung ngag sbyor drug sogs zab rgyas kyi chos tshul nod/ lo bco lnga pa la gsang phu'i gnas sgo grwa tshang gi 'dzin bdag
gnang / phyis rje ngor pas bkas gnang ste/ dpal ldan sa skyar gzhung lugs brgya la bshad pa'i dga' ston dang / gau sgra las drangs pa'i gnas bstod dang nga brgyad ma sogs
mdzad/ rig gnas lnga la snyan pa'i grags pas khyab/ nyid kyi zhes gnyis pa sa mo glang la paN chen don yod dpal ba'i bkas bskul te/ gser mdog can du 'dus tshogs brgya
phrag bdun la 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan pa spel te/ dgun chos la mngon pa gong 'og dpyid chos la dbu ma/ dbyar chos la 'dul ba gtso bor 'doms par mdzad/ mnga' ris
su chos rgyal bkra shis mgon gyis dpon slob sum brgya tsam spyan drangs pa'i tshe/ kun mkhyen rdzong dkar ba sdom rigs la 'chad pa'i dbyangs

snyan sgrogs pa'i snyan pas mtshams sbyar te/ sdom pa gsum la dka' gnad dpyod pa'i dri ba brgya rtsa brgyad pa mdzad/ shar lam byang ngam rings su 'dus pa'i tshogs kyi bsu
ba bsnyen bkur sogs mdzad/ chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags pa la dus 'khor gyi dbang sogs gsan/ slar gser mdog can du dri lan gser gyi thur ma mdzad/ lar 'di'i dri lan gyi bstan
bcos bcu phrag gcig gi sgo nas kyang bstan pa dkar por bgyis pa lags so/yongs 'dzin bcu phrag bzhi la gsan pa rgya cher mdzad/ blo brtan bzhi pa dang de'i nye gnas blo
ldan pa'i drung du ka tsan snyan ngag sogs sbyangs shing / yongs rdzogs paNDi ta chen por 'gyur/ spyir rig gnas lnga dang / khyad par sgra rig dang / nang rig gi snying
po/ bka' bar mtha' dang / lugs gnyis kyi srol las byung ba'i rang stong gzhin stong gi lta ba'i gnad zab mo la 'di kho na bka' drin che ba yin/ zha lu mkhyen rab chos rjes
'od gsal gyi ngang las bstan 'dzin chen po rnams la gzigs pa stsal bas/ byams chen rab 'byams pa/ mtshan dus sgron me 'bar te phyogs bzhir po ti bkram ste gzigs rtog gnang
zhing mtha' bram gzugs kyis bskor ba zhig gzigs/ paN chen 'di ni sku'i ngo bo mi snang zhing / steng gi nam mkha' la gser gyi rdo rje gzi 'od 'bar ba dang / gtor ma
la me 'od 'bar ba gzigs pa de yang / lta ba zab mo mnga' ba'i mtshon byed do zhes grags so/ mnga' ris 'khor 'phral 'du khang rnying pa dang / phyis gsar pa/ mgon khang /
gos sku sogs bzhengs shing / bstan pa'i sbyin bdag gtsang che hor shAkya dang / sgar pa don yod rdo rje dang / seng ge rtse ba 'phags pa rab brtan sogs kyis mthun

pa'i rkyen sbyar bar mdzad cing zhabs kyi padmo la gtugs/ rtsom pa yang / tshad ma'i dka' 'grel spyi don che chung gnyis/ /rnam rig Tig chen gnyis te rnam pa lnga/ /gong ma'i
dka' 'grel 'og ma'i spyi don ched/ /phar phyin Ti ka lung snying spyo don gsum/ /rtsa 'jug Ta ka stong thun chen mo gsum/ /'dul ba'i dkar 'grel las brgya'i Ti ka dang
/ /so thar Ti ka gzhi gsum las chog sogs/ /bde gsang rnam bshad gser thur chos tshan sogs/ /rtsom pa'i rnam grangs brjod par mi nus so/ /de ltar mdzad pa mthar phyin te dgung
lo brgyad cu pa me mo yos gro kun zla ba'i tshes lnga la gshegs so/thugs sras bstan pa 'dzin pa ni/ de dus grwa tshang go bzhi nas 'chad nyan gnang ba'i shangs chen
pa/ lcang ra ba/ rdor rgyal ba/ blo bzang sogs bgrang ba'i mi lang ba byon no/ des na shing pho byi lo 'di paN shAka pa byon pa'i sa spre nas brgya dang so bdun pa lags so/
sum stong lnga brgya dang re gcig 'das pa'i re gnyis pa sa mo bya spyi lo 1429la mdo khams su go rab 'byams pa bsod nams seng ge byon/ ngor dgon gsar btab pa'i lo de yin/
paN shAka pa las lo gcig gis gzhon/ lo bcu pa la byang chub sems dpa' kun dga' 'bum las rab tu byung / de nas bcu dgu bzhes pa'i bar du mkhan po de dang / go rab 'byams
pa shes dpal la sogs bsten te/ gzhung lugs gsum gyis lhag pa'i bcu phrag gcig mgrin pa'i lam rgyu zhing rjen par mdzad de/ go rab 'byams pa zhes snga mo nyid nas rang
byon du grags/ nyi shu pa sa pho 'brug

lor/ go rams sher dpal gyis/ rab 'byams la sogs bshes gnyen brgya rtsa gcig /ces brgya 'bul gyi rnam grangs su mang du bkod pa'i dkyus kyi gtso bor byas te/ rong ston smra
ba'i seng ge dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa gnyis lon pa/ chos grwa nA lendra thebs nas lo bcu gsum lon pa de nyid la rong ston chen po'i gsung gi bcud myangs te lo gnyis lon pa

po rnams kyis mkhan po dang las gsang mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mdor na bya lo nas me pho byi lo ngor chen zhi bar gshegs kyi bar lo ngo bzhi la/ gsung ngag sogs rgyud
man ngag gsan/ phyi lor ngor chen zhi bar gshegs na'ang / mus chen sogs mkhas pa du ma la/ gsung ngag sogs rgyud man ngag gi zab bcud blangs te lo ngo brgyad la rgyud

rje'i lcags kyus bzung ste/ so gsum pa sbrul lo nas sprel lo'i bar lo bzhi tsam zhig 'bras yul nyid du zur nas 'chad pa'i dbyangs kyi blo ldan rnams yid gsol par byas/
kyai rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen dang / sdom gsum gyi

Ti ka/ yum ston rab gsal sogs rtsom pa'i sgo yang phye/ slar mus chen nyid kyi thugs rje'i zhags pa drangs te/ mus su byon/ bya lor zab chos gsan pa dang / gsang 'dus rtsod
spong sogs mdzad/ so brgyad pa khyi lo rje mus chen chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags bzang gis/ byang ngam rings su spyan drangs te zhabs 'bring du bkod do/ blo gsal 'ga' la
legs bshad kyi skyes dang / kun rig rtsod spong / kye rdor rtsod spong sogs rtsom gyi me tog kha phye/ me pho khyi la de nyid kyi rgyal zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la blo gsal

gyi lo de nyid la/ thub bstan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling chen po btab/ 'dus pa'i tshogs chen po la mdo sngags kyi dga' ston ngo mtshar rmad du byung bas spyir bstan pa'i
snying po/ khyad par sdom rigs kyi bstan pa rma med pa sor chud/ nyid lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa chu mo yos la e waM chos ldan gyi seng ge'i khri la zhabs sen bkod de/ me pho

lam sngon mo rdzong du chos kyi dga' ston rtsol ba'i tshe cho 'khrul zla ba'i nyer

gcig la zhi bar gshegs so/ bstan pa 'dzin pa'i slob bu yang / kong ston dbang phyug grub pa/ mus rab 'byams pa thugs rje dpal bzang po/ dka' bcu smra ba bsod nams rgya mtsho
sogs bgrang bar mi bzod pa byon/ des na shing byi 'di paN chen 'di byon pa'i sa mo bya nas brgya dang so drug pa yin no/sum stong lnga brgya dang re lnga 'das pa'i re drug
pa chu mo glang spyi lo 1433la/ Biographical Sketch of 'Bum phrag gsum pargyal ba 'bum phrag gsum pa dang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' chos bzang gnyis byon/ 'di paN chen
shAkya mchog ldan las lo lnga dang / kun mkhyen go rab 'byams pa las lo bzhis gzhon pa tsam mo/ de yang rje paN chen g.yas ru byang gi sa'i thig le/ 'jam gsar lha sdings
zhes grags pa'i 'dabs khang dmar brag khung du byon/ lo bdun pa'i tshe chos rgyal dkon mchog legs pas byams chen 'dzam gling rgyun gcug lag'ag khang dang bcas pa bzhengs/byams

seng ge/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/ dol phrug chos bzang rnams las/ gzhung lugs chen po la gsan pa rtsal (btsal ) dpal ldan sa skyar bka' bcu'i bshad pa legs par

gsum la 'bum 'dzin pa'i bka' gnang phebs/ rje 'dis zla ba gcig la thugs smin/ tshig don gyi

bshad pas/ kun mkhyen chos rje 'dus tshogs dang bcas pa legs bshad bdud rtsi'i mchod pas mnyes te/ 'bum phrag gsum pa zhes mtshan gyi shis brjod snyan pa'i glu dbyangs su zlos/sgra
pa shes rin dang / shangs pa kun dga' dpal ldan la sgra ka tsan sogs rig gnas che chung la sbyangs pas paNDi ta zhes snyan par grags/ sum cu pa rta lo'o/ kun mkhyen
go rab 'byams pa zur 'chad ba'i skabs su/ byams chen chos rjes mkhan po/ go rams chen pos las slob/ zha lu ba dka' bcu pas dus go ba mdzad de/ 'jam dbyangs chos rje sogs
mang zhig dang mnyam du bsnyen par rdzogs/rta lo de nyid kyi dbyar chos la/ rtse thang sogs su gzhung lugs drug cu'i bshad pa'i dga' ston spel/so gcig pa lug'uga lo dgun
chos la dpal ngam rings su sher phyin stong phrag brgya pa la bshad pa'i srol chen po btod/ lug lor dbyar chos lho shel dkar du bshad pa'i chos sbyin rgyas par bstsal/
so gnyis pa sprel lor glo bo smon thang gi chos sder 'bum gyis gtsos pa'i gzhung lugs brgya la mkhas pa'i dga' ston bsgrubs/ chos rgyal a mgon drung du/ gdan du 'os pa'i
mtha' cad dang / 'bol grub dang / sum stan mnyel 'bol gyi khri la rim bzhin 'bul gyi glegs bam ka pa/ kha pa/ ga nga gnyis rnams mgrin pa'i dpal nas bkod pas/ rgyal blon
'bangs bcas ngo mtshar gyi dpal la bkod pas/ po ti lnga pa man chad gsung nas sgrogs pa dang / rgyal blon gyis thog drangs blon po lung gang gi skal ldan rnams la 'bum
