mus chen drung du

zab don gyi bdud rtsi zhus shing / skyed mos tshal du byams chen rab 'byams pa 'dus pa'i tshogs dang bcas pa la/ bsnyen cing bkur bas dges par mchod/ kun mkhyen go rams pasa
zur 'chad ma gnang nas lo gcig song ba/ nyid kyi so bzhi pa khyi lo/ 'jam dbyangs rje dang gnyis la zur gnas legs bshad spel ba'i 'os su bka' bstsal/ lo bcu gsum gyi bar
du blo gsal don gnyer nyis brgya skor la legs bshad kyis yid gsos par mdzad/ zhe bdun pa phag lor mi dge ba'i rkyen grogs su shar te/ blo gsal shes ldan brgya phrag gnyis
bdang bcas/ bsod nams kyi dpal la dbang sgyur ba'i sde dpon so sos mthun pa'i rkyen sbyar te/ gnas nges med du legs par bshad pa'i char phab/ de yang yul dbus kyi sman
ljongs su shar te phag byi glang gsum/ gtsang chu gru gsum du stag mos 'brug gsum/ yar 'brog tu sbrul lo/ rkyang 'dur du rta lo/ nor bu sgang rgyang gdong sogs su lug sprel
gnyis te/ lo bcu'i bar du gnas nges med du 'chad pa'i zlos gar ci yang bsgyur to/nyid kyi lnga bcu rtsa bdun pa sa mo bya'i lor/ gtsang stod bsod rgyal gyis mthun pa'i
rkyen sbyar te/ zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bzang po la dpal mnyan yod bya rgod gshongs kyi chos grwa chen po btab/ kun mkhyen go rams chen po gshegs pa'i lo de yin/ de'i phyi
lo nyid kyi nga brgyad pa khyi lor 'phags mchog klu sgrub rgyal tshab tu dbang skur te/lo bcu gsum du 'phags mchog rjes 'chad pa'i rgyun bzungs shing / paN chen chos rje
gnas nges med du skal par 'tshams pa la zab sngags kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ nyid kyi bdun cu pa chu pho khyi lo 'phags mchog dag pa'i dbyings su gshegs te/ slar nyid
kyis mnyan

yod du sngags kyi chos 'khor bskor/ phyi lo de la mnyan yod du bdag cag gi ston pa 'khor gnas brtan gyis bskor ba dri'i gtsug lag khang dang bcas pa bzhengs/ don gcig pa phag
lor rab gnas kyis mnga' gsol/ nyin kyi don gnyis su sleb pa/ mnyan yod thebs nas lo bcu drug pa shing pho byi lo dpyid zla ra ba'i nyer gcig la dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/
/rje 'di nyid kyis mdo sngags kyi chos gsan pa'i tshul yang rje ngor chen yab sras la sa skya ngor lugs/ bdag chen rgya gar ba dang rnal 'byor pa bstan 'dzin dpal sogs
la sa skya rdzong lugs/ bshes gnyen blo gros rgyal mtshan la rje btsun bo dong pa'i de nyid 'dus pa/ stag lung ngag dbang grags pa la dwags po bka' brgyud dang ras chung
snyan brgyud sogs/ mkhyen rab yon tan dpal 'byung la shangs pa dka' brgyud dang ri chos sogs/ ka tog nor bu bzang pola rdzogs pa chen po'i skor sogs/ rnal 'byor rdo rje'i
mtshan can la zhi byed sogs te/ ji ltar gsan pa de dag kyang gnas nges med du legs par dgongs pas dus 'das pa kho na lags shing / bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa ches cher gsal
bar mdzad/ khyad par rigs pa'i gnad zab mos blo gsal la nges pa bde blag tu skye ba la paN chen 'di'i 'phrin las kyi rgyun kho na bka' drin che ba yin no/thugs sras bstan
'dzin gyi bu slob kyang / thugs sras 'phags mchog klu sgrub/ ar ston [-] /blo gros rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen lcags thang chos rje/ rgyal ba dkon mchog dpal ba/ lha byang
gi lha dbang rnam gnyis/ 'jam mgon blo gros bkra shis sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon/

'jam dbyangs kun dga' mchog (chos ) bzang ni/ chu mo glang de nyid la glo bo 'brog gseb tu byon/ bcu pa la brag dkar grags rgyal ba la dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa nod/ bcob brgyad
pa la glo bo bdag pos sa skyar grwa bskor dang dbus gtsang du slob gnyer ba brgya phrag gsum tsam rdzong brda gnang ba'i skabs su/ dpal ldan sa skyar blo gros gzhon nu'i
bshad gsar dang / ngor du rje btsun rdo rje 'chang dang mjal/ bcu dgu pa la e waM chos ldan de nyid du/ rdo rje 'chang gis mkhan po/ brag dkar sems dpa' chen po kha char
ba zhes grags pas slob dpon/ gcung gzhon nu seng ges dus go ba mdzad de rab tu byung / bcu dgu pa lug gi lo la ston chos grwa chen po 'bras yul du phebs/ byams chen rab
'byams pa dang mjal/ nyin kyi nyi shur son zhing / rje byams chen chos rje'i zhe gnyis pa skyed tshal thebs nas lo bzhir sleb pa'i lcags pho sprel lo nas byams chen rab
'byams pa lus dang grib ma ltar bsten cing / gsung gi bdud rtsi mdo sngags kyi zab bcud la tshibs par rol/ sum cu pa la byams chen rab 'byams chos rje dang / go rams chos
rje mkhan slob las bsnyen par rdzogs/ so bzhi pa khyi lo nas/ paN chen 'bum pa gnyis kyi zur 'chad mdzad/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa phan tshun 'gran pa bzhin du rgyas par mdzad/
nyid kyi nga gsum pa shing mo sbrul lo byams chen rab 'byams pa dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/ lnga bcu rtsa bzhi pa me pho rta lo nas skyed mos tshal gyi gdan seng ge'i khri
la zhabs sen bkod ba'i sgo nas don gcig bzhes kyi bar du mdo sngags kyi bstan pa bskyangs/ don gcig pa chu mo phag gi zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu gcig la zhi bar gshegs/

thugs sras bstan 'dzin mang du byon yang / bstan pa la phan pa'i bshes gnyen pa nyid kyi gdan sa ba nyid dang / chos 'khor lhun po 'debs pa po paN chen dngos grub dpal 'bar
dang / gzhar ri dgon gsar 'debs pa po lha dbang blo gros rnams so/ des na shing byi 'di/ paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' chos bzang dang gnyis
byon pa'i chu glang nas brgya dang so bzhi pa lags so/ sum stong drug brgya pa'i skabs su byon pa ni rgyal ba lcags thang pa chen po la sogs te/ sum stong drug brgya dang
drug 'das pa'i bdun pa shing pho rta spyi lo 1474lor gtsang lcaT thang rab 'byams pa byams pa bsod nams byon/ bcu gcig pa la yul de'i sangs rgyas gling zhes bya bar bsod
nams legs pa dang / 'chad dka' bcu pas mkhan slob byas te rab tu byung / bcu gcig pa de nyid nas bco brgyad kyi bar la mdog chos 'khor sgang du bshesaganyen shAkya rgyal
mtshan dang blo gros rgyal mtshan gnyis la rigs pa'i rnam 'gyur legs par sbyangs/ bcu dgu par mnyan yod bya rgod gshongs thebs nas lo bzhi lon pa'i tshe chos grwa de nyid
du/ 'jam dbyangs 'phags mchog klu sgrub la grangs cha en bco brgyad kyi legs bshad dang / gsung ngag sogs sngags kyi zab gnad lo grangs brgyad kyi bar du myangs/ pan
chen 'bum phrag gsum pa la gsung ngag shangs pas bka' brgyud/ ras chung snyan brgyud sogs zab khrid kyi bcud chen po blangs/ nyer lnga pa la dpal 'khor bde chen dang / nyer
drug pa la rtsed thang du gzhung lugs bcu drug (bdun) la legs bshad kyi skyes phul/ nyer dgu pa la/ mdog ya ga chos sdings su/ byams pa dkon

mchog dpal gyis mkhan po/ lu phu gdan sa pa/ dbon brtson 'grus rgya mtshos las slob/ mtshungs med chos rje dpal 'byor bas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mdor na dgung
lo nyer gcig pa nas/ sum cu'i bar blo gsal don gnyer mang po la sgos su legs bshad ci yong ngos/ so gcig nas so lnga'i bar %gyi nas % bskor ba'i zur 'chad gnang / so drug
nas lo gsum/ gsang phu ba chos grags kyis mkhan po/ rje 'dis slob dpon mdzad/ so dgu pa chu pho sprel la dpal 'bum phrag sum pa'i rgyal tshab dam par mnga' gsol te/ de
nas dgung lo re bzhi bzhes kyi bar lo grangs nyi shu rtsa drug tu dpal 'bum phrag gsum pa'i gdan seng ge'i khri la zhabs bkod de 'chad ba'i sgra dbyangs bsgrags/ mdor na/
nyer gcig pa la sgos chos gnang ba nas/ re bzhin pa la gdan sa gtad kyi bar lo kun dril bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi bar du mdo phyogs kyi chad nyan kho nas bstan pa rin po che
gsal bar mdzad/ 'chad pa'i skabs der yang / mtshungs med rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dngos slob shes rab rin po che la rdzong lugs kyi gsung ngag gsan pa sogs gsan pa mang du
mdzad/ re bzhi pa me mo bya lo paN chen bzang po bkra shis la gdan sa gtad de na gza' brag phug tu gdan phab/ re lnga pa sa pho khyi lor chos rgyal tshe dbang rdo rjes
dpal ngar rings kyi mkhan por mnga' gsol/ re bdun pa lcags pho byi ba'i zla ba bcu gcig pa'i gnam gang la dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/ 'chad pa'i 'bras bu bstan 'dzin gyi skyes
bu brgya rtsa gtsig byon par bshad kyang / gtso bo bsdus na/ paN grub bzang po bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs

phyogs las rnam rgyal/ skyid gshongs pa chen po blo gros rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ 'dzam gling rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas lhun grub/ lnga rig bkra shis
chos 'phel/ gdan gcig pa shAkya rgya mtsho/ mkhas mchog grags pa bzang po/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan bkra shis dang brgyad do (gcig lhag ) /kho bo cag kyang lo bco lnga lon
pa'i tshe/ kun mkhyen chen pos gdan sa paN grub bzang po bkra shis la gtad tsam gyi bya lo/ dpal mnyan yod kyi gtsug lag khang du/ rje nyid kyi zhabs pad bsten/ rab tu byung
ba'i mkhan po dang / bla ma'i rnal 'byor sogs kyi bka' drin bstsal te/ dges pa chen pos bskyangs shing / byin rlabs snying la sim/ ming bsgyur ba'i tshe/ khyod kyi skya
ming la ci zer gsungs/ klu rgyal nor bur 'bod zhus pas/ ming zur gyi klu ming de ma chad pa zhig dgos pa 'dug da khyod yon tan che ba 'dam mam/ grags pa che ba 'dams
gsungs/ ci yang zhu ma spobs pa la/ yon tan che ba dga' mod/ ming la 'di bzhin gyis gsung ba phebs shing brtse bas bskyangs/ mdor na 'chad pa kho nas bstan pa spel ba la/
rong ston gyi rjes su/ kun mkhyen lcags thang pa 'di nyid bka' drin lhag par che ba yin no/sum stong drug brgya nyi shu rtsa bdun 'das pa'i rtsa brgyad pa shing mo yos spyi
lo 1495paN grub bzang po bkra shis byang phyi 'brog dol khrod du byon/ yongs kyi 'dren pa lha mang lcags gsum 'chi med dbang po 'dzam gling rab 'byams te lnga la mdo
sngags kyi gsan pa mdzad cing / zhes gsum pa

me mo bya la mnyan yod bya gshongs kyi khrir 'khod de/ lo ngo bdun du 'chad ba'i rgyun bsrings/ zhe dgu pa chu mo yos la dpal ngam rings kyi dbu mdzad dang / ya ga chos sding
kyi bshad grwa bskyangs/ lnga bcu rtsa gsum pa me mo lug la/ chos sde chen po'i khri chen po la zhabs brten nas lo bco brgyad du bstan pa bskyangs/ bdun cu pa shing pho
byi lo 'di nyid la dag pa'i zhing du phebs so/) de ltar kho bo'i bstan rtsis 'di ni/ shing pho byi lo nas 'go brtsams de me pho stag lor rdzogs par grub pa yin no/ 'di
yan gyi [bstan] rtsis rnams ni/ 'das lo nas lo grangs sum stong drug brgya dgu bcu rtsa dgu pa sum stong bdun brgyar nyag ma gcig gis ma chog pa'i lo de yin no/ zhes shes
par mdzod cigsum stong drug brgya so bdun 'das pa'i so brgyad pa shing mo glang spyi lo 1505la rgyal ba skyid gshongs pa blo gros rnam rgyal 'dar skyid gshongs su byon/
bco brgyad pa la mnyan yod du lcags thang chos rje'i zhabs pad bsten te mdo phyogs sbyangs/ phyis su rje blo gsal rgya mtsho dang / rje kun dga' grol mchog drung du gsung
ngag sogs sngags kyi zab don blangs/ nyi shu rtsa lnga pa la dpal 'khor bde chen dang nyer drug pa la byang ngam rings su bshad pa'i snyan grags ches cher khyab/ nyer bdun
pa la dpal chos 'khor gling gi bshad grwa gzung ste lo bcur bstan pa spel/ lo brgyad pa la mnyan yod kyi gdan seng ge'i khri mnan te lo brgyad du lung rigs kyis bstan
pa bzung / mi

dbang chos rgyal yab sras mnyes par byas te/ 'tsho ba'i rten du chos gzhis bzang po zhus te mnyan yod la mthun pa'i rkyen du sbyar/ zhe brgyad pa la ngam rings chos sde'i dbu
mdzad/ ya ga chos sdings kyi bshad grwa skyongs shig par chos kyi rgyal po tshe dbang rdo rje yab sras kyi bkas bkug ste/ lo bdun du 'chad pa'i dbyangs snyan par zlos/
lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa la gnas bzang po gnyag phur gdan phab ste zab don nyams su bzhes/ drug cu rtsa gcig pa glang gi lo la/ chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' rin chen sku mched
kyis dpal ngam rings kyi mkhan por mnga' gsol te chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bzhin pa'o/ mtha' dgung lo gya gcig pa bya lo zla ba gsum pa'i nyi shu dgu la dag pa'i zhing du
gshegs/kho bo cag gis kyang bya gshongs nas nyer gnyis la zhabs drung du 'byor/ sku mnyel ba med par chos zab mo'i 'bebal gtam cher mdzad/ nyer lnga'i tho rengs khyed 'chad
nyan 'chag phyin pa drag gsungs/ bdag sku khams kyi tsho zin zin mi 'gro zhus pas/ sku khams kyi tshod de ring zin yong gsungs/ cung gdangs su 'gro ba yin nam snyam pa
las ma byung / nyin par yang thugs dgyes pa'i 'bel gtam kho na gnang / dgong mo thugs dam rdzas rjes mnal cung zad mdzad/ de sad mtshams sku drang por bsrang ste da kho
bo la gsal 'debs kyis shig gsungs/ kho bos kyang gsal 'debs 'bul lugs bgyis/ 'jigs pa'i tshab tshub ma dgos lhod kyis lhod gsungs/ bum dbang gi 'da' ka ma phul bas de min
gsungs/ gong ma gsum gyi 'da' ka ma'i gsal 'debs phul bas de bzhin yin gsungs/ thugs dgyes bzhin du lta stangs

mdzad de mnyam par gzhag lta ba spros bral la blo phyam 'gro na 'da' ka ma mi thebs mi srid tshe 'di dang mthong lam gyi bar na dar tsam las med ces gsungs pa ltar/ 'da' ka
ma'i ngang de nyid la sa dang po'i grub mtha' 'khor 'das dbyer med snyoms par gdon mi za ba'i nges pa rnyed pa lags so/rje btsun dam pa kun dga' grol mchog me mo yos la
glo bor byon/ drug cu pa me stag zal ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad la chos lung byang rtser gshegs/ rje blo gsal rgya mtsho shing pho stag la 'dar mang mkhar rmu ru byon/
don gsum pa me stag zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga la 'dar snang tshar ram grang mo che'i dgon par gshegs/ rje 'di gnyis gshegs pa'i me stag ni/ 'das lo nas sum stong
dgu bcu rtsa dgu pa yin no/ zhes gong du bshad pa las shes dgos/ kho bo cag gi 'dren pa 'di gsum gyi rnam par thar pa ni logs su spro bar sha chags pas 'dir ma bris so/ 'dir
bstan rtsis mdzad pa po'i rnam par thar pa yang phyir logs nas 'chad do/ zhes smra bar bya'o/ gnyis pa dgon gnas rim par byon tshul la/ bstan pa phyi dar la/ 'das lo

(shes ) so/dpal ldan bzang ldan gyi mkhan po ni/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen kun spangs chos grags dpal/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas bzang po/ rtse lnga nam mkha' ye shes/ 'jam dbyangs

po/sum stong drug brgya dang nyag gcig 'das pa'i gnyis pa sa mo glang spyi lo 1469la dpal shAkya mchog ldan zhe gnyis lon pa'i tshe thub bstan gser mdog can du bshad
pa'i grwa btsugs/ sa glang de nas shing byi bar la dgu bcu rtsa drug sum stong drug brgya dang lnga ru sleb pa chu pho 'brug spyi lo 1472la

mdog lo phu rdzong lugs kyi sngags dgon byon/ de nas go gsum/ sgrub chen chos rin gyis lnga bcu rtsa gnyis lon tshe btab/sum stong drug brgya dang nyag drug tu sleb pa chu
mo sbrul spyi lo 1473la/kun mkhyen go rab byams pas zhe lnga lon pa'i tshe thub bstan rnam par rgyal ba'i bshad grwa btab/ de nas go gnyis/sum stong drug brgya nyi shu rtsa
gnyis pa sa mo bya spyi lo 1489la thub bstan mnyan yod bya gshongs dpal 'bum phrag gsum pas lnga bcu rtsa bdun lon tshe btab/ de nas bdun cu rtsa drug lon/ thub bstan
yangs chen de nas lo bzhi sa byi lor btab/sum stong drug brgya so lnga pa chu pho khyi spyi lo 1502lo bgyi (skyi) chu rdzong lugs kyi sngags dgon byon/ de nas drug cu rtsa
gsum/ 'debs mkhan byams pa dkon mchog dpal/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa bzhi'i steng du btab/gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir khro phu byams chen zhes grags pa ni/paN chen shAkya shrI
bod du byon pa'i shing pho khyi lo nas 'go brtsams te/ sum stong sum brgya zhe bzhi 'das pa'i bzhi bcu rtsa lnga pa/ chu pho sprel spyi lo 1412lor/ pan chen de nyid kyi
gtso byas te rab tu gnas pa'i me tog gtor/ khro lo byams pa dpal lo zhe gcig lon pa'i tshe yin/ me tog 'thor rgya pho sprel lo nas/ sum brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum lon pa
'di yin no/ rab gnas mkhan po paN chen gyi sum stong lnga brgya dang drug cu rtsa drug

stag spyi lo 1434la dpal ngam rings byams chen byon/ de nas brgya dang so gcig 'debs mkhan chos rgyal dkon mchog legs pa/ mkhan po A nan ta ma ti dang / seng ge dpal rin pa
gnyis kyi ngo la sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog gis bkod pa gnang nas btab/ de'i tshe sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu ba lnga bcu yin/ A nan ta pas drug cu re gsum lon/
sum stong drug brgya 'das nas nyag gcig gi steng du slebs pa sa pho byi spyi lo 1468lo rin spungs byams chen byon/ de nas dgu bcu rtsa bdun/ 'di'i zhal bkod kyang sems
dpa' chen po bas gnang zer bas/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa drug pa'i lo yin no/ de ltar kho bo'i bstan rtsis 'di ni/ shing pho byi ba spyi lo 1564nas brtsams/ me pho stag spyi
lo 1566la rdzogs par grub pa yin mod/ 'di yan chad 'das lo nas du song sogs rtsis pa ni/ shing byi yan chad bzhir bzhag pa yin la/ rdzogs par grung pa'i me pho stag 'di
ni/ 'das lo sum stong drug brgya dgu cu rtsa dgur slebs pa'i lo de yin pas/ sngar rtsis pa'i steng du lo gnyis bsnan te me stag yan la gsal bar shes par gyis shigde ltar
bstan rtsis lhag bsam rab dkar zhes bya ba bstan 'dzin skyes bya dam pa la yid ches pa'i rnam thar lo rgyus dang sbyar te/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa spyi bye brag la
gus pa bskyed pa'i phyir 'dren pa dam pa rnam gsum gyi zhabs sprul gtsug gis mchod pas/ lung rtogs kyi bstan pa spyi bye brag la so sor ma 'dres pa'i rnam dpyod kyi spobs
pa/ gzu bor gnas pa'i chos bzhin rjes su 'brang bas/ so so la ma dad pa'i rnyog pa'i dri ma bsam pa shAkya'i dge

slong sde snod 'dzin pa mang du thos pa klu sgrub ces bya bas/ ston pa chos dbyings su bzhugs nas sum stong brgya phrag drug dang dgu bcu rtsa dgu pa bdun brgyar gcig gi ma
chog pa me stag spyi lo 1566gi sa ga zla ba'i dus bzang po la/ dpal ya ga chos sdings kyi mdun sa chen po sbyar ba 'dis kyang / bu ram shing pa'i bstan pa rin po che bshad
sgrub thos bsam sgom gsum dang / 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas phyogs mtha' dag tu dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas par gyur cig de ltar rang gis sug ris su bgyis
pa las/ slad kyi 'das lo sum stong bdun brgya nyi shu pa spyi lo 1587thams cad 'dul zhes pa me mo phag gi lo zla ba brgyad pa'i dkar phyogs rdzogs pa gnyis pa'i tshes
'dar chos 'khor yang rtse'i sngags grwa slob bshad gling gi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba'o/ shu bha mastu sarba dza ga te/

tha snyad rig gnas lnga ji ltar byung ba'i tshul gsal bar byed pa blo gsal mgrin rgyan legs bshad nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba bzhugs so/

swasti pra dza bhyaHgang gi mtshan tsam dran pas ma rig pa'i/ /mun pa'i tshogs rnams ma lus nyer bsal te/ /rig pa'i gnas la blo gros mchog stsol ba'i/ /klu sgrub rgya mtsho
snying nas dran no skyongs/ /tshul gnas gser gyi yol go rnam dpyod kyi/ /'od snang rmongs mun 'joms la dpa' ba dang / /lhan cig brtson 'grus lhag bsam rgyan bkra ba'i/ /mdzada'
bshes legs bshad mchog sbyin 'dir dgyes rol//zhes bsngags brjod sngon du song nas/ 'dir rang cag gi ston pa shAkya'i rgyal pos 'dul bar bya ba'i bstan pa 'di la ni
thar pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang bla na med pa thob par 'dod pa'i blo gsal dag gis bslab par bya ba'i gnas ni rig pa'i gnas lnga po 'di nyid yin te/ mdo drin lan
gsab ma las/ de bas na bla na med pa'i byang chub thob par bya pa'i phyir du rig pa'i dngos bo lnga la bslab par bya'o/ /zhes dang / mdo sde rgyan las/ rig pa'i gnas lnga/
zhes sogs dang / bdag nyid chen po sa paNDi nas/ rang blo shes bya kun la ma sbyangs na/ thams cad mkhyen pa nam mkha'i mtha' pas ring / de ltar dgongs nas rgyal dang
mkhas rnams kyis/ /shes bya'i gnas rnams spyong shes legs par gsungs/ zhes dang / mkhas pa'i dbang po sgra pa shes rin pas/ rig pa'i gnas lngar legs par ma sbyangs na/ /dgra
bcom skyes kyang kun mkhyen thos mi srid/ /de bas don gnyes mthar phyin bya ba'i phyir/ kun mkhyen las 'dir mkhas rnams brtson par rigs/ zhes dang 'dren pa dang pa klu
sgrub rgya mtsho'i gsung las/ lnga rig chos la ma sbyangs bag med kyi/ bdud rtsi thos pa'i rgyal ba'i

med/ /rig gnas che chung shes bya'i gnas rnams la/ /blo gros rtsal du thon cig grogs po dag /ces gsungs pa ltar/ sgra rig pa/ gtan tshigs rig pa/ bzang rig pa/ gso ba rig pa/
nang rig pa ste lnga po la legs par bslab dgos pa yin no/ /'o na de lnga la slob pa las dgos pa ji lta bu snyam na/ tha snyad tshig gi cha la legs par sbyangs pas/ de
nyid mkhas par shes pa na/ tshig gi cha la log rtog zhugs pa thams cad tshar gcod par byed pa dang / mngon gyur sogs don gyi cha la legs par sbyangs pas de'i tshul bzhin
du shes na don la log rtog zhugs pa thams cad sun 'byin nus pas/ rig gnas dang po gnyis shes na rgol ba ngan pa gzhan dag tshar gcod pa dang / bzo gnas sku gzugs kyi cha
tshad dang / gser 'gyur gyi rtsi la sogs pa shes pas skye bo 'byor pa can dang / dbul phongs rnams kyi don byed cing / gso ba rig pa'i gnas tshul bzhin du shes pas sems can
nad pa sdug bsngal gyis nyen pa rnams rjes su bzung ba'i phyir rig gnas bar pa gnyis dang / rang nyid kun shes mkhas pa'i go 'phang bde blag tu thog par bya ba'i phyir
rig gnas lnga la legs par bslab dgos pa yin te/ gzhan dag tshar gcod rjes su gzung phyir dang / bdag nyid kun shes bya phyir zhes gsungs pas so/ /byams mgon gyi gzhung 'di
nyid la rje btsun lo tsA ba chen po 'gyur med bde chen gyi bzhed pas/ 'phags mchog gis kyang zhes pa ni cung zad mi 'thad de/ 'phags mchog rnams kyis rig gnas la sasbyang
mi dgos shing gzhung 'di'i don du yang / ka tanyi zhes pa cing kyang gi skad dod yod pa yin gyis

gis kyang zhes pa'i skad dod kyang med pa'i phyir/ des na gzhung gi 'bru gnyer ba'i tshe 'khor du gnas pa'i 'phags mchog rnams la 'phags mchog ces bos nas/ thams cad mkhyen
pa'i go 'phang thob par byed na cis kyang rig gnas lnga la sbyang dgos zhes gsungs/ thams cad mkhyen pa mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i bzhed pas/ de lta bu'i dgos pa ni
rang gi blo tshod du/ 'phags pa mchog gis rig gnas la sbyang mi dgos so snyam pa shar ba'i tshod dpag las yin mod/ 'dir skabs kyi 'phags pa ni byang sems 'phags rnams yin
pas/ de rnams sa yongs sbyongs kyi skabs su shes bya'i gnas thams cad la slob dgos par bshad yod pas/ 'phags pa dman pa nyan rang las ches mchog tu gyur pa'i byang chub
sems dpa' sar gnas rnams kyis kyang thams cad mkhyen pa thob pa'i phyir du rig pa'i gnas lnga la slob dgos na/ so skye'i blo gsal rnams kyis rig gnas la slob dgos pa lta
smos kyang ci dgos zhes pa'i don yin gsungs te/ bla na med pa'i bshad tshul yin no/ /byams pa'i gzhung 'di nyid kyis rig gnas lnga'i go rim dang / thog mar gang nas 'jug
gi rim pa yang log smra tshar gcod pa'i yan lag gnyis thog mar bstan/ don gnyer rjes su 'dzin pa'i yan lag bar du bstan/ nang rig pa rjes su ston par mdzad pa las tshad
mar ci yang ma mdzad par/ rig gnas kun shes las/ rig gnas dang po don gnyer rjes 'dzin te/ /bstan pa gnas phyir dkon mchog gsum gyi rten/ /bzhengs bar 'dod pa'i 'byor ldan
lhag bsam can/ /rgyal bas bstan 'dzin nyid du lung bstan zhing / /zhes bya ba la sogs pas bzo rig rig gnas dang por mdzad pa ni cung zad mi

'thad par mngon no/ /de ltar rig lnga las kyang thog mar sgra rig pa la slob dgos te/ brjod bya'i don rtogs pa ni rjod byed kyi tshig la rag las shing / de'i tha snyad rtogs
pa yang sgra rig pa la rag las pa'i phyir ro/ ji skad du yang slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis/ tha snyad la ni ma brten par/ /dam pa'i don ni rtogs mi nus/ /dam pa'i
don ni ma rtogs na/ /mya ngan 'das pa'i thob mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ rgyu mtshan de dag gi phyir na/ don dam pa'i bden pa rtogs pa'i thabs su tha snyad sgra rig
pa'i gzhung lugs la legs par slob dgos pa yin no/ /ji ltar slob pa'i tshul la yang gnyis te/ sgra rig pa ji ltar byung ba'i tshul dang / ji ltar byung ba'i sgra rig pa
bshad pa'o/dang po la lnga/ rgyal bas gsungs tshul/ rgyal sras kyis mdzad tshul/ lha yul du byung tshul/ rgya gar du dar tshul/ bod du 'gyur tshul bshad pa'o/dang po ni/
mkhas pa'i dbang po sgra pa shes rin pas rig gnas kun shes las/ gsum pas tshig la 'khrul pa sel ba'i phyir/ /de la log par smra ba tshang gcod byed/ /sgra rig de bzhin gshegs
pas gsungs pa ni/ /nges tshig so so yang dag rig pa yi/ /yi ge dbri dang bsnan dang bsgyur ba dang / /tshig gi rnam dbye sogs kyi rnam 'gyur ro/ /khyad par rnga bo
che yi mdo las ni/ /byings dang ming dang kun bshad nyer bsgyur dang / /kr-ita dang de phan gyis bsdus sgrub pa rnams/ /rgyal ba'i gsung rab las 'byung gsal bar gsungs/ /zhes
gsungs pas/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis gsungs tshul ston pa

yin te/ de la spyir nges don par rlom pa rtsing por gzu lums su spyod cing / tha snyad kyi bden pa la rgyab kyis phyogs pa dag na re/ sgra rig pa'i gzhung lugs ni/ rig pa'i
gnas thun mong ba tsam yin zhing / lhag par phyi rol pa'i drang srong dag gis bshad pa la gtso bor brten pa yin gyi/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab rnams
las gsal bar mi 'byung zhing / bslab par bya ba'i gnas kyang ma yin no snyam du sems shing / de skad tshig tu yang smra bar byed do/ /unaudited'di ni 'thad pa ma yin
te/ gal te khyod kyi 'dod pa gzhir bzhag na thun mong ba'i rig gnas dang / lam la slob tu mi rung zhes par song la/ de lta ni khyed rang gi lag len dang dngos su 'gal ba
ste/ khyed rang yang tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi bsgom zhing / de'i nang nas phyi rol pa dang thun mong ba'i chos med par khas len dgos shing / khyad par grub mtha' bye brag
smra ba nas bzung ste/ dbu ma pa'i bar gyi zhi lhag gi nyams len dang / bya rgyud nas bla med kyi bar gyi zhi lhag gi nyams len spyir bshad pa rnams dang / lhag par snying
po'i bcud phyag rgya chen po bsgom pa'i tshe/ lhag mthong gi rten gzhir gyur pa'i zhi gnas shig bsgom mas mi bsgom/ bsgom na ni phyi rol pa dang thun mong ba'i nyams len
khyed rang yang byed bzhin par ma song ngam/ legs pas soms shig /gal te de la kho na re/ zhi gnas tsam sgom yang lhag mthong dang byang chub kyi sems la sogs pa'i khyad
par yod do zhe na/ kho bo cag kyang de skad smra ba yin te/ sgra rig tsam thun mong yin kyang / lhag bsam byang chub kyi sems dang / gang la skyabs su 'gro ba'i gnas dang
/ thos

don snying por dril lugs kyi khyad par shin tu che ba yin no/ /yang sangs rgyas kyi gsung las mi 'byung snyam pa yang khyeng rang thos pa chung ba'i skyon te/ spyir chos dang
/ don dang / nges pa'i tshig dang / spobs pa so so yang dag pa ste bzhi'i gsum pa nges pa'i tshig 'chad pa'i tshe/ yul ljongs kyi skad dang nges tshig mtha' dag sogs skad
rigs spyir slob tshul dang / khyad par saMskra ta la ye ge dbri ba dang / bsnan pa dang / bsgyur ba dang / tshig thams cad ka lA pa ltar si sogs te sogs dang / tsandra
pa lta supra dang thing gi mtha' can khyad par 'khor lo tha ma'i mdor gtogs pa rnga bo che'i mdo las/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung las sangs rgyas rtag pa dang bdag la sogs
pa med pas de dag ni phyis 'ga' zhig gis rang bzor byas pa'o zhes smra bar 'gyur yang / de lta min te/ de dag de'i gsung las rgyas par 'byung tshul gsungs shing / de bzhin
du de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung la skad kyi byings la sogs pa med pas/ de dag phyis 'ga' zhig gis rang bzor byas so zhes smra bar 'gyur yang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung
la byings la sogs pa yod par gsungs shing / gzhan yang sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'da' tshul ston yang / don la thar pa'am myang 'das ni rtag brtan ther zug yin pas skye
'jig med pa'i dpe khang bzang zhig kyang de'i nam mkha' mi 'jig pa dang / de dper byas na Shidhu zhes bya ba'i skad kyi byings kyi don ni kta zhes bya ba'i rkyen gyis de
grub pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rkyen du 'gyur te/ ji ltar 'jig rten pa'i bstan bcos rnams las/ nA mAkhyA ta u

pa sarga krita tad ni ta zhes bya ba la sogs pa bsdus pa'i grub pa'i tshig de la grub pa zhes bya'o/ /grub pa'i tshig de'i grub pa gang yin pa de ni yang mi mngon pa med do
zhes byings rkyen gyis bsgyur yang / byings kyi rang bzhin mi 'gyur ba ni thar pa'i dper gsung zhing / sgrub tshul de dag ston pa'i gzhung ni/ nA ma zhes pa'i ming le dang
/ A khyA ta kun bshad/ kr-ita ces pa kr-ita kyi le'u ste sgra'i lus gzhung tsan gsum du sdus shing / de dag gi rnam 'gyur dang nyer mkho ni u pa sarga nye bsgyur dang
/ tad dhi ta de phan la sogs pa'i gzhung ngo / /de yang She tu bstan bcos la ste bkra shis pa'o/ /zhes pa'i byings bzhag de las la kta'i zhes pas kta'i rkyen sbyin/ byings
mtha'i u dang / rkyen gyi ka rjes 'brel yin pas phyis/ gha dzha Dha dha bha rnams kyi dha min pa'i ta tha dag la dha'o zhes pa dha ru bsgyur/ byings kyi dang po She'i sa'o
zhes pas Sha sa ru la dha'o zhes pas dha ru bsgyur/ dhu Ta rnams kyi gsum pa'o zhes pa'i mdos dha yig da ru bsgyur/ ming tshig du sgrub pa la rnam dbye gnyis pa'i sam
byin pas/ grub pa zhes pa grub pa la 'jug pa'i grub pa'i tshig go/ /de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i skad kyi byings ni mkhas shing khong du chud pa'o gsungs te/ budha khong
du chud pa'i rtogs pa la'o/ /zhes pa'i byings las sgrub ces gsal bar gsungs pa'i phyir dang / khyad par sngags kyi rgyud sde rnams su gzungs sngags kyi rigs phal cher
zhig legs par sbyar ba dang mtshungs par gsungs pas/ legs spyar ma shes na de dag klog pa dang / 'chad pa'i thabs mi shes pas thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son par

'dod pa'i blo gsal dag gis brda sprod pa'i gzhung lugs la 'bad pa chen pos brtson par bya'o zhes snying nas gdams so/ /gnyis pa rgyal sras kyis mdzad tshul ni/ kun shes las/
'jam pa'i dbyangs dang 'jig rten dbang phyug gis/ /dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbyangs gsal la brten pa'i/ /yi ge'i bsdu ba mdzad pa'i sgra yi mdo/ /yod par dbyangs 'char mdor bsdus
thog mar gsal/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ 'jam dbyangs dang spyan ras gzigs kyis gsungs pa'i sgra mdo yang yod pa yin te/ dus 'khor dbyangs 'char gyi mdor bsdus thog mar/
dbyangs dag gi dang po a yig yin pa de ni/ a sogs lnga ste/ a i r-i u l-i zhes rang byung gi bshad pa'o/ /a i u Na r-i l-i ka zhes pa ni so sor bsdu ba gzung phyir ro/ /e
o zhes bklag pa las mtshams sbyor gyi yi ge ste/ e yig dang o yig dag gi yon tan gyis so/ /r-i kr-i a Na las ri la dag go/ /zhes pa'i mdo'i phyir/ r-i li dag ni ma ning
du mi 'gyur te/ de gnyis kyang yon tan dang ldan pas e yig la sogs pa rnams dang khyad med do/ /zhes sogs nas de dag kyang nam mkha' la sogs rang bzhin gyi dbang gis grangs
bzhin du 'jam dpal gyis/ rang gis brda sprod pa las bris so zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /gsum pa lha yul du byung tshul ni/ kun shes las/ tshangs pa rtag zhi bas byas
pa yang yod/ /brgya byin gyis byas indra bu ka ra/ de la drang srong phur bus legs sbyangs pas/ /shin tu mkhas pa'i nga rgyal mchog tu gyur/ /nga rgyal brgya byin gyis bcom
zhum nas ni/ /lha phran blo gsal mang la 'chad 'phro bzhag /da dung rang nyid sgra la sbong bar zhus/ /nyan 'chad gnyis

ka gyis zhes bkas bskul bas/ /dus bzang brgyad la gzhan la mi ston par/ /rang nyid bslab pa'i sbyor la brtson pas na/ /nyan po gzhan gyis dus bzang bsrung dgos shar/ zhes gsungs
te/ 'di dag gi lo rgyus rgyas par ni spyi don du gsal zhing / sarba dznyA zhes pa'i sgra mkhan cig gis lha'i dbang po la bslabs zhes pa'i sarba dznyA ni tshangs pa'i
ming yin la/ 'di dag ni phyi rol pas mchod pa'i lha yin zhing / des bshad pa'i sgra rig rnams kyang phyi rol pa'i lugs yin mod/ gang zag dang bstan bcos de dag ngan par
ni mi blta ste/ tshangs pa la sogs pa de dag 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi rnam 'phrul du mdo sde za ma tog bkod pa las gsungs pa'i phyir/ ji skad du/ mdo de nyid las/ bskal
pa bzang po 'di 'das pa'i sngon bskal pa dgu bcu rtsa gcig pa na/ sangs rgyas rnam par gzigs zhes bya ba 'jig rten du byon pa'i tshe 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang
phyug gis snyigs ma lnga dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa'i cha byad kyis mi 'dul bar/ phyi rol pa'i lha'i gzugs dang rtags dang mtshan mas 'dul
bar mkhyen nas/ lha thams cad mkhyen pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs te/ tshangs pa phrag pa nas byung / dbang phyug dpral ba nas byung / nyi ma
spyan g.yas nas byung / zla ba spyan g.yon nas byung / chu lha lto ba nas byung / dbyangs can ma zhal gyi lce rtse las phyung ngo / /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /bzhi pa rgya
gar du dar tshul la gsum ste/ pA Ni byA ka ra Na byung tshul/ tsandra ka ra Na byung tshul/ ka lA pa byA ka ra Na byung tshul lo/ /

dang po ni/ kun shes las/ de bzhin bram ze pA Ni ni las kyang / rang ming ldan pa'i bstan bcos chen po sbyar/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ bram ze pA Ni ni byung tshul spyi don du
gsal zhing / spyir 'phags pa'i yul du grags pa'i sgra mdo ka tsan gnyis su ma 'dus pa dbyangs can byA ka ra Na ka lA pa'i mdo shin tu rgyas pa zhig paNDi ta rA dza shris
ka tsan gnyis kyi don bsdus pa rA dza shri byA ka ra Na zhes bya ba dang / rje btsun mchog gi sprul pa'i sku'i chos 'byung las/ rgyal po tsanda skyong gi grogs po bram ze
indra dhu ba zhes bya bas lha'i dbang po bsgrubs nas sgra'i ngems gnas zhus te/ des bshad pa bris pa indra dbang po'i brda sprod pabyA ka ra Na zhes grags pa sho lo ka
nyis khri lnga stong yod pa 'di la lhas bstan pa'i brda sprod pa zhes zer ro gsung bas/ indra byA ka ra Na'i bshad rgyun yang rgya gar na yod par gsal lo/gnyis pa ni/ kun
shes las/ de la tsandra go mis bsdus pa yi/ /gzhung la tsandra par grags chos 'bangs kyis/ /byas pa'i 'grel pa dang bcas bod du 'gyur/ zhes slob dpon chen po tsandra go
mis mdzad pa'i tsandra pa char gtogs dang bcas pa byung tshul stod pa ste/ de yang lo rgyus yongs grags rnams spyi don na gsal zhing / der cung mi gsal ba rje btsun mchog
gi sprul pa'i sku'i chos 'byung du gsal ba ni/ slob dpon tsandra go mis ni shar phyogs wa randrar 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi zhal mthong ba'i paNDi ta zhig mu stegs rgyang
'phen pa'i ston pa zhig dang rtsod par gyur te/ de'i ring lugs sun phyung yang rig pa ni blos rnam par brtags pa yin pas/ gang blo sgrims pa de rgyal bar zad kyis/
skye ba snga phyi yod pa'i rtags mngod sum du

med pas/ kho bo cag de mi 'dod zer ba na/ rgyal po la sogs pa dpang por bzhag ste/ nga nyid skye ba len pa yin pas dpral bar rtags thob cig byas nas des dpral bar mtshal gyi
thig le sha thim pa zhig byas/ kha nang du mu tig bcug ste/ de nyid du 'das te de'i lus zangs kha sbyar gyi nang du bcug ste rgyal pos rgyas btab bo/ de'i tshe rgyal rigs
kyi paNDi ta bi sha sa kha zhes bya ba'i bur skye ba blangs pa bzhin/ de la khye'u mtshan dang ldan pa zhig btsas ma thag tu/ mtshalagyi thig le dpral bar yod pa kha na
mu tig yod pa de byung / rgyal po sogs kyis sngar gyi phung po de la bltas pas/ dpral ba'i mtshal gyi thig le yang byi/ mu tig gi shul har re 'dug go/ /der mu stegs de
yang skye ba snga phyi yod par yid ches skad/ khye'u des ma la btsas ma thag tu phyag byas te/ zla ba bcu 'o brgyal bar ma gyur tam byas pas/ byis pa btsas ma thag smra ba
ni ltas ngan no snyam nas kha rog 'dug byas so/ /de nas lo bdun gyi ngar cang la smras pas lkugs pa'o snyam mo/ /der mu stegs kyi rgol ba zhig gis/ shin tu go dka' ba'i
snyan ngag gi tshigs su bcad pa sangs rgyas pa'i grub mtha' 'gog pa zhig brtsams nas rgyal po dang mkhas pa'i tshogs la 'grims so/ der bi sha sa kha'i khyim du byung ba
na/ de yun ring du brtags pas sgra don ji bzhin go ba yang med na lan gdab par ga la nus te/ don de sems shing khyim gyi phyi rol tu bya ba zhig la song ngo / de tsandra
go mi la bdun lon pa des bltas pa na/ don shes shing lan gdab par dka' ba med de/ de'i don 'grol ba'i yig chung btab/ lan gyi tshigs bcad kyang bris so/ /

pha nang du 'ong ba na de ltar bris pa mthong nas/ khyim du su byung zhes tsandra go mi'i ma la dris so/ gzhan su yang ma 'ongs te bu lkugs pa blta zhing bri'o/ der phas bu
la dris pa na ma'i gdong la blta zhing 'dug go/ /mas smros shig byas pas/ 'di ni bdag gis bris pa yin te/ rgol ba 'di ldog pa ni dkar ba ma yin no zhes zer/ de nas nang
par zhig na tsandra go mi dang / mu stegs kyi ston pa de rtsod par tsandra go mi rgyal de bya dga' chen po thob/de nas sgra dang rtog ge la sogs pa'i rig gnas thun mong ba
thams cad ma bslabs par rang shes shig byung ste/ phyogs thams cad du grags pas khyab bo/de nas theg pa chen po'i slob dpon zhig la skyabs su 'gro ba dang / bslab pa'i
gnas lnga blangs slob dpon chen po blo gros brtan pa la mdo sde dang mngon pa'i sde snod nan cher lan cig nyan pa tsam gyis mkhyen/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i slob dpon mya ngan med
pa zhes bya ba la bka' lung nod de rig sngags bsgrubs pas 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dang / sgrol ma'i zhal mngon sum gzigs/ shin tu mkhas pa chen por gyur/de nas shar
phyogs su rgyal po bha ra Sha yul du sman dpyad dang sdeb sbyor dang bzo'i gnas kyi ston pa mang du byas/ khyad par du sgra rig pa mang du bshad cing yod/ de'i tshe rgyal
po'i bu mo ta rA zhes bya ba bag mar blangs shing rgyal pos yul 'khor zhig kyang sbyin/ lan cig de'i g.yog mos ta rA zhes 'bod kyi 'dug pas/ yid dam dang mtshan mthun pa
khyim thab tu mi rung ngo snyam nas/ slob

dpon nyid yul gzhan du 'gro ba rgyal pos shes te/ de nga'i bu mo dang lhan cig mi 'dug na sgrom du chug la ganggA la skyur cig ces bsgos te de bzhin du byas pa na/ slob dpon
gyis sgrol ma la gsol ba btab pas/ nam mkha' dang rgya mtsho phran mtshams kyi gling zhig la thon/ gling de 'phags mas sprul pa yin yang zer te/ tsandra dwI pa zhes bya
ba tsandra go mi nyid der bzhugs pa la ming chags shing da lta yang yod/ grong bdun stong tsam shong ba zhig 'dug zer/ der slob dpon gyis bzhugs te 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs
dang sgrol ma'i rdo sku bzhengs/ thog mar nya pa rnams kyis gtam de thos/ de nas rim gyis skye bo gzhan yang byung ste grong khyer chags/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi
bskul bar go mis dge bsnyen mdzad/ mtshan de ltar grags/ de nas tshong pa rnams kyis khyer te singga'i gling du byon/ yul de na klu nad mang du 'byung ba zhig yod pa las
der seng ge sgra'i lha khang bzhengs pas rang zhi/ sman dpyad dang rig gnas rgya cher spel/ gling phran gyi skye bo rnams la phan btags/ theg chen ci rigs bshad/ yul bdag
gnod sbyin las nor blangs te chos mang du btsugs/ slar 'dzam bu'i gling gi lho phyogs kyi brgyud du byon/ bram ze mchog srid kyi lha khang na/ klu la sgra nyan pa'i bkod
pa dang / klu she Shas byas pa'i pwa Ni pa'i 'grel pa 'dug pa yang gzigs pas/ 'grel ba zhes bya ba tshig nyung la don mang ba/ ma zlos pa tshang ba zhig dgos pa yin pa
las/ klu ni rab tu rmongs te tshig mang ba/ don nyung ba/ zlos pa ma rdzogs pa'o/ /zhes smad nas pA Ni'i don 'grel du tsandra bya ka ra Na yan lag brgyad dang bcas pa bcas
mdzad/ gzhung der nyung

ngu rnam gsal yang dag rdzogs/ /zhes pa yang klu la zur za ba'o/ /de nas rig pa'i 'byung gnas na lendAr byon/ de nas zla grags dang rtsod pa mdzad pa'i tshul rnams phal cher
spyi don gzhin la/ tsandra go mis thogs med kyi srol la brten te rnam rig gi phyogs bzung / zla grags kyis klu sgrub kyi gzhung sangs rgyas bskyangs sogs kyis bkral ba
la brten te ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyogs bzung / lo gsum gyi bar du bgro gleng gi brgal brtag mdzad do/ rtsod pa de blta ba'i phyir skyes bo mang po rtag tu 'dus pas/ grong
pa'i khye'u dang bu mo tshun chad kyis kyang phyogs tsam rig nas/ kye ma 'phags pa klu sgrub gzhung / /la la'i sman la la la'i dug /mi pham 'phags pa thogs med gzhung /
/skye bo kun gyi bdud rtsi nyid/ /ces glur len no/ de nas na lendAr bzhugs nas/ bzo gnas brgya rtsa/ sgra/ rtog ge sman dpyad/ sdeb sbyor/ zlos gar/ mngon brjod/ snyan ngag
skar rtsis la sogs pa'i bstan bcos mang du brtsams/ slob ma rnams la de rnams gtso bor bshad pa'i tshe/ 'phags ma sgrol mas/ sa bcu pa dang zla ba sgron me dang / /sdong
po rgyan pa dang ni larka 'jug /rgyal ba rnams kyi yul gyur klogs shig kye/ /sdeb sbyor ngan g.yo'i sbyor bas khyed la ci/ /zhes gsungs pas phyi rol gyi rig pa'i gnas
rnams nyung ngur bstan cing / rmad du byung ba'i mdo lnga po de dag dus rtag tu gsungs/ bdag nyid kyang nyid rer zhal 'don mdzad/ mdo de rnams la bsdus don re yang mdzad/
spyir snga phyir mdzad pa la bstod pa brgya dang brgyad/ nang rig pa'i bstan bcos brgya dang brgyad phyi rol gyi bstan bcos brgya dang brgyad bzo gnas brgya dang brgyad
de phra mo thor

bu ba bzhi brgya dang sum cu rtsa gnyis brtsams zer/pra ti ma ta mi zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos byang chub sems dpa'i lam rim mtha' dag ston pa zhig kyang mdzad de ches ma dar/
'gro lding dang singga'i gling na de 'chad pa'i srol da lta'ang 'dug gsung / sdom pa nyid shu pa dang zla ba sgron me'i 'grel pa dang / sku gsum 'jug pa ni/ theg chen gyi
paNDi ta phyis byon pa thams cad kyis slob par byed pa byung ngo / sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang / spyan ras gzigs kyi sgrub thabs brgya rtsa zhes slob dpon 'dis
mdzad pa bod du 'gyurabar snang ngo / khyad par tsandra pa'i mdo le'u nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ sho lo ka bdun brgya yod pa pA Ni dang mthun pa nyung ngu rnam gsal/ de'i yan
lag tu yi ge'i mdo dang / u Na de'i mdo dang / ting supra kyi 'grel pa/ nyi bsgyur gyi 'grel pa rnams mdzad/ de ltar sems can gyi don yun du mdzad nas/ mthar po ta lar gshegs
par bzhed de/ 'dzam bu'i gling nas dha na shri'i gling du byon pa na/ sngon klu she Sha la smad pas 'khon du bzung nas rgya mtsho'i rlabs chen pos gru gzings gzhig
par brtsams/ rgya mtsho'i dbus nas sgra byung nas tsandra go mi phyir phyung zhig zer/ sgrol ma la gsol ba btab pas/ 'phags ma gtso 'khor lnga nam mkha' lding la chibs pa
mdun gyi nam mkha' la byon nas klu rnams 'jigs shing skrag nas bros/ gru dha na shrIr bde bar slebs/ der dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten la mchod cing / sgrol ma'i
lha khang brgya rtsa dang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi lha khang brgya rtsa bzhengs/ ri bo po ta lar gshegs nas da lta yang lus ma spangs par bzhugs yod/

slob ma la springs pa'i 'phrin yig ni/ rgyal po'i bu rin chen grags la zhes bya ba rab tu byung ba phab pa zhig la po ta la nas tshong pa rnams las bskur bas/ de yang slob
springs mthong nas thos bzhin spyod par gyur to zhes grags so/ /zhes 'byung / tsandra pa'i yan lag tu 'grel bshad sogs don 'grel ji ltar byung ba ni spyi don bzhin no/ /gsum
pa ni/ kun shes las/ dbang phyug go chas gzhon nu gdong drug bsgrubs/ /grub nas tshar gcig bstan pas tshig don rtags/ /cha bsaT ka lA pa yi mdo zhes bya/ rang sde'i mkhas
pa bgrod dka' seng ge yis/ /sbyar ba'i 'grel pa dur sing zhes bya dang / /gzhan sde jo bo grags 'byor gyis sbyar ba'i/ /slob phan zhes pa'i 'grel pa bod du byon/ zhes
gsungs pa ste/ lo rgyus raT rim spyi dron ltar dang / der mig gsal ba'i lo rgyus ngo bo mchog gi sprul pa'i sku'i chos 'byung dang / slob dpon klu sgrub kyi grogs po slob
dpon bram ze mchog sred ces bya ba dang / rgyal po bde byed kyi mdun na 'don du gnas so/ /de'i tshe rgyal po'i btsun mo tha chung zhig gi sgra'i gnas cung zad shes la
rgyal pos ni mi shos so/ skyed mos tshal du chu la rtse ba'i tshe/ rgyal pos de la chu gtor bas/ des ma mo da ka pinytsa zhes bod skad du bdag la chu ma 'thor zhes pa'o/
/rgyal pos lho phyogs kyi yul skad dang sbyar bas/ bal sran gyi 'khur ba ting mar gyis btsos pa byin cig ces par go nas de byin pas/ btsun mo des rgyal po ba lang lta bu
dang lhan cig tu gnas pa las shi ba sla'o snyam nas/ lceb par brtsams pa las/ rgyal pos bzung nas sgra slob par byas te/ bram ze

mchog sred la legs par bslabs so/ /'on kyang cung zad ma rdzogs pa las slob dpon sapta warma las blangs pa yin no/ de la slob dpon mchog sred kyi lo rgyus ni/ sangs rgyas kyi
bstan pa la mngon par dad pa'i bram ze las drug la brtson pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub na landa'i mkhan po mdzad pa'i tshe mdzada' bshes su gyur pa zhig ma ga dha'i shar phyogs
ra ra'i yul na yod pa las/ des lo bcu gnyis su 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sngags bzlas shing / mthar gser 'bum phrag bzhi'i yo byad sbyin sreg tu phul bas 'phags
pa spyan ras gzigs zhal mngon sum du bstan nas/ khyod ci 'dod gsum ba la/ bdag grub pa chen po brgyad kyis sems can gyi don bya bar 'dod pas nag po chen po mngag gzhug tu
'tshal zhus pas de bzhin du gnang nas/ deng phyin chad du rig sngags thams cad ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du grub cing / ri lu la sogs pa grub pa brgyad po stong phrag res sems
can rnams la phan btags so/ /grub pa thob pa stong phrag brgyad po de dag kyang khong la bla mar 'dzin/rig pa mtha' dag kyang ma bslabs par rang shes so/ /de nas nub phyogs
kyi yul du song nas rgyal po sandi wa ha na zhes bya ba longs spyod chen po dang ldan pa'i yul du gnas so/ /der yang sngags dang rgyud kyi sbyor bas sems can la phan
'dogs shing gnas pa las/ wa ra Na sir 'ongs pa'i tshe/ bar skabs der byung bi rgyal po ba'i ma shu la zhes bya ba'i yul du'ang sems can gyi don rgya chen po byas te/ skabs
der ka lI dA sa'i lo rgyus sbyar/

de nas lho phogs su phyin/ rgyal po bde byed sgra slob par 'dod pa la/ sgra pA Ni yongs su rdzogs par shes pa'i slob dpon ma rnyed nas/ klu'i rgyal po she Sha zhes bya ba pA
Ni pa yongs su rdzogs pa shes pa zhig yod par shes nas/ bram ze mchog sred kyi rig sngags kyi mthus bkug nas shlau ka 'bum gyi pA Ni pa'i don thams cad rgya cher 'grel
nus par 'chad par byas shing / slob dpon gyis yi ger 'bri ba las/ de gnyis kyi bar du yol bas chod par byas so/ /shlau ka stong phrag nyi shu rtsa lnga song ba na/ de'i lus
ni ci 'dra snyam slob dpon gyis yol ba btegs nas bltas pas/ sbrul chen po 'gying ba mthong / klu yang ngo tsha nas bros so/ /de man chad du slob dpon nyid kyis 'grel pa
byas te/ de la ni tshigs su bcad pa stong phrag bcu gnyis kyi tshad las med do/ /de gnyis bsdoms pa la klus bstan pa'i brda sprod pa zhes grags/ der sgra la sogs pa'i rig
pa'i gnas rnams kyang mang du bstan/ mthar nag po chen pos phrag pa la thogs te/ ri rab kyi rtse mo yongs 'du sa brtol gyi gnas su gshegs so/ /zhes grags so/ /der rgyal
po bde byed slob dpon mchog sred kyis byas pa'i 'grel pa la yid ma ches par/ bram ze sapta warma gzhon nu gdong drug bsgrub tu bcug go/ /grub nas khyod ci 'dod zer ba la/
indra byA ka ra Na shes par 'tshal lo byas pas/ siddhi warNas ma nA ya/ zhes brjod pa tsam gyis sgra'i don mda' dag shes so/ /sngar bod du grags pa'i lo rgyus ltar na/
ka lA pa'i kun bshad bzhi

pa yan chad gzhon nu gdong drug gis bshad cing / ka lA pa zhes pa cha bsags kyi don rma bya'i mjug sgro kha dog sna tshogs pa bsags pa'i don du 'chad mod/ 'dir ni de ltar ma
grags te/ ka lA pa ni sapta warma nyid kyis brtsams la cha bsags kyi don ni nye bar mkho ba'i cha shas mtha' dag bsags pa'o/ /zhes pa'i don no/ /de bzhin du slob dpon 'di'i
ming la dbang phyug go cha zhes bya ba yin cing / sarba warma zhes pa yang yin nor brgyud pa ste/ sapta warma bdun pa'i go cha yin no/ kA li da sa'i lo rgyus ni/ wa
ra Na si'i rgyal po bi ma shukla'i mchod gnas su bram ze mchog sred yod pa'i tshe/ rgyal po'i bu mo dpyid ldan ma zhes ba ba bram ze mchog sred la sbyin par byas pa las/
dpyid ldan ma nga rgyal gyis dregs pas mchog sred las kho mo mkhas pa'i phyir g.yog mo mi byed do zhes byas so/ /der mchog sred kyis 'di rdzan gyis bslu bar bya'o snyam nas/
'o na bdag gi slob dpon mkhas pa/ bdag las blo gros brgya 'gyur gyis che ba zhig yod pa de spyan drangs la/ de la rgyal pos dpyid ldan ma stsol cig ces bas nas/ ma ga
dha'i gnag rdzi gzugs bzang pa zhig shing gi yal ga'i rtse mo la gnas te/ yal ga'i rtsa ba la ste'u bsnun par byed pa mthong nas/ shin tu blan par shes te/ de bos nas zhag
'gar khrus dang bku mnyi phun sum tshogs par byas/ bram ze paNDe ta'i cha byad du bcos/ i swasti zhes bya pa gcig bu bslabs te/ rgyal po skye bo'i tshogs dang bcas pa'i
bzhugs/ rgyal po la me tog gtor te/ i swasti zhes bya ba

'di brjod cig gzhas su zhig gis dris kyang lan 'debs par ma byed cig ces bsgos te de ltar byed rgyu la/ de ngag btab ste rgyal po la me tog gtor nas/ u sha ra Ta zhes zer ro/
der slob dpon gyis yi ge bzhi po de dag gi don bkrol te/ u ma ya sa hi to ru tra/ shangka ra sa ni twa bi ShNu Tam ka ra shrA la pA NiShatsa/ rakShantu shi ba sarba ta
zhes pa'i don te/ shis pa brjod pa yin zhes kha bsgyur ro/ /tshig de bod skad du bsgyur na/ u ma dang bcas drang po dang / bde byed dang bcas 'jug sel te/ TaM tshul phyag
na mdung thung yang / zhi bas rtag tu bsrung bar mdzod/ ces so/ /de nas dpyid ldan mas skra'i don la sogs pa dris kyang cang mi smra la/ mchog sred kyis bdag gi slob dpon
mkhas pa 'di bud med kyis dris pa la lan ci la 'debs/ zhes rmongs par byas nas/ bram ze mchog sred lho phyogs su bros so/ unauditedde nas lha khang rnams su khrid kyang
cang me smra'o/ /mthar lha khang gi phyi khyams su srog chags sna tshogs pa'i gzugs bris pa la/ pa lang gi gzugs brnyan mthong ba dang dga' ste/ phyugs skyong ba'i rnam
'gyur byed do/ /de nas kye ma ho 'di ni pa lang rdzi'o zhes te bslus par shes so/ /blo dang ldan na sgra bslab par bya'o zhes brtags pas skye bo shin tu blo rtul bar byung
ste/ dpyid ldan mas kyang sdang por byas shing / nyin re bzhin me tog 'thu ru btang ngo / /ma ga dha'i phyogs gcig na lha mo nag mo'i sku ya'i batho bos rgyas pa

zhig yod de/ nyin re bzhin de la me tog mang du phul nas phyag btsal te gus pas gsol ba btab pas dus nam zhig na/ dpyid ldan ma lha la mchod pa'i dus shig la/ des tho rangs
me tog 'thu ru song ba'i tshe dpyid ldan ma'i g.yog mo zhig kyal ka'i don du go la mur bzhin du lha mo nag mo'i rten gyi rgyab tu yib cing 'dug go/ /phyugs rdzi des sngar
bzhin gsol ba btab pa'i tshe/ g.yog mo des go la mur 'phro lag tu gtad pas/ 'di ni lha mos dngos grub tu gnang ba yin no snyam du sems shing yid ches so/ /de nyid blo gros
thogs pa med pas rtog ge dang / brda sprod pa dang / snyan ngag smra ba chen por gyur te/ lag pa g.yas su padma'i me tog dang / g.yon du utpal zhig thogs te/ padma ni
me tog bzang yang yu ba rtsub/ utpal ni me tog chung yang yu ba 'jam pas gang zhig 'dod/ ces pa'i don la bdag gi lag pa g.yas na padma dang / /g.yon na de bzhin utpala'i
me tog /'jam pa'i yul ba'am rtsub pa'i yu ba can/ /gang 'dod long zhig padma'i mig can ma/ /zhes brjod pas mkhas par song ba shes te bkur sti chen po byas/des lha mo nag
mo la shin tu gus par byas pas/ kA li da sa ste nag mo'i 'bangs sam nag mo'i khol por grags/ dus de tsam na snyan ngag mkhan mtha' dag gi gtsug gi nor bur gyur/ sprin gyi
pho nya la sogs pa pho nya brgyad dang / gzhon nu 'byung ba la sogs pa'i snyan ngag gi bstan bcos che ba yang mang du brtsams/ 'di dang sapta warma gnyis ka grub mtha'
ni phyi

rol pa zhig go/ /zhes 'byung ngo / /lnga pa bod du 'gyur tshul bshad pa la gsum ste/ thu mi sam bho Ta'i dus su brda sprod pa'i dbu brnyes tshul/ ska cog dang rin chen bzang
pos srol btod tshul/ bdag nyid chen po sa paN dang / shong dpang yab sras kyi skabs su dar zhing rgyas tshul bshad pa'o/ /dang po ni/ rje btsun sprul pa'i lo tsA ba chos
skyong bzang po'i gsung las/ bod yul dbus kyi rgyal po mchog /gnam ri srong btsan yan chad la/ /bod la yi ge med ces grags/ chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po'i dus/ /mkhan
po thu mi sam bho Tas/ /latstsha'i yi ge dper mdzad nas/ dbyangs yig i u e o bzhi/ /gsal byed ka sogs sum cu mdzad/ /de las rjes su 'jug pa bcu/ /de las kyang ni sngon 'jug
lnga/ /ra la sa yi mgo gsum dang / /ya ra la yi smad 'dogs gsum/ /da dang sa yi yang 'jug sogs/ /ston pa'i bstan bcos rnam brgyad mdzad/ /bka' srol de nyid la brten nas/
/lo paN skyes mchog du ma yis/ /rgya gar rgya nag kha che dang / /li dang bal po'i yul sogs nas/ /thub pa'i gsung rab sna tshogs bsgyur/ /brda yang mi 'dra sna tshogs
bsgyur/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ /bod yul mun pa'i gling 'dir brjod pa sna tshogs kyi skad gdangs yod kyang / rjod byed kyi yi ge med pas/ gsung rab dang / lugs brgya'i gtsug
lag bzang po'i srol lam med pa ni/ dper na skyes bu blo dang ldan yang smra ba'i lce med pa dang tshul mtshungs par gyur pa'i tshe/ de dag thugs brtse bas rjes su bzung
bar bzhed nas/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid mi'i gzugs kyi rnam

par rol pa mkhan po thu mi sam bho Ta zhes bya ba chos kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i dus su byung bar gyur te/ de yang thu mi a nu'i bu thu mi sam bho zhes bya ba rgya
gar du brdzangs paNDi ta lha rig pa'i seng ge dang / yig mkhan bram ze li byin la sogs pa la yi ge dang brda sprod pa'i tshul legs par bslabs/ mkhas par mkhyen/ bod du byon
nas/ lha sa'i pho brang dgu mkhar mar bod la nye bar mkho ba'i gzugs 'cho bar mdzad de/ de yang rgya gar gyi phyi mo lnga bcu las/ bod du phyi mo sum cur byas/ dbyangs
bcu drug las i u e o bzhi rnams dbyangs su mdzad/ a gsal byed du bsdus/ gsal byed las kyang Ta'i sde pa dor/ sde pa bzhan bzhi'i yang / bzhi pa rnams dang Sha rnams mi
dgos par gzigs nas bzhag tsa tsha dza rnams rgya gar shar phyogs pa 'ga' zhig ca cha ja zhes te de gsum bkod/ rgya gar la med kyang bod la zha za 'a rnams dgos par dgongs
te btsud/ de dag la nye bar mkho ba'i yan lag tu brda sprod pa'i gzhung tshan pa brgyad tsam mdzad par grags na'ang / bstan pa 'phel 'grib kyi dbang gis phal cher nub nas
mi snang la/ sum cu pa dang rtags kyi 'jug pa gnyis ni ding sang du yang mkhas pa dpyod ldan thams cad kyis tshad grub tu mdzad cing / rgya gar mkhas pa'i gzhung lugs ltar
rtogs dka' zhing / rtogs na gzhung don phun sum tshogs la gsung rab spyi la 'jug na yang gsal byed kyi mig lta bur gyur pa zhig ste/ de yang gzhung 'di nyid kyi yi ge'i
rnam gzhag dang 'jug tshul sogs bod kyi skad gsung rab dang sbyor tshul rang tshugs thub par bshad cing / brdo sprod pa'i gzhung lugs chen po rnams dang sbyar na/ sum
cu pa las ka lA pa'i ming le

dang bshad tshul mtshungs shing / rtags 'jug gi kun bshad kyi brjod don 'brel ba yin no/ /de ltar bstan bcos dang yi ge de dag rgyal po srong btsan sgam pos kyang slob tshul
yun ring du bstan/ thu mis thog mar mdo sde za ma tog bkod pa dang / mdo sde dkon mchog sprin sogs bsgyur/ gzhan yang bod kyi slob dpon dharma ko sha sogs blo gsal mang
po la bshad pas/ bstan pa rin po che'i srol legs par tshugs/ rab byung gi gra med kyang rgyal pos spyan ras gzigs kyi chos skor mang du gsungs shing / de dag gi sgom gra
legs par btsugs pas/ thar pa bla na med pa'i go 'phang thob pa yang mang du byung ba yin no/ /de ltar bstan bcos 'di nyid dgongs pa 'grel ba'i bstan bcos phyis su byung
ba yang / bdag nyid chen po bsod nams rtse mo'i byis pa bde blag tu 'jug pa/ 'jam dbyangs sa paNDi tas de'i 'grel pa dang / sgra'i bstan bcos mkhas pa'i kha rgyan/ dbus pa
blo gsal gyi sum rtags kyi 'grel pa/ sgra pa sangga shrI'i sum cu pa'i 'grel pa/ yar 'brog pa rin chen tog gi rtags 'jug gi 'grel pa/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan gyi sum
rtags kyi don 'grel pa chos la 'jug pa'i sgo/ kun mkhyen gau rab 'byams pa'i rtags kyi 'jug pa'i TI ka/ snyigs dus kyi 'jig rten mtha' dag gi mig zha lu lo tsA ba chen po'i
sum rtags kyi 'grel pa/ karma pa'i sum rtags kyi 'grel pa/ don 'grel yi ge'i brda dag ston pa la lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis nyer mkho bsdus pa/ dbus pa blo gsal
gyi phrad kyi gnad bsdus pa'i 'grel chung / snye thang pa grags

bzang gi ganggA'i chu rgyun/ gtsang nag sbug pa thuT rje seng ge'i bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun/ stag tshang gzhon nu dpal gyi 'od zer brgya pa/ bu ston seng ge 'od kyi sgra don rgya
mtsho'i me long / rje byams pa gling pa'i smra ba'i rgyan/ bsam sdings pa kun bzang gi 'bral pa spong ba/ rje btsun zha la u lo chen gyi za ma tog bkod pa/ dpal khang
lo tsA ba'i ngag gi sgron ma/ thams cad mkhyen pa klu sgrub rgya mtshos slob ma phan pa la sogs pa mang du yod pa yin no/ gnyis pa ska cog dang rin chen bzang pos srol btong
tshul ni/ zha lu lo chen gyis/ /chos rgyal ral pa can gyi dus/ ska cog zhang gsum mkhas mang gis/ /rgyal po'i bkas bskul gsar bcad kyi/ /skad kyis brda sbyar gtan la
phab/ /slad nas rin chen bzang po dang / /blo ldan shes rab la sogs pa/ /mkhas mchog rnams kyi de la brten/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ sang skabs su lo tsA ba chen po ska cog
zhang gsum dang / rin chen bzang po/ /blo ldan shes rab la sogs pa rnams kyis tshul 'di'i srol ches cher btod par mdzad pa yin te/ de yang rgyal po khri ral pa can gyi dus
su rgyal blon rnams kyi bka' bskul te/ sngon lha sras yab kyi ring la mkhan po / ye shes dbang po/ zhang rgyal nyen nyi bzang / blon po khri sher sang / lo tsA pa dznyA
de wa ko Sha/ lce khyi 'brug bram ze a nanta la sogs pas 'gyur mdzad pa rnams la chos kyi skad bod la ma grags pa mang dag cig byung zhing / rgya dkar nag dang / li dang
/ za hor la sogs pa yul sna tshogs nas bskur bas yul de dag gi brda si 'dra pa mang pos chos slob dka' bar gzigs nas 'og gi mkhas pa A tsarYa dzi na mi tra dang / su rendra
sa nyi dang /

dhi dang / dA na shI la dang / bod kyi mkhan po ratna rakShi ta dang / dharma shrI la dang / lo tsA ba mkhas par tshud pa ska ba dpal brtsegs/ cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan/ dznyA
na se na ste zhang ye shes sde dang / dza ya rakShi ta dang / manydzu shI warma dang / ra nantra shI la la sogs pas theg pa che chung las byung ba'i chos rgya gar skad
las bod kyi skad du bsgyur zhing / ming du btags pa rnams dkar chag tu bris nas nam du yang gzhung lugs de ga las mi bsgyur zhing / kun gyis slob tu rung bar gyis shig
ces bka' stsal pa la brten nas/ sngar bsgyur ba rnams skad gsar bcad kyis gtan la phab/ bkas bcad rnam pa gsum mdzad de/ skad dod so so dang bsgyur tshul yig char bkod/ sde
pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba las gzhan dang / gsang sngags rnams rgyal blo paN dang bcas pa mthun grub na ma gtogs/ lko tu mi bsgyur bar bkas bcad/ tha na bre dang
srang zho la sogs pa yang rgya gar dang mthu par bcos/ de thams cad lo paN rYal blon dang bcas pa'i phyag rgyas btab/ dkar chag tu bkod de/ bod 'bangs thams cad la de dag
las mi 'da' bar dril bsgrags pa yin no/ ji skad du yang sgra sbyor bam gnyis las/ rta'i lo la btsan po khri lde srong btsan pho brang 'on cang rdo na bzhugs/ stod smad
kyi dmag rje dang rkun chen btul/ gar log gi pha nyas phyag btsal/ blon chen zhang khri zur ram shags dang / blon ma rje lha mdo la sogs pas bya las gnang mang bcad de/
rnga rta dang ba mar phal mo che phyag tu phul/ zhang blon man chad so sor bya dga' stsal pa'i lan la/ nyi 'og gi mkhan po

su renda bo dhi dang / shI lendra bo dhi dang / dA na shI la dang / bo dhi mi tra dang / bod kyi mkhan po ratna rakSha ta dang dharma ta shi dang / lo tsA ba mkhas par tshud
pa dznyA na se na dang / manydzu shri warma dang / ra nendra shi logs pas/ theg pa che chung gi chos las byung ba'i rgya gar gyi skad las bod kyi skad du bsgyur zhing ming
du btags pa rnams dkar chag tu bris te/ nam du yang gzhung lugs de las mi 'gyur zhing / kun gyi slob tu rung bar gyis shig /ces bka' stsal nas sngon lha sras yab kyi
ring la A tsarYa bo dhi ratwa dang / ye shes dbang po dang / zhang rgyal nyen nyi bzang dang / blon po khri sher sang shI dang / lo tsA ba snyi de ba ko Sha dang / lce khyi
'brug dang / bram ze a nanta la sogs pas chos kyi skad bod la ma grags pa las/ ming du btags pa dag cig mchis pa'i nang nas/ kha cig chos kyi gzhung dang / byA ka ra Na'i
lugs dang mi mthun te/ mi bcos su mi rung ba rnams kyang bcos/ skad kyi ming gce so 'tshal gyis bsnan nas theg pa che chung gi gzhung las ji skad 'byung ba dang / gna'i
mkhan po chen po nA gardzu na dang / bha su bantra la sogs pas ji ltar bshad pa dang / byA ka ra Na'i lugs las ji skad du/ 'dren pa dang yang bstun te mjal dka' ba rnams
kyang tshig so sor bkral nas gtan tshigs kyi bshad de gzhung du bris/ skad kyang pa bshad mi 'tshal ba sgra ji bzhin du bsgyur ba'i rigs pa rnams kyang sgra btsan par
bgyis te ming du btags/ skad kha cig don bzhin du gdags pa'i rigs pa rnams kyang don btsan par bgyis te ming du btags te/ btsan po'i spyan sngar bandhe chen po yon tan dang
/ bandhe chen po ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'ang 'tshogs te/ rje blon gdan 'joms pa la zhus te/ dharma bsgyur

ba'i thabs dang / rgya gar gyi skad las bod kyi skad du ming gdags pa'i rnam gzhag bkas bcad de gtan la phab/ dam pa'i chos bsgyur ba'i lugs ni sgra dang mthun la/ don dang
yang mi 'gal la/ bod skad las kyang gar bde bar gyis shig dharma bsgyur ba la rgya gar gyi skad go rim las mi nor bar bod kyi skad du bsgyur na don dang tshig tu 'brel zhing
/ bde na ma bsnor bar sgyur zhig bsnor na bde zhing go ba bskyed pa zhig yod na/ tshiT bcad la ni rtsa ba bzhi pa'am drug pa'ang rung ste/ tshigs su bcad pa gcig gi
nang gar bde bar bsnor zhing sgyur cig rkyang pa la ni don gar snyegs pa yan chad kyi tshig dang don gnyis ka la gar bde bar bsnor zhing sgyur cig skad cig la ming du ma
'dren pa ste/ ltag 'og dang bstun la gar snyegs pa bzhin du ming thogs shig /gau ta ma lta bu gau'i sgra las/ tshig dang / phyogs dang / sa dang / 'od dang / rdo rje dang
/ pa lang dang / mtho res la sogs pa rnam pa du mar snyegs pa dang / go'u shi ka dha bu rtswa ku sha thogs pa dang / mkhas pa dang pad ma la dga' ba la/ 'ug pa dang mdzod
ldan la sogs pa sgra'i lugs las drangs shing bsgyur na/ rnam grangs mang po zhig tu snyegs la/ bsgyur ba rnam pa gcig gi nang du ni/ rnam grangs de kun 'du yang mi btul
ste/ gcig tu chad par bya gtan tshigs chen po med pa rnams ni mi bsgyur bar/ rgya gar gyi skad so na zhog cig gar yang drang du rung ba'i tshig byung na/ phyogs gcig tu
'chad par mi bsgyur bar/ spyir snyegs su rung bar gyis shig yul dang sems can dang / me tog dang rtsi shing la sogs pa'i ming bsgyur ba mi go zhing tshig mi bde ba dang /
'ol cir bsgyur du rung yang don du de ltar

yin nam min gtol med pa rnams ni 'go la yul zhes sam/ me tog ces bya ba gang la bya ba'i ming zhig bla thabs su bsnon la/ rgya gar gyi skad so na zhog cig grangs la rgya gar
gyi skad bzhin du bsgyur na/ dge slong brgya phrag phyed dang bcu gsum zhes 'byung ba la sogs pa ni/ stong nyis brgya lnga bcu zhes tha mal par bod kyi lugs bzhin du bsgyur
na don dang yang mi 'gal la/ bod kyi skad la yang bde bas grangs bsdom du rung ba rnams bod kyi lugs bzhin du thogs shig /sa ri dang / sam dang / u pa lta bu la sogs
pa tshig gi phrad dang rgyan lta bur 'byung ba rnams bsgyur na/ don dang mthun zhing 'byor ba'i thabs ni/ yongs su zhe'am/ yang dag pa zhe'am/ nye ba zhes sgra ji bzhin
du sgyur cig don lhag par snyegs pa med pa rnams ni tshig gi lhad kyis bsnan mi dgos kyi don bzhin du thoT shig rnam grangs su gtogs pa'i tshig rnams ni ma 'dogs na ming
gang / bod skad du phyir gdags shing tshig tu gang bde bar gdags so/ 'doms na so sor btags pa bzhin du thogs shig sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos la sogs
pa la zhe sa dang / ko long gi tshig gi rim pa ni/ sangs rgyas la zhe sa'i tshig tu bsgyur/ gzhan ma tshig 'bring po yan chad tsam du bya ste/ sngon lha sras yab kyi spyan
sngar mkhan po dang lo tsA ba mkhas pa tshogs pas/ dharma dkon mchog sprin dang / 'phags pa langkar gshegs pa bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'i lugs bzhin du sgyur cig skad kyi
lugs 'di ltar bkas bcad pa las so sor nas su 'chos shing 'og tu ming gsar du 'dogs su mi gnang gi /bsgyur ba dang 'chad pa'i gra so so nas skad gsar du ming gdags dgos
pa zhig na/ so so'i gra grar ming chad pa ma gdags

par/ chos kyi gzhung dang / sgra'i lugs las ji ltar 'byung ba'i gtan tshigs dang chos la ji skad du gdags pa spyod de/ pho brang du bcom ldan 'das kyi ring lugs kyi 'dun sa
dang / dharma zhu chen 'tshal ba'i grar phul la snyan du zhus te bkas bcad nas skad kyi dkar chag gi dkyus su bsnon/ gsang sngags kyi rgyud rnams gzhung gis gsang bar bya
ba yin te/ snod du ma gyur pa rnams la bshad cing bstan du yang mi rung la/ bar du bsgyur zhing dpyod du gnang gis kyang / ldem po'i ngag tu bshad pa ma khrol nas/ sgra
ji bzhin du 'dzin cing log par spyod pa dag kyang 'byung / sngags rgyud ni nang nas thu zhing bod skad du bsgyur ba dag kyang 'byung / zhes gdags kyi/ phyin chad gzungs
sngags dang / bla nas bka' stsal te bsgyur du bcug pa ma gtogs pa sngags kyi rgyud dang / sngags kyi tshig thu zhing bsgyur du mi snang ngo / /zhes gsungs pa ltar de ltar
sngar dar gyi skabs su sgra'i yig cha byung ba ni/ lo tsA ba lce khyi 'brug gis sgra'i gnas brgyad pa rtsa 'grel/ lo tsA ba spyis thun mong du bye brag rtogs byed che 'bring
chung gsum sgra sbyor bam po gnyis pa sogs so/ /de dag gi rjes su zhugs nas bstan pa phyi dar gyi skabs su lo tsA ba rnams kyi mchog rin chen bzang po dang / blo ldan
shes rab la sogs pas kyang gtso bor lo tsA ba rnams kyi brda chad las ma g.yos shing / cung zad bcos pa gnyi zla la nyi zla dang / bstan chos la bstan bcos dang / stug
po la mthug po la sogs pa yod do/ /de ltar brda gsar rnying gi bye brag rnam par 'byed tshul yang / dbus

pa blo gsal gyi bstan bcos thor bu kha re dang / paN chen shAka mchog gi brda'i bye brag rnam par 'byed pa'i bstan bcos/ smin drug lo tsA ba'i legs par bshad pa li sha'i gur
khang la sogs pa rnams la rtog par bya'o/rtsa ba'i gsum pa bdag nyid chen po sa paN dang / shong ston yab sras kyi skabs su dar zhing rgyas tshul bshad pa ni/ kun shes
las/ snga ma'i byings mdo yi ge'i mdo 'grel bcas/ phyi ma'i byings mdo uN 'grel par bcas/ /byings dang kun bshad dpung gnyen si sogs kyi/ /bya ba rgyas pa la sogs mang po
dang / /snga ma'i supra mtha' rin chen 'byung ldan sogs/ /sgra yi yan lag sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung / /snyan ngag me long mngon brjod 'chi med mdzod/ /kun tu dga' ba'i
zlos gar la sogs pa/ /shong dpang yab sras rnams kyis bsgyur zhing bshad/ /sgra dang snyan ngag sdeb sbyor mngon brjod dang / /zlos gar rnams la rig gnas chung ngu 'am/ /tha
snyad rig pa'i gnas lngar grags pa rnams/ /chos rje sa paN yan la ma dar zhing / /thar lo yan la sgra mdo 'gyur ba med/ /sgra rig brjod bya spros te bshad na ni/ /zhes
gsungs pa ltar ro/ /'di dag ni don legs par 'grel ba la sa bcad rnam pa gsum ste/ dang por bka' drin che ba bdag nyid chen po sa paN byon tshul/ bar du bka' drin che ba
shong dpang yab sras byon tshul/ mthar bka' drin che ba zha lu lo tsA ba chos skyong bzang po byon tshul bshad pa'o/ /dang po ni/ skye ba du mar sbyangs pa dang / /mkhas
pa du ma bsten pa dang / /rnam par dpyod pa'i blo gros gyis/ /shes bya kun la 'jigs med thob/ /ces rang nyid kyi zhal gyis bzhes shing mkhas pa thams cad kyi tshad mar gyur

pa/ bod du rig gnas rnam pa bcu'i srol gang zag gcig nyid kyi dang por phye ba ni bdag nyid chen po sa paNDi ta kho na ste/ de yang / yab dpal chen 'od po dang / yum nyi khri
lcam gyi sras su 'khrungs pa nas bzung ste/ rnam thar rgyas pa ni gzhan du shes shing / 'dir rig gnas kyi tshul legs par gsan pa'i tshul cung zad brjod na/ go mkhyen tsam
gyi dus kyi ba snga ma'i bag chags sad pa'i stobs kyis saMskraM ta'i skad du ma smra ba byung bas/ yum na re/ 'di la rang ga gcig pa yong ba legs sam/ gtam go rgyu med
pa'i ngag ngog mang po zer ba zhig gda' zhus pas/ rje bas saMskraM ta'i skad mkhyen pas/ khyod kyi la (gu) ba byung dogs med gsungs/ yang sa la phyag mdzub kyis nA ga ra
dang / lanytsha'i dbyangs gsal bris nas klog tshul mdzad/ mi 'gom par phyag gis byil phyis nas gtong ba byung / thog mar rang gi yab las kye rdor gyi dbang sogs nod/ yi
ge'i bye brag du ma dang / rtsis dang gso dpyad ri mo la sogs pa mthar phyin par bslabs/ rje btsun rin po che la dbang rgyud man ngag sogs gsang sngags yab chos thams cad
dang / rig gnas kyi cha shas 'ga' zhig kyang gsan pas tshegs med du thugs su chud/de nas dge bshes zhu la sogs pa'i bod ston du ma las/ bod la yongs su grags pa'i chos
skor thams cad gsan pas thams cad tshar re la thugs su chud/ lhag par rje btsun chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi drung du lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs zhus
pas/ dus de nyid du bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs su gzigs/ chos thams cad skad cig la thugs su chud/ des bya'i

gnas thams cad la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa thob pa yin te/ bstod pa mdzad pas kyang / zab mo'i lam gyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshe/ /zhes sogs gsung pa lta bu'o/ /'on kyang tha
snyad du gnas bcu gsan nas srol phye tshul cung zad brjod na/ thog mar sgra rig pa la/ rje btsun chen po grags pa'i zhabs drung du sgra'i gnas brgyad smra sgo la sogs
pa rnams gsan cing / de nas 'dzam bu gling gi rgyan dam par gyur pa/ kha che'i bsod snyoms pa chen po mahA paNDi ta shAkya shrI la sgra ka tsan snying po bsdu ba la sogs
pa'i sgra'i mdo rnams rags rim gsan cing / nub phyogs a ti na war sku 'khrungs pa'i bram ze'i slob dpon chen po surga ta shrI dpal ldan sa skyar spyan drangs nas lo gnyis
kyi bar du ka lA pa rtsa ba dang / de'i 'grel pa stong phrag drug pa dang bcas pa/ ming sgrub pa su wanti/ byings sgrub pa ti wanti/ rab tu sgrub pa mtha' dag gsan/ paNDi
ta chen po sangga shrI la tsandra pa/ de'i ming dang byings kyi sgrub pa rnams mtha' chod dang bcas pa gsan nas khong du chud par mdzad de/ de dag gi tshul gsal bar ston
pa la/ skra la 'jug pa'i rnam bshad/ mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgo/ smra sgo'i don bsdu la sogs pa mdzad nas/ sgra rig pa'i phyogs kyi srol legs par btod pa yin te/ nyid kyi gsung
las/ gzhan dag gis ni sngon chad lugs 'byung 'di/ /gangs ri'i ngogs 'dir rgyas par ma mdzad la/ /de na mkhas pa rnams kyang rmongs gyur pas/ /'di la kho bo blo gros
gsal phyir dbye/ /zhes gsungs shing / dpal khang lo tsA ba'i bstod par yang / indra pA Ni byA kar cha bsags so/ /legs sbyar rgya mtsho de nyid

skad cig la/ /gzigs tshe brda sprod byed pa sarbadznyA/ /skabs gsum bla ma'i stan las babs sam snyam/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de bzhin du tshad ma rig pa yang bod ston rnams
la mang du gsan cing / khyad par kha che paN chen la rnam 'grel le'u dang po'i 'grel pa stong phrag phyed dang bzhi pa yan gsan nas bsgyur cing zhus/ slob dpon thar pa'i
'byung gnas zhes bya ba'i rtog ge'i skad ces pa'i bstan bcos gsan cing bsgyur/ gzhan phyi rol rig byed kyi tshad ma drang srong chen po gzegs zan gyis sbyar ba'i rtog
ge'i bstan bcos rig pa zhes bya ba sogs gsan cing / mdor na sde bdun mdo dang bcas pa'i yan lag thams cad thugs su chud cing / de dag gi don 'brel bar byed pa tshad ma rigs
pa'i gter rtsa 'grel gnyis mdzad pa yin cing / nyid kyi gsung las/ shes bya'i mkha' la thogs med rgyu nus shing / /phas rgol nyi zla'i gzi brjid za nus kyang / /rtag tu
skye bo kun gyis ma mthong ba'i/ /kun dga' rgyal mtshan nam mkha'i sgra gcan 'dra/ /zhes gsangs shing / /bstod pa mdzad pas kyang / /tshad ma gsum gyi gnas gsum gzhal bya'i
don/ ma lus rtogs pas sgrub dang sun 'byin gyi/ /ma rtogs log rtog the tshom tshar gcod par/ /sde bdun mdzad pa'i blo bdun khyod kyi mtshan/ /zhes gsungs so/ /yang sdeb
sbyor gsan pa'i tshul yang / paNDi ta sangga shrI la dmar ser dang rgyal ba'i lhas mdzad pa'i sdeb sbyor gyi gzhung / khyad par de dag las yon tan brgyad kyis khyad par
du 'phags pa slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi

bas mdzad pa'i sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas dang / 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi brita ma la sogs pa gsan nas legs par khong du chud/ de dag gi don 'grel pa la sdeb sbyor sna
tshogs me tog gi chun po mdzad de rig gnas 'di'i srol legs par phye ba yin te/ gzhung de nyid du/ sngon chad gangs ri'i khrod dir mkhas rnams kyi/ /rna ba'i snod du nye bar
ma lhung zhing / lce yi dbang po kun nas ma myangs pa/ /ro brgya'i 'byung gnas dpag bsam shing 'di skyed/ /ces gsungs shing / bstod pa mdzad pas kyang / dmar ser rgyal
lha'i lugs las khyad par du/ /yon tan brgyad kyis 'phags pa'i sdeb sbyor gzhung / br-itta dzA ti'i ngo mtshar rtogs byed la/ /zhi ba'i zhabs dang khyod blo mthun mong gyur/
/zhes gsungs so/ /snyan ngag gi rig pa ni/ rje btsun chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan la skyes rabs so bzhi pa dang / gzhon nu ma bdud gyi rtogs pa brjod pa la sogs pa'i
skyes rabs kyi rigs du ma gsan cing / paNDi ta sangga shrI la snyan ngag gi bstan bcos chen po gsum dang chung ngu gsum/ rgyan gyi bstan bcos dbyangs can gyi mgul rgyan
stong phrag brgyad pa dpag bsam 'khri shing la sogs pa mtshan nyid dang mtshan gzhi ston pa'i bstan bcos mang du gsan zhing / lhag par daNDi'i tshig rgyan la mkhas par bslabs
te/ de dag gi brjod don ma lus pa mdor bsdus pa'i pa'i tshul gyis/ mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgor gtan la phab pas rig gnas 'di nyid kyi srol bla na med pa phye ba yin te/
bdag nyid chen po'i gsung las/ 'ga' zhig sgra dang rnam par dbye ba dang / khams dang byed tshig dpe dang tshig gi rgyan/ /dbye bsdu grangs dang go rim nges pa

la/ /'di na phal cher rmongs par mthong nas 'dir/ /mang du thos shing mthong nas goms pa dang / /man ngag dbang gis dpal ldan kun dga' yi/ /rgyal mtshan 'di na 'ga' tsam 'chad
pa la/ /mkhas pa rnams kyis dga' ba bskyed de nyon/ /zhes gsungs shing / /bstod pa mdzad pas kyang / /dbyangs can lang tsho zag zad ye shes kyi/ /rtse dgas thugs yid
gcugs pa'i seng ge brtsen/ /tshig rgyan bal la ki ste lha'i rol sgras/ /yid bsgyur khams gsum dbugs 'byin snyan ngag mkhan/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de bzhin du mngon brjod
kyi rim pa yang bod du yongs su grags pa'i sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhir gsungs pa'i ming gi tshogs mtha' yas pa dang / de dag kyang 'dod rgyal dang / rjes grub 'dra
'brel sogs so sor phye zhing / bkas bcad thog mtha' bar gsum du grags pa ltar/ brda gsar rnying gi bye brag thams cad legs par phyed cing / lhag par mkhas pa chen po
dge 'dun dpal las mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos las yi ge re re'i mngon brjod gsan cing bsgyur/ a ma ra ko Sha dang / sna tshogs gsal ba'i 'grel pa dang bcas pa gsan cing /
de dag sde gsum mam bzhir 'dus shing / rtags gsum gyi rnam dbye legs par phyed pa'i sgo nas rig gnas 'di'i srol cher btod pa yin te/ nyid kyi gsung las/ byang phyogs 'di
na tshig la mkhas pa med/ /legs par shes nas 'chad pa kho bo tsam/ /rtags kyi dbye ba phal cher 'dir mi 'jug /'on kyang bod la mkho ba tsam zhig bsdu/ /zhes gsungs shing
/ bstod pa mdzad pas kyang / tidra supra mtha' dang rtags kyi rnam dbye sogs/ /so sor ma 'dres sna tshogs mngon brjod dag /'chad mkhas mtha' yas ming la

ma rmongs pas/ /'chi med seng ge'i khengs pa thung ngur mdzad/ /ces gsungs so/ de bzhin du zlos gar gyi bstan bcos kyang paNDi ta sangga shrI las gzugs kyi nyi ma'i bstan bcos
dang / dha ra ta la sogs pa gsan cing khong du chud de/ de dag gi tshul phyogs tsam ston pa la rol mo'i bstan bcos zhes bya ba mdzad cing / nyid kyi gsung las kyang /
/sngon chad gzhan gyi yid la ma shar ba/ /'di 'dra gang gis shes de blo gros ldan/ /rgan po rnams kyis yang yang rnam dpyad pa'i/ /don de rtogs kyang de la ngo mtshar med/
/ces gsungs shing / bstod pa mdzad pas kyang / sngon byung zlos pa'i gar de skad rigs bzhi/ /brda sbyor la byang rgya mtsho'i mtha' la sogs/ /tshar phyin thugs chud zin
dang pham zin pa'i/ /sgra skad kun gyis khyod la lung du ston/ /ces gsungs so/ /de bzhin du dus sbyor shes pa yang / rtsis kyi gzhi lo zla dag pa/ lnga bsdus/ sgra gcan/
gza' lnga/ nyi zla gza' 'dzin/ du mjug la sogs 'char ba dang / nub pa'i mtha' dang / de dag gi dge legs kyi rtsis dang / dbyangs 'char la sogs pa'i rtsis rnams kyang phul
du phin pa mkhyen cing / de dag rgan po rnams la grags zin pa'i phyir/ srol 'byed kyi bstan bcos ni ma mdzad la/ legs par gsungs pa'i brgyud pa'i srol ni mang du yod pa
yin no/ /bstod pa mdzad pas kyang / rtsis grangs rig pa kun rdzob rten 'brel che/ za 'og ltar gzigs srid pa'i A darsha/ /dkar nag rtsis la byang ba'i rnam rig gi/ /gtsug
lag rgya mtsho ri byi'i khyor chu bzhin/ /zhes gsungs so/ /

de bzhin du bzo rig pa yang rgya bod kyi mkhas pa rnams las legs par sbyangs shing / ri mo dang sku gzugs kyi mtshan nyid dang / cha tshad la sogs pa mdo rgyud kyi lung dang
mthun par mkhyen cing / zhar byung brtag pa rnam pa brgyad kyang khong du chud/ de dag gi mtshan nyid ston pa'i sku gzugs kyi bstan bcos dang / brtag pa'i bstan bcos sogs
yod par gsungs kyang / deng sang dpe rgyun mthong ba ma byung la/ de'i phyir nyid kyi gsung las/ shes bya'i me tog yon tan dri bsung can/ /snyan pa'i mdog mdzes kun gyis
bsngags na yang / /sbrang rtsi 'dzin pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal/ /bzang po min pas shes bya'i bcud ma rnyed/ /ces gsungs shing / de bzhin du bston pa mdzad pas kyang
/ lus ngag yid dang bzo dang mchog phal gyi/ /gzugs brnyan bskrun la tshad dang 'phrul gyi dbyibs/ /sna tshogs byed po las tshul mtshar sdug gi/ /tshon brgya 'dren pa dpyod
ldan dga' ba'i gnyen/ /zhes sogs dang / gso ba rig pa'i tshul yang / spyir phyi nang gi gzhung lugs du ma las byung ba rnams dang / khyad par yan yag brgyad pa'i snying
po 'grel pa zla zer dang bcas pa thugs su chud cing / de dag gi don legs par ston pa'i bstan bcos yan lag brgyad pa'i bsdus pa zhes bya ba mdzad pa yin te/ ji skad du/
bstod pa mdzad pas/ ma rig rtsa ba zhi brgya rtsa bzhi'i nad/ /'phel zad 'khrug pa'i gnyen po tshe'i rig byed/ /thar pa'i 'tsho srog bsrung ba'i thabs tshul stong / /ji
bzhin mkhyen pa de 'dra gzhan gyis min/ /zhes gsungs so/ /nang rig pa ni/ rgya bod kyi bla ma rnams las/ bsam pa'i ra ba las

'das pa zhig gsan zhing / khyad par rje btsun chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi bka' drin gyis/ mdo rgyud thams cad la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa thob/ lung dang rtogs pa'i yon
tan thams cad mnga' ba yin pas/ de'i tshul rgyas par su zhig gis brjod par nus/ che long tsam brjod na yang mang du dogs pas 'dir rgyas par ma spros la/ dpyod ldan dag gis
gzhan du shes par gyis shig de dag gi tshul ston pa'i bstan bcos kyang / gzhung lugs legs bshad/ thub pa dgongs gsal/ sems bskyed chen mo/ sdom gsum rab dbye/ bdag med
bstod 'grel la sogs pa ji snyed cig yod pa yin pas bka' 'bum du shes par bya'o/ de bzhin du nyid kyi gsung las kyang / bstan pa'i 'jug der bstan la rab gus shing / /bstan
pa mtha' dag bsrung zhing 'dzin 'dod pa/ /shAkya'i dge slong kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal/ /bzang pos bstan la phan phyir 'di sbyar ro/ /zhes gsungs shing / de bzhin du bstod
pa mdzad pas kyang / yongs 'du'i tshal du kumbhi da ra dang / /'od ldan tshogs pa'i mkha' nang nyin byed ltar/ /mkhas mang 'dus pa'i dubs na thams cad mkhyen/ /khyod
dang mtshungs pa sngon dang phyi mthar su/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de ltar na rig gnas rnam pa bcu'i srol legs par phye nas gangs ri'i ljongs kyi blo gsal dag mkhas pa mkhas pa
zhes bya ba'i grangs su chud cing / rigs pa dang mi rigs pa'i tshul mtha' dag 'byed shes pa ni rje btsun nyid kyi sku drin yin la/ de lta bu'i rnam par thar pa gzhan la
son par bzhed nas/ nyid kyi gsung las/ sgra pa nga yin rtog ge pa nga smra ba ngan 'joms nga 'dra med/ /

sdeb sbyor nga mkhas snyan ngag nga nyid mngon brjod 'chad la 'gran med nga / /dus sbyor ngas shes phyi nang kun rig rnam dpyod blo gros mtshungs med nga / /de 'dra gang yin
sa skya pa ste mkhas pa gzhan dag gzugs brnyan yin/ /zhes gsungs shing / rang nyid kyi grel pa'i sgo nas kyang gsal bar mdzad pa yin no/ /gnad des na bod yul gangs ri'i
ljongs 'dir theg pa gsum dang rig gnas cha shas tsam gyis 'gyur dang bshad pa mdzad pa ni sngon dus kyang mang du byung mod/ bdag nyid chen po sa paN ma byon gong du ni
rig gnas rnam pa bcu'i srol cher ma dar la/ dper na nor bu rin po che rdog ma phul du phyin pa yod kyang / de nyid la bug pa phug ste/ srad bu brgyu ba'i lam med na lha dang
mi rnams kyi mgrin pa'i rgyan du ci yang byed mi nus la/ de nyid la bzo bo mkhas pas rdo rje rin po che ste pha lam gyis bug pa phug zin na dar la sogs pa'i skud pa 'jam
pos kyang rin po che rnams phreng bar byas nas mgrin pa'i rgyan du byed nus pa ltar/ bdag nyid chen po rnam par dpyod pa'i blo gros rdo rje rin po che pha lam gyi zegs
mas rig gnas rnam bcu'i nor bu brjod don legs par 'byed pa'i bug pa'i snang bas srol ma phyer bar/ lo tsA ba gzhan mkhas par rlom pa'i rig pa srad bu'i tshogs kyis 'jug
pa thod pa min na/ bod kyi blo gsal rnams kyi mgrin pa'i rgyan du rngo gar yang thogs pa min la/ de'i phyir bdag nyid chen pos srol btod/ shong dpang yab sras kyis dar zhing
rgyas par mdzad nas/ rig gnas rnam pa bcu'i nor bu'i phreng bas bod kyi blo gsal rnams kyi mgrin pa'i rgyan mdzes par byed pa'i shing rta'i srol 'byed ni sa paNDi

ta yin no/ /zhes pa'i snyan grags 'og min gyi bar du khyab bo zhes ston pa la/ bstod pa mdzad pas/ bsil sbyor sgeg mo theg gsum bsgyur bshad kyi/ /snang ba ka tsa li ta'i gos
klubs kyang / /gser zhal mngon du ma 'phyar de srid du/ /rig gnas rgyan gyi lang tsho'i gtam yang ci/ /rin thang che ba'i nor bu rig gnas bcu/ /khyod blo'i rdo rjes yang
dag ma phug bar/ /gzhan rig srad bus 'jug pa thod min na/ /blo gsal mgrin pa'i rgyan du rngo gar thogs/ /de slad 'di na tha snyad shing rta'i srol/ /thog mar 'byed la
ston pa gnyis pa zhes/ /gcig tu dkar ba'i snyan grags A na ka /phyogs kyi mdzes mas brtan g.yo 'jig kyang brdung / /zhes gsung pa yin no/ /de ltar bu'i bka' drin gsab pa
dang / rang nyid kyang dam pa'i rjes su 'jug pa'i phyir/ rjebatsun sa paNDi ta'i gsungs rab la thos bsam bsgom gsum zhe thag pa nas gyis shig ces yang yang du snying nas
gdams pa yin te/ de ltar bgyis pa'i bsod nams kyis 'di phyi'i don thams cad 'grab cing bstan pa la phan pa'i thos bsam bgyis pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang yang bde
blag tu thob pa'i phyir/ de skad du yang nyid kyi gsung las/ des na sangs rgyas gsung rab dang / /mkhas pa rnams kyis mdzad pa yi/ /bstan bcos la ni byin rlabs yod/ /'di
'dra nyan bshad byed pa la/ /thos pa zhes ni brjod pa yin/ /de don spyod pa bsam pa yin/ /nan tan gyis ni de sgrub pa/ /sgom pa yin par shes par bya/ /thos bsam sgom gsum
de ltar yin/ /'di ni sangs rgyas bstan pa yin/ /zhes dang / 'di la dga' bas nyan dang sems rnams kyi/ /sems la 'jam pa'i rdo rjes zhugs nas/ khyad par

tshig gi don la mkhas pa yi/ /nges par byin gyis brlab par bdag gis shes/ /zhes gsungs shing zhal gyis bzhes pa lags so/ /gnyis pa bar du skra drin che ba shong dpang yab sras
ji ltar byon pa'i tshul ni/ de yang thog mar bdag nyid chen pos srol legs par btod pa de nyid rgya gar gyi gzhung phal mo che bsgyur ba dang / bshad pa'i rgyun ches cher
dar bar mdzad pa po ni shong dpang yab sras rnams yin pas bod la bka' drin shin du che'o/ unauditedde yang thog mar shong lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan ni la stod lho'i
dpyad lung shar gyi bong ra zhes par sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu la rab tu byung / go yul ba mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan gyi drung du/ dus 'khor chag lugs/ bde kye phreng ba
skor gsum sogs mang du gsan cing / gar thig rtsis la mkhas par sbyangs/ gza' gsal bar byed pa'i sgron me sogs rtsis kyi bstan bcos mang du mdzad/ de nas tsha nar srag bde
ba'i drung du phar tshad mngon sum la mkhas par sbyabs/ dus 'khor gyi skor shog ldebs bzhi bcu tsam phyag bris su bris nas yon du phul te/ 'bro lugs kyi dbang rgyud bshad
pa man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ 'phags pa rin po ches snga res sa skyar byon pa na bstod pa'i tshigs su bcad pa spel legs phul nas lo tsA slob tu 'gro bas rdzong bar zhu
zhus pas/ de lta bu'i blo skye ba bzang / re zhig gzhung lugs gsar pa bsgyur ba'i nus pa ma byung yang / /paNDi ta la slob gnyer dang dri gtugs legs par gyis shig kho bos
kyang chos rje pa brten yun thungs pas/ sdeb sbyor me tog gi chun po dang / tshig gter sogs tshul bzhin mi shes par

'di dag shes pa zhig cis kyang gyis shig /mkhas par gyur pa'i tshe nged la chos rjes pa'i dgongs pa skong dgos kyi 'gyur 'dra yang dgos pa yod de rjes su byed do gsungs nas/
de dag gi dpe dang gser srang lnga/ dar yug bcu rnams gnang byung ste/ rten 'brel yod pas do nub rje btsun gong ma'i gzims khang dpe khang du nyol la song / slar 'khor
