ba na shog cig gsungs nas brdzangs so/ /shong gi thugs la skyes stobs kyi blo gros ni phun sum tshogs/ sbyor byung gi nan tan mchog tu gyur na legs bshad gsar pa mang du
bsgyur ba cis mi nus snyam du dgongs te 'phags pa'i gzims g.yog pa mdo smad pa blo gros rgyal po dang 'grogs nas bal yul du byon te/ paNDi ta sa dbang bzang po'i drung du
sgra snyan ngag sdeb sbyor zlos gar mngon brjod la byang bar mdzad nas sa skyar byon/ 'phags pa rin po che'i drung du phebs/ shin tu dgyes par gyur/ nged kyi chos rje pa
byang phyogs sprul pa'i sder sku'i bkod pa bsdu ba'i tshe/ tha ma'i gsung du bka' stsal pa la/ da ni sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa yang mchog tu dar bar byas/ brgal brtags kyi
sgo nas gtan la 'bebs pa'i srol bzang po dod/ tha snyad rig gnas kyi tshul 'di la yang lag rjes chen po byung bas sems la 'phreng ba cher med/ 'on kyang 'phags pa bsnyen
par ma rdzogs pa dang / rtogs brjod dpag bsam 'khri shing ma 'gyur ba dang / dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud phreng 'dzin gyi tshigs bcad bzhin ma 'gyur ba gsum tsam mo/ /zhes
gsungs pa zhig yod na'ang bsnyen par rdzogs zin/ 'gyur gnyis sngar ma byung bas da khyed kyis gyis shig /de'i grogs dpon chen shAkya bzang pos kyang byed pa yod do/ /zhes
dgyes bzhin bka' stsal bas/ sa skyar dus 'khor rgyud

'grel shong 'gyur zhes yongs su grags pa'i mkhas pa thams cad 'gyur legs pa rang du mdzad pa 'di mdzad/ slar rdo rje gdan du byon nas mahA bo dhi la mchod pa dang skor ba mdzad/
paNDi ta lakShim ka ra spyan drangs nas/ dpag bsam 'khri shing / klu kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar/ snyan ngag me long / 'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstod pa brgya pa/ 'jam
dpal gyi bstod pa br-i ta ma la/ tsandra pa'i mdo sbyor ba'i rtsa 'grel/ bzlog pa bsdus pa rtsa 'grel/ slob dpon su pa rakShi tas mdzad pa'i smra ba kun la 'jug pa rtsa
'grel/ slob dpon se ge bzang pos mdzad pa'i rnam dbye'i le'ur byas pa la sogs pa sngon ma 'gyur ba bsgyur/ 'chi med mdzod la 'gyur mchan mdzad nas/ sgra snyan ngag gi bshad
rgyun spel/ 'phags pa rin po ches kyang sde snod 'dzin pa shong lo tsA ba'i snyan du gsol ba zhes pa'i 'phrin las yig mdzad pa na/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel
pa dang bcas pa rgya che la zab cing gting dpag par dka' ba/ tshig brling zhing sdeb sbyor byings che bas chen po rnams kyis kyang nyams su len dka' bas sngon byung gi lo
tsA ba dag gis kyang ma 'gyur ba dang / log par bsgyur ba dang / rnam grangs gzhan dang phyogs re ba dang / thar bar bsgyur ba la sogs pa de dag khyed kyis legs par khong
du chud cing nges te/ zhu chen mdzad pa'i glegs bam dang / klu rnams kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar mthong bas/ dge ba dang rjes su yi rang ba khyad par can skyes zhes rab
tu bsngags/ sgra bsgyur rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bur gyur to/ de nyin kyi dpon po shong lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pas gsan te/

de ni 'phags pa rin po che'i sras kyi thu bor gyur cing / se chen rgyal pos kyang bla mar bkur bas gzhi 'gyur dang 'gyur 'chos mang po mdzad/ gcen gyi yon tan bum pa gang byo'i
tshul du mkhyen cing / khyad par du dus 'khor dang tha snyad rig pa'i gnas la mkhas pa'i slob ma mang du thon/ de la lo tsA ba mchog ldan dang / sgra tshad pa rin chen
rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis gsan la/ lo mchog pa ni mang mkhar khra tshang du sku 'khrungs/ 'phags pa rin po che las rab tu byung / mtshan mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros dpung
rgyan mdzes pa'i tog ces rang nyid kyis 'dogs par zhus pa bzhin btags la/ phyis lo mchog pa zhes grags/ shong sku mched las dbang rgyud man ngag gsan/ ka tsan la sogs
pa rig gnas mtha' dag bslabs/ bod na 'gyur ro 'tshal gyi dbang gdams ngag bka' bstan bcos phal mo che'i lung mnga' bas/ bod kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po'i bla mar gyur/
de'i slob ma ni/ dpang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa ste/ la stod lho spyang lung gi 'o 'bu gyam du me pho byi ba la 'khrungs/ gdung dpang / yum snga mo nas grongs te lug
gi 'o mas gsos pas lu gu zhes grags/ kho bo ba'i 'o mas gsos na legs pa la blun po rnams kyis lug gi 'o ma byin pas blo gros kyi phyed 'gribs su bcug gsung / grub chen
o rgyan pas bu chung de la dge bshes chen po zhig 'ong bas 'di byin gsung nas/ ja gsol 'phro zhig gsol zhal dang bcas pa bskur/ lo lnga pa la rgod tshang pa'i gdan sa/ byang
gling pa las dge bsnyen nod/ mtshan blo gros brtan par btags/

bdun pa la mkhan chen gser khang pa dang / mes ston 'dul 'dzin pa las rab tu byung / bcu pa la mdo rtsa TIkka dang bcas pa khyi bdun gyis bdas kyang thon pa byung / sngon tshe
sbyangs pas skye ba 'dir/ /gzhung rnams rtsed mo'i zhor la shes/ /zhes gsungs/ grogs shig gis chu la khur bas khyed stobs ches sangs rgyas bstan pa rangs po khur bas
theg 'gro ba 'dug gsungs pas/ des 'thab skad do/ /bcu gsum pa la tsha nar rtag bde ba'i drung du byon/ lo drug bar ma chad dubasten nas/ phar tshad mngon gsum/ dbu ma/ khyad
par du dus 'khor la sbyangs pas/ bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mkhas par mkhyen/ phyi nang gzhan gsum don ston pa'i/ /rgyud 'grel tshig do narang bshad nas/ /rdo rje theg
par blo phyogs mdzad/ /gsang ba'i don ston bla mar 'dudu/ /bsams bzhin yang bla ma 'di bka' drin che/ /rtag bde ba 'di bka' drin che/ /bka' drin can gyi bla ma la/ /gus
pas phyag 'tshal skyabs su mchi/ /zhes sogs gsol 'debs kyang mdzad/bcu dgu pa la rtag bde ba sku gshegs nas/ mang mkhar khra tshang du lo mchog pa la dus 'khor shong lugs/
ka tsan me long / rong pa shes rab seng ge la dus 'khor rwa lugs/ sa skyar 'jam skya ba la brtag gnyis/ rnam 'grel/ rig gter gsan//nyi shu pa la gser khang pas mkhan po/
me tog pas las slob/ byang ston pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ a tsa ra byung tshad la

phral skad bslabs/ 'jam dbyangs bzhi thog pa dang / paNDi ta'i bar gyi lo tsA mdzad pas lo tsA bar grags/nyer gcig pa la bal por byon/ ra ma A tsarYa dang / ma tha na A tsarYa
la tsandra pa gsan/ sa skyar byon te/ ka lA pa'i 'grel pa gnyis rags rim bsgyur/ shong ston legs bshad lde mig blangs/ /legs sbyar skad kyi gter kha phye/ /sna tshogs
gzhung lugs rin chen blangs/ /legs bshad dga' ston 'gyed la dbang / /zhes gsungs/ dge shing pa la bstod pa rgyas 'bring mdzad nas bskur bas/ dad de dngul bre chen phul ba
bsnams nas/ yang bal por byon/ paNDi ta snga ma gnyis dang / rgya gar shar phyogs kyi tsu Ta paNDi ta rnams bsten nas ka lA pa sogs rig gnas phyi ma gsan/ dgongs rgyan
sogs bsgyur/ slar sa skyar phebs dus 'jam skya bas gtso mdzad kyis ser sbreng dang / bkur sti chen po mdzad/ bal por lan bdun byon/ bal po'i paNDi ta phal che bas man snye
dang dgongs rgyan sogs zhus/ sa skyar bzhi thog pa dang 'jam skya la lam 'bras sogs mang du gsan/so gnyis pa la gung thang gnas po cher chos gzhis btsugs te gung thang
pa bde blo sogs slob ma'i mchog rgya mtsho lta bu 'dus pa la/ dbyar dus 'khor/ dgun phar tshad mngon gsum gyi dus chos gsungs/ snyan pa'i grags pas rgya gar dang hor yul
tshun khyab/ ya tshe dang hor rgyal pos gdan 'dren byung ba la bar chad du gzigs nas/ springs yig gong 'og can gyis ya tshe bzlog cad pu dgon gsar la seng ge gling du btags
te der bzhugs pas hor bzlog sdig pa'i grogs po'i g.yo ba ring du spangs/ /bdud kyi zhags pa'i 'ching ba

che las grol/ /'jigs pa med pa seng ge'i khyim du slebs/ /dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa'i bsam pa 'grub/ /ces gsungs/ skabs der sa skyar byon nas/ lo mchog pa la mnga' ba'i bka'
lung mtha' dag bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan/ shas cher gnas po cher bzhugs nas/ rtsom bshad bsgyur gyi sgo phye/ slar sa skyar byon/ chos mang du gsungs/ de'i skabs
su bo dong e'i dge 'dun rnams kyis rgyal sras thogs med la gdan sar gsol ba btab pas/ bdag gis mi yong / nged kyis lung bstan pa ltar byas na de'i brgyud pa bdun gyi bar
du lugs gnyis kyi sa sde 'di la phan par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so/ de la dge 'dun rnams kyis kyang bka' bzhin bgyid pa zhu ba'i ngo chen phul ba na/ sems dpa' chen po des
kyang dpang lo rtsa ba'i drung du phebs te/ dpal e'i dge 'dun rnams ni nyid la mkhan por gsol ba 'debs kyis/ bdag la yang ngo chen gyi lus su bgyid pas na/ de ni mgon po
khyed kyis mdzad par rigs so zhes thal mo thugs kar sbyar bas bdag nyid chen po de ni thugs shin tu rings par gyur cing / 'jig rten gyi spyod pa la rgyab kyis phyogs pas/
gu ru thogs med thos pa'i gtam la snyan/ /nyin kyi zhal nas legs bshad ma gtogs pa/ /nyes par snang ba ga la srid pa ste/ /kho bo'i mkhan po chen po rtag bde pa/ /seng
ge rgyal mtshan gyis kyang ma thob pa'i/ /gdan sa yin pas de ring rang la 'gro/ /'gyur na mi yong da lta rang la 'gro/ /zhes gsungs shing / khri thog tu phebs nas bstan
pa'i bya ba yun ring mdzad/ de nas dbus su byon pa'i lam du glegs bam mang po slob ma la bkye ba'i mnal lam byang bas zla ba bcu drug gi bar du dbus su bzhugs nas/ lha

sa/ bsam yas/ gung thang / stag lung / rwa sgreng / gsang ne'u thog rnams su dus 'khor/ dgongs rgyan/ phar tshad mngon gsum/ dbu ma rgyan/ sgra snyan ngag zab mo'i mdo lnga
sogs chos mang du gsungs pas/ dbus kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen phal mo ches gsan/ da ni shi yang mi 'gyod do zhes gsungs/ de nas snar thang du mchims blo bzang pa sogs la dgongs
rgyan snyan ngag sogs gnang / de na e dang sa skyar byon/ si sogs kyi mtha' dpyad 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa tsandra pa'i yi ge'i mdo/ ting mtha'i bya ba/ slob dpon
gtsang kha shas mdzad pa'i 'grel pa mdor bstan/ sogs gzhi 'gyur dang zhu chen mang du mdzad cing / dus 'khor 'grel chen gyi bstod 'grel ka lA pa snyan ngag me long gi
'grel pa/ tshogs gsum gsal ba sogs bstan bcos mang du mdzad nas/ de bdun pa chu pho rta'i nag pa'i tshes bcu gsum la bde ba can du gshegs so/ /lo chen 'di la ni slob ma 'jam
dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan mched gnyis/ bu dol lo tsA ba ma ti rnam gnyis/ gung thang bde blo/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo sogs mang du byung zhing / bu ston rin po
ches ni gtso bor thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan la sgra gsan no/ /mkhas pa 'di la rig gnas kyi dogs gnas mang du zhus nas/ 'grel pa dur sing yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba sogs
dur sing gi 'grel pa spyan gsum 'bangs kyis mdzad pa phal cher bsgyur 'gyur mang po dang / ka lA pa'i 'grel pa yang mdzad/ slob ma'i gtso bo sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam
rgyal sogs la gsungs pas/ rig gnas kyi bshad rgyun shin tu dar ba byung /

sa bzang ma ti paN chen gyis ni ka lA pa'i 'grel pa shin tu rgyas par mdzad cing / rang gi slob ma sa bzang 'phags pa dang / lo tsA ba dpal ldan smra ba'i seng ge sogs la gsungs
shing / 'phags pa'i rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po la yang sgra snyan ngag legs par gsungs so/ /gung thang pa bde blos mnga' ris su rig gnas legs par spel zhing /
snyan ngag gi 'grel pa dang gtam rgyud ganggA'i tshu rgyun sogs mdzad/ slob ma'i mchog lo chen byang chub rtse mo ni zur tsho zhes par yab gzhon nu dpal bzang / yum dpang
lo'i lcam mo ye shes sman ne gnyis kyi sras su shing mo yos la 'khrungs/bdun pa la dpang lor dge bsnyen nod/ shong gi dbon po chos skyong dpal las rab tu byung /bcu drug
pa la gung thang gnas po cher dpang lo la mngon tshad gsan cing sbyangs/ dpang lo e'i gdan sar bzhugs dus lo bzhir rig gnas phal mo che la sbyangs/nyer gsum pa la 'jam
dbyangs don rgyal bas mkhan po/ dpang los las slob/ chos rje bla mas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/nyer lnga pa la lo tsA ba mkhas par mkhyen/ dpang lo zhi bar ma
gshegs kyi bar phyi bzhin 'brengs nas dus 'khor sogs nyid la mnga' ba'i yon tan ma lus thugs su tshud/de nas bu ston/ chos rje bla ma/ rgyal sras pa rnams la/ rgyud sde
rgya mtsho'i dbang rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ nyams su bzhes pas/ grub

pa'i dbang phyug tu mnga' gsol/ rgyal sras pas/ lo chen 'di la zhal zas kyis bsnyen bkur na mu ge'i skal pa las thar gsung ba'i snyan grags kyis rnyed bkur mchod pa'i mtsho
brdol/ chu la mi 'bying / bug pa chung ngu la skus brtol/ khang chung du mi mang po la dbang bskur bas rdzu 'phrul bstan/ mngon par mkhyen pa mnga'/ dpal ldan bla ma'i bkas
e'i gdan sa mdzad/ de'i phyag phyir dbus su byon/stag lung ratna kA ras lo chen 'di'i nged kyi dbon po'i slob dpon du 'jog par zhus pas gnang ste/ stag lung pa nam mkha'
dpal bzang la dus 'khor sgra snyan sogs gnang bas de'i bshad rgyun dbus su cher dar/ slar dgas por chos rje bla ma'i drung du byon/ ka lA pa'i sa ris phul/ gtsang phyogs
su bzhugs nas dgung lo mthon por gyur kyang / spyan snga grags 'byung bas gdan drangs nas/ yar klungs/ gdan sa thel/ gung thang rnams su dus 'khor sgra snyan gyi chos
char phab/ mkhas pa kun tshim par byas/ e'i chab tshan la byon dus thugs mkhyen mang du gsungs/ stag tshang / shangs/ 'u yug nyang stod rnams su dus 'khor gyi dbang rgyud
khrid nang du gsungs/ gsang chab 'thungs pas lkugs pa mang po smra shes/ zhal mthong ba/ gsung thos pa/ gsol ras zos pa tsam gyis nad thon pa dang / byin rlabs zhugs pa
mang du byung / gdul bya mang po smin grol la bkod nas ka lA pa'i 'grel pa slob phan sogs 'gyur du ma mdzad/ don brgyad pa lcags pho spre'u'i lo mchu zla'i nyer gcig la
ngo mtshar ba'i rtags dang bcas te gshegs so/ /

de'i slob ma'i mchog lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang po/ /lo chen grags pa rgyal mtshan shes rab dpal sogs mang du byon pa las/ lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang po ni sgra tshad dus 'khor
rnams la mkhas par gyur nas/ lo chen gyi phyag phyi dang / gnas gzhan du yang / dus 'khor/ ka tsan/ snyan ngag sdeb sbyor sogs la bshad pa mang du mdzad/ lo chen byang
rtse'i phyag phyi mdzad na ka lA pa'i 'grel pa slob phan yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba la sogs pa'i phyag rjes kyang shin tu che/ /lo chen byang chub rtse mo dang / lo chen
nam mkha' bzang po gnyis char gyi slob ma ni/ bo dong pa shes rab dpal ste/ 'di nyid kyis ra ma tsandra'i 'grel pa rdzogs par bsgyur cing rig gnas bshad pa'i slob ma po
dong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis ka lA pa'i uN sogs kyi 'grel par durga senghas mdzad pa dang / byings kyi mdo si sog kyi mtha' dpyad bram ze'i slob dpon sarba dha ras
mdzad pa sogs 'gyur mang po mdzad do/ /lo chen grags pa rgyal mtshan ni lo chen byang chub rtse mo'i rus dbon yin zhing / nyid la ji ltar mnga' ba'i chos thams cad thugs
su chud cing / e dang gyam gyi gdan sar bzhugs te mdo rgyud rig gnas kyi bshad pa rgya cher stsal bas/ slob ma mkhas par gyur pa grangs las 'das pa zhig thon/ sras kyi mchog
ni bo dong paN chen phyogs rgyal rnam rgyal te 'dis mkhyen pa la ni mtha' med cing / rtsod pa'i sgo nas kyang g.yag mi chos kyi bla ma/ rong ston shes bya kun rig /rigs
pa smra ba bsod nams skyabs/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal la sogs pa'i spobs pa bcoms/ rtsom pa'i sgo nas de nyid 'dus chen

zhes bya ba ste/ bzhugs tshul yang 'jug pa'i sgo bzhi/ phyi nang gi gnas lnga/ bshad sgrub rin po che'i yan lag dang nye ba'i yan lag brgya phrag rim par phye ba brgya drug
cu/ le'u nyi khri chig stong drug brgya/ man ngag bdud khri nyis stong / chos choms brgyad khri bzhi stong / po ti brgya dang bcu yod pa yin no/ /'chad pa'i slob ma thon
tshul yang / bzo rig nas bzung yongs su rdzogs pa'i bar/ /de dang de yi bka' babs nyi shu gsum/ /'jam pa'i rdo rje mi yi zlos gar mkhan/ /rnam dag 'khon gyi gdung brgyud
rnam pa gsum/ rig sngags 'chang ba'i khyu mchog chen po gcig /nyi ma zla ba ltar grags mkhas grub gnyis/ /'jig rten gsum gyi mig gcig lo chen gsum/ /phyogs las rnam par
rgyal ba'i bshes gnyen drug /ces sogs mang du gsungs pa'i nang nas/nyi zla ltar grags pa gnyis ni/ dang po mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang po ste/ 'dis ni nags shod pa chos
dbang grags pa sogs dge phyogs kyi rig gnas smra ba thams cad kyi rig gnas chu rgyun spel ba'i rgya mtsho mdzad pa yin la/ zla ba lta bu ni/ gsung rab rgya mtsho chu gter
gyi mngal las thon te/ yongs su rdzogs pa'i bstan pa'i nam mkhar 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gi dkyil 'khor yongs su gang bas/ mkhas par btags pa'i ri bong gis sgeg cing /
tha snyad kyi gtsug lag rgya mtsho'i 'od dkar gyi snang bas blo gsal ku mu ta'i tshogs rgyas par mdzad pa la mkhas pa dpang lo tsA ba ba chen po'i sku'i skye ba snye thang
blo gros brtan pa bzhi par bod pa de yin

te/ 'dis kyang dbus su rig gnas kyi bstan pa cher dar bar mdzad do/ /lo tsA ba thams cad gsum ni e'i lo tsA ba chen po bsod nams bzang po/ lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ lo
tsA ba thugs rje dpal lo/ /yang tsho tsA ba nam mkha' bzang po dang / lo tsA ba shes rab dpal gnyis kyi thugs kyi sras dam pa ni/ shab smad lo tsA ba thugs rje dpal te/
'di ni rig gnas la shin tu mkhas pa tsandra pa'i 'grel pa dharma dA sa rdzogs par bsgyur/ ka tsan gnyis la 'grel pa shin tu rgyas shing mtha' yod pa bzhugs tshogs chen po
re mdzad cing / tha snyad rig gnas kyi bshad rgyun rgyas par spel ba las/ slob ma'i mchog gtsang du chos 'khor sgang pa shes rab rin chen/ zha lu pa gzhung brgya smra ba
bkra shis rgya mtsho/ gnas brtan legs pa rgyal po/ snar thang lo tsA ba sangga shrI/ bo dong shes rab bzang po/ chos 'khor lo tsA ba manydzu shrI/ nyid kyi zhabs pad yun
ring du bsten pa grags pa'i mtshan can/ dbus su rong ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ rje byams pa gling pa la sogs pa'i mkhas pa dpag tu med pa bskrun zhing / tha snyad ri pa'i
tshul 'di shin tu rgyas par mdzad do/ /de yang snar thang lo tsA ba sangga shrI ni ka tsan la sogs pa'i sgra mdo nyi shu tsam gyi sa ris la thogs pa mi mnga'/ ka lA pa
la TIkka yongs su rdzogs pa legs pa phul du phyin pa yang mdzad/ snyan ngag me long gi TIkka bklags pas don thams cad 'grub pa don rgyan gyi dper brjod mi 'dra ba gnyis/
sgra rgyan gyi dper brjod shin tu legs pa/ sngags kyi klog thabs sogs yig cha'i rigs phul du phyin pa mang du mdzad cing bshad pa'i srol

bzung bas tha snyad rig gnas mkhas pa'i slob ma mang du byung zhing / slob ma'i mchog ni 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal te/ 'dis ni dbus su rig gnas kyi srol rgya cher btod cing
/ slob ma'i mchog khrus khang lo tsA ba bsod nams rgya mtsho ste dpon slob 'di gnyis nas dus 'khor dang rig gnas kyi bshad rgyun 'phel ba ni kar 'brug?'drug gnyis sogs
mtha' yas pa zhig yod pas bka' drin shin tu che ba yin no/ /slob ma'i mchog chos 'khor sgang pa lo chen shes rab rin chen ni/ yab don grub rgyal po dang / yum lha mo skyabs
zhes bya ba'i sras su shing mo bya'i hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes gsum la 'khrungs/ mtshan dkon mchog skyabs su btags/dgung lo bdun la yi ge thams cad mthar phyin/ slob dpon
gzhan du byon pas yig?mig phrug pa rgan gzhon bco lnga skor gyi slob dpon mdzad/ dgung lo nyi shu'i bar du yab yum gyi dgongs pa bskang phyir rab tu byung rgyu ma byung
yang / de'i lo thabs mkhas pos seng ge rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du rab tu byung / ka ri ka lnga bcu pa sogs mdo phyogs la sbyangs pa mdzad de bshad pa yang brtsams/
thams cad ngo mtshar bar gyur/ gzhan yang chos 'khor ba yab sras kyi drung du mdo phyogs kyi chos thams cad legs par sbyangs shing / sngags kyi dkyil chog du ma dang
/ tshig rtsa la sbyangs pas mkhas pa chen po rnams la yang dgag sgrub du ma mkhyen pa byung /de nas dngus 'bras spungs sa 'jam dbyangs bkra shis dpal ldan la mdo phyogs
mang du gsan cing gra skor gzhung shin tu mang ba mdzad cing / gra

skor gyi tshe yang chos 'brel zhu mkhan mang du byung /yar res rje byang sems pa'i drung du lam 'bras dus 'khor sogs gsang sngags kyi chos tshul mang du gsan/ dbyar shab dpal
sding du sems dpa' chen po skad gnyis smra ba thugs rje dpal bzang po'i drung du phebs/ chos 'khor ba dang thugs 'brel che zhing / khyad par mtshan lam du dge slong chos
gos ngur smrig dang ldan pa khyad par can zhig dang mjal ba rmis gsungs nas shin tu dgyes par mdzad/ snga dro ka lA pa dang phyi dro tsandra pa'i bstan bcos tshugs/ rig
gnas 'di la snga ma'i bag chags ma gtogs sku tshe 'dir thugs rtog ma chug cing / yig cha dkon pa dang / rnam rgyal 'joms/ dus 'khor sogs sngags dus ma'i skad dod sbyor
ba dang / yig rigs du ma mkhyen yang gar yang ma phyin pa lta bur song / yig cha thams cad thun bar la bris/ shog las mtshan mo byas/ tsha dro'i bar la gzhung bzung / srod
tho rangs skyong ran mdzad pas shin tu bsnyel ba byung yang rags rim thugs su chud/ slar lo chen chos 'khor du spyan drangs/ tha snyad rig gnas lnga char yongs su rdzogs
par gsan cing mkhyen/ slob sbyong gsan rgya dpe mang po'i gnang sbyin dang bcas te rig gnas kyi bstan pa gtad/ de nas bo dong paN chen dang mjal/ gsung chos mang du gsan
cing bsngags pa rgya cher mdzad/ de nas chos 'khor gyi gdan sar phebs/ 'khor lo gsum gyi mdzad pas yun ring du bstan pa bskyang zhing / nang du ting nge 'dzin zab mo la
brtson par mdzad/ mdo sngags kyi bstan bcos mang du mdzad cing rig gnas la yang / ka lA pa'i spyi don 'grel pa/ rig gnas

kun shes kyi rtsa 'grel la sogs pa mang du mdzad cing / sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas sogs 'gyur yang mang du mdzad/ bshad rgyun 'dzin pa'i slob ma yang / 'ug tshang rin
po che/ slob dpon 'dul 'dzin sngon mo/ rta nag rab 'byams pa shes rab chos 'byor/ slob dpon dka' bcu pa skyes mchog /mgon bzang pa rin chen rgyal mtshan bzang po/ kun dga'
rgyal mtshan/ bsam 'grub 'od zer ba sku mched/ rta nag pa nor bzang rgya mtsho/ byams chen pa sangs rgyas 'phel/ se ra ba blo gros seng ge/ zha lu ba blo gros seng ge/
dgas po blo gros mtha' yas/ sgra dus la sbyangs pa kun dga' 'od zer sogs mang du byung zhing / khyad par slob ma'i mchog ni zha lu lo chen yin no/ /gsum pa/ mthar bka' drin
che ba zha lu lo chen ji ltar byon pa'i tshul ni/ mkhas pa'i 'byung gnas zha lu gser khang zhes bya ba'i grong khyer du yab lung rtogs kyi yon tan dang ldan pa 'gos kyi
rigs sku zhang pa bsam 'grub dpal bzang po dang / yum bud med kyi yon tan thams cad dang ldan pa rin chen chos 'dzom zhes bya ba'i sras su lcags pho byi ba'i lo la sku
bltams/ mtshan chos skyong 'bum zhes bya bar gsol/ /gzhon nu'i tshe yang sngon gyi bag chags kyi dbang gis/ dad brtson shes rab snying rje la sogs pa phun sum tshogs shing
/ sku rtsed kyi tshe yang chos 'chad pa dang / sgra bsgyur ba dang / yi ge 'dri ba la sogs pas dus 'da' zhing skabs 'gar ting nge 'dzin bzang po la snyoms par 'jug la yang
byung /

dge ba'i bshes gnyen bkra shis rin chen pa la bod kyi klog yig bslabs pas sngar gyi bag chaT chung ba la brten cung zad dka' ba tsam byung /de nas dgung lo nyer gnyis kyi bar
du khyim pa'i tshul bzung yang / thos pa mang du mdzad/nyer gnyis pa la mkhan po 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po/ slob dpon kun dga' dpal bzang gi drung du dge tshul
gyi sdom pa bzhes/ nyer drug pa'i tshe/ mkhan po don grub grags pa dpal bzang / las kyi slob dpon bsod nams grags pa/ gsang ston bsod nams blo gros la sogs pa dad pa'i dge
'dun gyi dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyes ltung gi dri ma thams cad dang bral ba'i gnas brtan chen por bzhugs pa yin no/ /de ltar gzhi tshul khrims rnam par dag pa la gnas
nas thos bsam gyis sgro 'dogs bcad tshul yang / sku zhang dge slong mkhan chen chos grub/ brag dmar rab 'byams pa bla ma don rin pa/ dka' bzhi thugs rje dpal ba/ bshes
gnyen bzang po ba/ dge 'dun drug pa/ snye mo sku zhang pa/ ting 'dzin 'od zer ba/ bsod nams grags pa/ gong ma kun dga' legs/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' dbang phyug /go rams
bsod nams seng ge/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rin dpa' ba/ chos grags rgya mtsho/ sku zhang mkhyen rab mchog grung / rab 'byams bde bzang pa/ kun bzang rtse
pa/ zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa bzhi dka' thub pa stag lung nas bla ma rnam pa gsum/ kun mkhyen don yod dpal ba/

slob dpon ngag dbang grags pa/ dkon mchog tshul khrims/ snar thang ras chen la sogs pa'i yongs su 'dzin pa bcu phrag lnga bsten nas bod du 'gyur ba'i bka' dang bstan bcos thams
cad dang / mdo phyogs kyi bshad lung mtha' yas pa/ sngags phyogs kyi dbang / byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / rgyud bshad/ snying po phyung ba'i don khrid la sogs pa mtha' dag
thugs su chud cing / bsam pa'i sgro 'dogs rgya cher bcad pa yin la/ lhag par rig gnas kyi bshad rgyun nyams pa thams cad gso ba'i phyir du sgra rig pa chen po gnas brtan
legs pa rgyal po/ dpal sdings sgra pa/ lo chen grags pa rgya mtsho/ rgya ston lcags ri ba thar pa bzang po/ stag tshang lo tsA ba chen po shes rab rin chen/ chag lo bzhi
pa rte'u ra pa rin chen chos kyi rgyal po/ dwags?dgas po paN chen sogs mkhas pa mang du bsten nas tha na yig rigs mi 'dra ba sna tshogs pa nas bzung ste/ sgra dang / snyan
ngag dang / sdeb sbyor dang / mngon brjod dang / zlos gar te tha snyad sde lnga po 'di dag la 'phags yul nas 'gyur zin pa'i gzhung chen po 'grel pa dang bcas pa mtha'
dag dang / ma 'gyur ba mang po rgya dpe'i steng du gtan la phab/ mdor na thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs legs par bcad de/ ji snyed pa'i gnas thams cad ma 'dres par so sor 'chad
pa'i nus pa thob/ rig pa'i gnas kyi bstan pa rin po che'i bdag po gcig pu par gyur pa yin no/ /lhag par stag tshang lo chen gyi drung du ka lA pa'i spyi TIkra/ nyer mkho'i
mdo so so 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ rig gnas phyi ma bzhi'i zab bshad/ nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bstan bcos mtha' dag gi bshad lung yongs su rdzogs par

zhus/ thugs dges pa chen pos rjes su bzung zhing rig gnas kyi bstan pa gtad/ bshad rgyun dpag tu med par 'phel bar lung bstan pa yin la/ sems pa dpa' chen po thugs rje dpal
gyi thugs sras mchog tu gyur pa/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgya mtshos tsandra pa'i mdo/ 'grel pa dharma dA sa/ nyer mkho'i mdo so so 'grel pa dang bcas zhib tu nan chags chen
pos stsal zhing gsan pa yin no/ /de ltar rig gnas la mkhyen pa dpag par dka' bas/ dus 'khor 'grel chen/ dpag bsam 'khri shing la sogs pa'i bstan bcos brgya phrag tsam gyi
rgya dpe dang bod dpe legs par sbyar te/ gzigs rtog mdzad pa dang gzhan la 'doms par yang mdzad/mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos sna tshogs gsal ba/ 'grel pa 'dod 'jo/ mu tig
phreng ba/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa dbu ma la dga' pas mdzad pa la sogs pa'i gzhi 'gyur shin tu mang ba dang / byams chos lnga/ rgyud gsum/ me long / sdeb sbyor sogs gzhung
shin tu mang po la 'gyur 'chos hor khongs gsab pa sogs kyi sgo nas ma 'gyur ba dang / log par bsgyur ba dang / 'gyur chad pa sogs mtha' dag gi dri ma bkrus nas/ bstan pa
rin po che gsal ba las kyang ches shin tu gsal bar mdzad pa yin no/ /'gyur mdzad pa'i tshe ches shin tu myur ba yin te/ rje btsun nyid kyi rgya dpe rnams bod skad du bsgyur/
yi ge gcig kyang chad lhag med par gsung ba slob ma rnams kyis bod dpe bzung nas mnan pa na/ bod klog bzang ba kun gyis kyang non dka' bar gyur ba ni mngon sum du gsol
lo/

de ltar 'gyur mdzad pa'i tshul thams cad mkhyen pa zha lu lo chen gyi zhal snga nas kyi gsung dngos las 'di skad ces gsungs te/ bdag la yon tan skye ba dran pa sogs ma mchis/
rmi lam du sngar paNDi ta su rendra bo dhir gyur ces pa tsam rmi ba dran/ bla ma rnams kyi byin rlabs kyis tshul khrims rin po che dang ma bral tsam dang / byang sems
smon 'jug blo sbyong rim pas dran pa dang dad gus ma bral tsam mchis/ lam rim gnyis yi dam lha dran pa dang / lam zab la dmigs rnam ma brjed ma dor tsam dang / lam gyi cha
shas kyi nges shes 'dren pa lags/ skad gnyis smra ba'i lo tsAr gtogs tsam 'di snga ma'i bag chags dang / tshe 'dir mkhas pa bsten pas/ ka lA pa dang tsandra pa'i gzhung
rdzogs pa'i sa ris slob sbyong dang / rgya dpe klog shes pas 'phags pa brgyad stong pa nyi khri dang 'bum gyi glegs bam dam dum/ sher phyin bdun brgya dang / yi ge nyung
ngu / sher snying / rdo rje gcod pa'i 'grel pa/ mngon rtogs rgyan 'grel chung dang bcas pa/ byams chos phyi ma bzhi/ rgyud bla 'grel chen/ dkon brtsegs/ byang chub sems
dpa'i sde snod/ blo gros bzang pos zhus pa/ byams pas zhus pa sogs dang / 'dul ba mdo rtsa/ so thar mdo/ sum brgya pa/ me tog phreng rgyud/ las chog tshad ma rnam nges/ rnam
'grel/ gtan tshigs thigs pa/ rgyud gzhan grub pa/ 'grel brtag dbu ma rtsa ba/ 'jug pa/ bzhi brgya pa/ 'grel pa tshig gsal/ stong nyid bdun cu pa/ rig pa drug cu pa/ zhib
mo rnam 'thag chos dbyings bstod pa/ byang chub sems 'grel/ don dam par bstod pa sogs bstod pa bzhi/ bshes springs rnams dang / gzhan yang slob springs/ spyod 'jug

gzhon nu ma bdun gyi rtogs brjod/ rgyud sde las mtshan brjod 'grel pa phan yon dang bcas pa/ dus 'khor gyi dbang mdor bstan/ bsdus rgyud rtsa 'grel/ don dam snye ma/ rta 'dod
mdor bstan/ dus 'khor sgrub thabs mai dri pas mdzad pa/ brtag gnyis/ gur/ sambu Ti/ gur gyi 'grel pa lha'i rigs kyi blo gros/ kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa padma can gyi dka'
'grel/ gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud/ 'grel pa sgron gsal/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud phyag rdor bstod 'grel/ rdo rje snying 'grel/ bde mchog sdom 'byung gi rgyud/ ArYa de wa'i spyod
bsdus sgron me/ rim lnga/ mdor byas/ mdo bsre/ sems kyi sgrib sbyong rnams dang / bslab btus/ ched du brjod pa'i tshoms/ mdo sde las brgya pa/ a bha ya'i phreng ba skor gsum/
dar paN AtsarYa'i kri ya sa munydza/ mngon pa mdzod rtsa ba/ rang 'grel/ de 'grel blo brtan/ sgra ka lA pa/ 'grel pa dur sing / u Na sogs kyi 'grel pa/ byings mdo/ tsandra
pa/ 'grel pa chos 'bangs/ de'i 'grel bshad ratna ma ti/ mngon brjod 'chi med mdzod/ 'grel pa 'dod 'jo/ mngon brjod sna tshogs gsal ba/ sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas/
sman yan lag brgyad pa ste 'di rnams kyi rgya dpe dang bod dpe sbyar ba'i brda thog tshig don la dpyod pa zhugs pas/ sngon gyi lo tsA ba rnams kyis chos bsgyur tshul/
rjes su dpag pa'i sgo nas rtogs par gyur pa lags/de dag gi skabs su sdig pa dag pa'i rtags khrus byas pa dang / chu'i gseb nas 'o ma 'thung ba da nga/ glegs bam rgya dpe
bod dpe gser gyi ngos la padma rA gas bris pa dang / dar dang gos chen gyi ngos la lha dang yi ge spel te bris pa ma mang ba sogs rmi lam du byung / i/ zhes phyag bris
ngo

ma las byung bas/ yid ches shing dad pas kun nas blangs te yongs su rdzogs par bris pa'o/rtogs pa'i yon tan yang gzhon nu'i dus su lha khang bskor du byon pa na/ mgon po beng
gi skus rigs kyi bu khyod mngon par sangs ma rgyas kyi bar du kho bos bsrung ba dang / skyob pa dang / sba bar bya'o zhes gsung byon pas/ grung khyer gyi nad ngan pa bsrung
ba'i thugs dam mdzad pa na/ gdugs mchog tu mdzes pa nyis rim phub pa'i sgrol ma'i sku dngos su bstan nas/ grong khyer bsrung ba'i tshul mdzad par gzigs pa dang / mnal
lam du dpal ldan birwa pa la kye rdo rje'i dbang bskur gsan pa dang / khams pa brtson 'grus zhes bya ba'i mi ngan zhig gis rje'i phyag rdzas mang du brkus pa zin kyang
slar gnang ba dang / bstan pa dang sems can la phan na dmyal ba'i g.yang sa la yang 'jigs par mi bya zhes gsungs shing / zhal gyis bzhes pa sogs yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab?khyang
/de nas dbus su byon/ stag lung chos rje/ zhwa nag pa/ zhwa dmar ba sogs bla chen gsum la sgra dang snyan ngag gi gsung gi bdud rtsi yang yang stsal/ zhwa nag cod
pan 'dzin pa chos grags rgya mtshos spyan ras gzigs kyi sku shin tu legs pa sogs gnang sbyin dpag tu med pa stsal te/ bod kyi skye bo blo gsal sgra dang snyan ngag dang
sdeb sbyor mngon brjod la sogs pa'i tha snyad rig gnas kun legs par slob pa'i bstan pa'i sgron mer bkas yang yang bskul zhing bsngags pa rgya cher stsal/ nga gsum pa la
rgya ston lcags ri ba'i gdan sar phebs/

nga lnga pa la grwa pa mngon shes can gyi gdan sar phebs/don bzhi pa la bu ston rin po che'i gnad sar phebs te/ spyir mdo sngags gnyis dang / lhag par rig gnas la bshad rgyun
yang yang spel/ gsung rtsom kyang ka tsan gyi spyi don/ 'grel pa rnam pa gnyis/ byings mdo'i bsdus don/ ka lA pa'i sa bcad/ nyer bsgyur gyi 'grel pa rgyas 'bring bsdus
gsum/ snyan ngag me long gi 'grel pa/ sdeb sbyor gyi gnad bsdus pa/ dag yig za ma tog aShTa'i byings sgrub pa sogs sngags kyi byings sgrub mang po/ mtshams sbyor gyi 'grel
pa gnyis sogs bstan bcos kyang mang du mdzad pas gangs ri'i khrod kyi blo gsal gzur gnas thams cad kyi bkur sti'i gnas dam pa dang / lashag par rig gnas kyi bstan pa'i
bdag por 'gyur pa yin no/ /de ltar gsung las skyes pa'i thos pa 'dzin pa yang gangs ri'i khrod kyi mkhas pa dang grub pa thams cad kyi chod pan dam pa 'jam dbyangs pa lo
tsA ba gnyis pa kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ /rje btsun sprul pa'i lo tsA ba ratna bha dra/ mthu stobs chos rje ngag dbang bsod nams mtshan can/
nyid kyi dbon po lo tsA ba chen po padma dkar po/ skyob lo tsA ba ngag dbang rin chen bkra shis/ ka tsan gyi don khong du chud cing / gangs can gyi brda'i tshul la ma
rmongs pa'i g.ya' bzang pa mkhas btsun dbang po la sogs te/ mkhas pa chen po sa skya lo tsA sogs/ /lo tsA legs par shes pa rnam dgu dang / /gangs can khrod na tha snyad gtsug
lag la/ /legs par bya ba'i mkhas pa du ma yod/ ces gsungs pa ltar lo tsA ba chen po dgu dang / tha snyad rig gnas la mkhas pa dpag tu med pas gangs can

gyi ljongs thams cad khyab ste bstan pa rin po che gsal bar mdzad cing / der ma zad rje btsun lo tsA ba chen po dpon slob 'di nyid kyi bka' drin las/ deng?ding sang gi bar
du bshad rgyun cher rgyas shing / slad nas kyang mi nyams pa bstan pa ji srid gnas kyi bar du dar zhing rgyas pa ni thugs rje dang smon lam gyi mthu las so/ /gzhan yang sngags
kyi bshad rgyud 'dzin pa'i slob ma ni/ mkhas grub o rgyan rdzong pa/ rtses thang 'bum rams pa/ mkhan chos grub song ge/ rje btsun rdo rings pa chen po sogs mang du
yod pa rnams kyis kyang dbang bshad khrid rgyun sogs rgyas par spel ba yin no/gya bdun pa la rang gi dbon lo tsA ba padma dkar po gdan sar bskor/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa
brgyad la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te bde bar gshegs/ dbon lo tsA bas phyi rten nang rten gshegs rdzongs dpag tu med pas dgongs pa rdzogs par mdzad cing / gdan
sa yun ring du bskyangs/ nyid kyi gsung rgyun sngags dang rig gnas kyi bstan pa rgyas par spel/ nyid kyi zhal slob rnams kyi mchog rje btsun sa lo tsA ba ni/ lo chen nyid
kyis kyang tshe 'dir lan re zung re tshos tsam gyis gzhung lugs kun shes/ chos kya irje sa paNDi ta dang nges par gnyis su med pa'o/ /zhes gus pa'i thal mo yang yang zum
par mdzad cing / nyid kyi gsung las kyang / 'gos lo dharma pa la'i zhal snga nas/ /dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang bskur sa lugs dang / /jo zhal lugs kyi sbyor drug la sogs zhus/
ka lnga tsandra rin chen 'byung gnas dang /

sna tshogs gsal ba snyan ngag me long dang / /dpal bsam 'khri shing la sogs tha snyad kyi/ /gtsug lag phal cher zhus shing nan tan byas/ /rang bzhin rkyen dang rnam 'gyur la
sogs pa/ /dus dang don la 'jug tshul cung zad shes/ /saM skr-ita dang bod kyi klog tshul la/ /snga rabs 'chad tshul rab tu mang na yang / /skyon med 'dri dang brjod pa'i
tshul shes pa/ /mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan 'di nyid bka' drin las/ /gzhan la 'chad dam rang nyid nyams su len/ /ji ltar byed kyang lag nom mi dgos tsam/ /zhes gsungs shing
spyir mdo sngags mtha' dag gi bstan pa gsal bar mdzad cing / lhag par ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub sogs mkhas pa mang po la rig gnas kyi bshad rgyun rgyas par stsal zhing
/ ding sang gi bar ngu yang ngor phyogs na shin tu dar ba byung ngo / /) rje btsun sprul pa'i lo chen ratna bha dras kyang / spyir mdo sngags kyi bshad pa dang / sgos
rig gnas la ched rtsol du mdzad pas/ byang phyogs 'dir rig gnas kyi bshad rgyun ches cher dar zhing / lhag par slob ma'i mchog grub chen thang stong rgyal po'i gdung 'dzin
cing / rgya gar gyi paNDi ta mi tri pa'i sku skye ba rje btsun sprul pa'i lo tsA ba chen po 'gyur med bde chen ni spyir mdo sngags rig gnas la mkhyen pa che zhing / lhag
par rig gnas la phul du phyin ba'i bshad rgyun spel zhing / byang chos rgyal gyi ti shri mdzad de ding sang gi bar du 'gro don rgya chen por bzhugs bzhin pa 'di ga'o/ /de
la slob ma mtha' yas kyang dge bshes stag tsang lo tsA ba ratna seng ge la bshad pa'i rgyun cher babs so/ /

yang lhang mthong lo chen gyis kar lugs kyi rig gnas kyi rgyun thams cad bzung zhing / khyad par bal po dza gad rA dza'i gsung rgyun sgra rig gi legs bshad mang po rje btsun
'gyur med bde chen la stsal ba'i brgyud pa yang yod do/ /yang lo chen pad dkar brang chen rab 'byams dpal ldan 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ sgang ra lo tsA ba 'od zer rgyal mtshan
nas brgyud pa mang / sgang ra bas ni dpal khang lo tsA ba la yang kar lugs bshad rgyu rdzogs pa nyan no/ yang grub chen gyi dbon ngag dbang kun dga' blo gsal gyis 'brug
lugs kyi rig gnas smra ba mang po la gtugs ba'i bshad rgyun yang stag tshang lo tsA ba la yod do/ /yang sgra snyan ngag dpag bsam 'khri shing gi bshad rgyun zab bsdus tsam
bsdus tsam ni snye thang blo brtan bzhi paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ dbon shAkya rgyal mtshan/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po sogs nas brgyud pa yang yod do/ /thams cad mkhyen
pa klu sgrub rgya mtsho ni slob dpon gang la yang ma brten kyang / sngon gyi bag chags sad pa dang / lhag pa'i lhas byin gyis brlabs pas rig gnas thams cad thugs su
chud cing / spel bar mdzad pa ni brgyud pa'i mchog yin no/ /ces tha snyad rig gnas lnga ji ltar byung ba'i tshul gsal bar byed pa blo gsal mgrin rgyan legs bshad nor bu'i
phreng ba zhes bya ba 'di ni rje btsun rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho'i zhabs pad kyi yan lag mchog tu reg pa'i bka'

drin thob cing / thams cad mkhyen pa mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i bka' drin las rig ba'i gnas la blo gros cung zad gsal ba la/ rdo rje 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gyi sku
drin las snyan rgyud zab mo'i chos la dad pa thob pa yang dag 'jog la gcig tu 'dun pa'i blo can ngag rig pa dgra 'dul dbang po la/ yul dbus kyi sman ljongs su skyes pa'i
dge slong lo tsA ba rnam dpyod can dngos grub rgya mtsho zhes bya bas ka lA pa'i sgra rig yongs su rdzogs pa dang / snyan ngag me long / sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas/
mngon brjod la sogs pa'i tha snyad gzhung lugs rnams legs par nyan te mkhas par byas pa'i rjes su lhag bsam dad pas nye bar bskul ba la brten nas/ nyin byed dbang po smin
legs dga' ma'i khyim du rtse dgas rol pa'i khrums zla dmar po'i phyogs kyi dga' ba gsum pa'i tshes la rang gi bsti gnas lugs gnyis kyi 'dun sa 'dar stod yang rdzogs dkar
po'i ba gam rig gnas mngon par bkra ba'i lding khang du bris pa'o/ /lan gcig zhus dpyad/ mangga laM// //
